MOBODY: Model Based Off-Dynamics Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yihong Guo, Yu Yang, Pan Xu, Anqi Liu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-10T05:36:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T17:33:14+00:00
Comments: Published at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study off-dynamics offline reinforcement learning, where the goal is to learn a policy from offline source and limited target datasets with mismatched dynamics. Existing methods either penalize the reward or discard source transitions occurring in parts of the transition space with high dynamics shift. As a result, they optimize the policy using data from low-shift regions, limiting exploration of high-reward states in the target domain that do not fall within these regions. Consequently, such methods often fail when the dynamics shift is significant or the optimal trajectories lie outside the low-shift regions. To overcome this limitation, we propose MOBODY, a Model-Based Off-Dynamics Offline RL algorithm that optimizes a policy using learned target dynamics transitions to explore the target domain, rather than only being trained with the low dynamics-shift transitions. For the dynamics learning, built on the observation that achieving the same next state requires taking different actions in different domains, MOBODY employs separate action encoders for each domain to encode different actions to the shared latent space while sharing a unified representation of states and a common transition function. We further introduce a target Q-weighted behavior cloning loss in policy optimization to avoid out-of-distribution actions, which push the policy toward actions with high target-domain Q-values, rather than high source domain Q-values or uniformly imitating all actions in the offline dataset. We evaluate MOBODY on a wide range of MuJoCo and Adroit benchmarks, demonstrating that it outperforms state-of-the-art off-dynamics RL baselines as well as policy learning methods based on different dynamics learning baselines, with especially pronounced improvements in challenging scenarios where existing methods struggle.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MOBODY：基于模型的异动态离线强化学习
本文研究异动态离线强化学习，目标是从动态不匹配的离线源数据集和有限目标数据集中学习策略。现有方法或通过惩罚奖励，或丢弃动态差异较大的状态转移空间中的源数据转移，导致策略优化仅依赖低动态差异区域的数据，限制了在目标域中对高奖励状态的探索。当动态差异显著或最优轨迹位于低差异区域外时，此类方法常失效。为此，我们提出MOBODY——一种基于模型的异动态离线强化学习算法，其通过已学习的目标动态转移来优化策略以探索目标域，而非仅使用低动态差异转移进行训练。基于“在不同域中达到相同下一状态需采取不同行动”的观察，MOBODY为每个域设置独立行动编码器，将不同行动编码至共享潜空间，同时共享统一的状态表征和转移函数。我们进一步在策略优化中引入目标Q加权行为克隆损失，以避免分布外行动，使策略偏向具有高目标域Q值的行动，而非高源域Q值或均匀模仿离线数据集中的所有行动。在MuJoCo和Adroit基准测试中，MOBODY显著优于现有异动态强化学习基线及基于不同动态学习基线的策略学习方法，在现有方法难以应对的挑战性场景中改进尤为显著。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of off-dynamics offline reinforcement learning, where a policy must be learned from offline datasets with mismatched dynamics between source and target domains. The proposed method, MOBODY, is a model-based algorithm that overcomes limitations of prior approaches—which restrict learning to low dynamics-shift regions—by using learned target dynamics transitions to explore the target domain. It employs separate action encoders per domain to map actions to a shared latent space while sharing state representations and a transition function, and introduces a target Q-weighted behavior cloning loss to avoid out-of-distribution actions by favoring actions with high target-domain Q-values. Experimental results on MuJoCo and Adroit benchmarks show that MOBODY outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, particularly in challenging scenarios with significant dynamics shifts.
本文研究了离动态离线强化学习问题，其目标是从动态不匹配的离线源数据集和有限目标数据集中学习策略。所提出的MOBODY是一种基于模型的算法，它通过使用学习到的目标动态转移来探索目标域，克服了现有方法仅局限于低动态偏移区域学习的限制。该方法为每个域使用独立的动作编码器将动作映射到共享潜在空间，同时共享状态表示和转移函数，并引入了目标Q加权的行为克隆损失，通过偏好具有高目标域Q值的动作来避免分布外动作。在MuJoCo和Adroit基准测试上的实验结果表明，MOBODY优于最先进的基线方法，在动态偏移显著、现有方法难以处理的挑战性场景中改进尤为明显。
Unified Policy Value Decomposition for Rapid Adaptation
Authors: Cristiano Capone, Luca Falorsi, Andrea Ciardiello, Luca Manneschi
First: 2026-03-18T17:19:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T17:19:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rapid adaptation in complex control systems remains a central challenge in reinforcement learning. We introduce a framework in which policy and value functions share a low-dimensional coefficient vector - a goal embedding - that captures task identity and enables immediate adaptation to novel tasks without retraining representations. During pretraining, we jointly learn structured value bases and compatible policy bases through a bilinear actor-critic decomposition. The critic factorizes as Q = sum_k G_k(g) y_k(s,a), where G_k(g) is a goal-conditioned coefficient vector and y_k(s,a) are learned value basis functions. This multiplicative gating - where a context signal scales a set of state-dependent bases - is reminiscent of gain modulation observed in Layer 5 pyramidal neurons, where top-down inputs modulate the gain of sensory-driven responses without altering their tuning. Building on Successor Features, we extend the decomposition to the actor, which composes a set of primitive policies weighted by the same coefficients G_k(g). At test time the bases are frozen and G_k(g) is estimated zero-shot via a single forward pass, enabling immediate adaptation to novel tasks without any gradient update. We train a Soft Actor-Critic agent on the MuJoCo Ant environment under a multi-directional locomotion objective, requiring the agent to walk in eight directions specified as continuous goal vectors. The bilinear structure allows each policy head to specialize to a subset of directions, while the shared coefficient layer generalizes across them, accommodating novel directions by interpolating in goal embedding space. Our results suggest that shared low-dimensional goal embeddings offer a general mechanism for rapid, structured adaptation in high-dimensional control, and highlight a potentially biologically plausible principle for efficient transfer in complex reinforcement learning systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：统一策略价值分解框架实现快速适应
复杂控制系统的快速适应仍是强化学习的核心挑战。本文提出一种框架，使策略函数与价值函数共享低维系数向量——即捕捉任务特征的目标嵌入，无需重新训练表征即可实现对新任务的即时适应。预训练阶段，通过双线性行动者-评论者分解联合学习结构化价值基函数与兼容的策略基函数。评论者分解为Q = Σ_k G_k(g) y_k(s,a)，其中G_k(g)是目标条件系数向量，y_k(s,a)是习得的价值基函数。这种乘法门控机制——通过情境信号缩放状态相关基函数——类似于第5层锥体神经元中观察到的增益调节现象，即自上而下的输入在不改变调谐特性的情况下调节感觉驱动响应的增益。基于后继特征理论，我们将该分解扩展至行动者模块，通过相同系数G_k(g)加权组合原始策略集合。测试阶段基函数固定，G_k(g)通过单次前向传播进行零样本估计，无需梯度更新即可实现对新任务的即时适应。我们在MuJoCo Ant环境中以多向运动目标训练软行动者-评论者智能体，要求其沿连续目标向量指定的八个方向行走。双线性结构使各策略头专注于特定方向子集，共享系数层实现跨方向泛化，通过在目标嵌入空间插值适应新方向。研究表明，共享低维目标嵌入为高维控制中的快速结构化适应提供了通用机制，并揭示了复杂强化学习系统中高效迁移的潜在生物合理性原理。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of rapid adaptation in reinforcement learning by proposing a unified framework where policy and value functions share a low-dimensional goal embedding vector to capture task identity, enabling immediate adaptation to novel tasks without retraining representations. The method involves jointly learning structured value bases and compatible policy bases through a bilinear actor-critic decomposition, where the critic factorizes as a sum of goal-conditioned coefficients and learned value basis functions, and the actor composes primitive policies weighted by the same coefficients, inspired by gain modulation in neural systems. In experiments on the MuJoCo Ant environment with multi-directional locomotion objectives, the approach allows policy heads to specialize in subsets of directions while generalizing across them via shared coefficients, facilitating zero-shot adaptation to novel directions through interpolation in goal embedding space, demonstrating effective rapid adaptation without gradient updates.
本文针对强化学习中快速适应的挑战，提出了一种统一框架，其中策略和价值函数共享一个低维目标嵌入向量来捕获任务身份，从而无需重新训练表示即可立即适应新任务。该方法通过双线性行动者-评论者分解联合学习结构化价值基和兼容策略基，评论者分解为目标条件系数与学习价值基函数的和，行动者则由相同系数加权的原始策略组成，灵感来源于神经系统的增益调制机制。在MuJoCo Ant环境的多方向运动目标实验中，该方法使策略头能够专注于方向子集，同时通过共享系数实现泛化，通过在目标嵌入空间中的插值实现对新方向的零样本适应，展示了无需梯度更新的有效快速适应能力。
Operator-Theoretic Foundations and Policy Gradient Methods for General MDPs with Unbounded Costs
Authors: Abhishek Gupta, Aditya Mahajan
First: 2026-03-18T16:01:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T16:01:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Markov decision processes (MDPs) is viewed as an optimization of an objective function over certain linear operators over general function spaces. Using the well-established perturbation theory of linear operators, this viewpoint allows one to identify derivatives of the objective function as a function of the linear operators. This leads to generalization of many well-known results in reinforcement learning to cases with generate state and action spaces. Prior results of this type were only established in the finite-state finite-action MDP settings and in settings with certain linear function approximations. The framework also leads to new low-complexity PPO-type reinforcement learning algorithms for general state and action space MDPs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一般成本无界马尔可夫决策过程的算子理论基础与策略梯度方法
马尔可夫决策过程可视为在一般函数空间上对特定线性算子的目标函数优化。借助成熟的线性算子摄动理论，该视角能够将目标函数的导数表达为线性算子的函数，从而将强化学习中许多经典结论推广至广义状态与动作空间。此类结果先前仅适用于有限状态-动作的MDP场景或特定线性函数逼近场景。该框架还催生了适用于广义状态-动作空间MDP的新型低复杂度PPO类强化学习算法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to extend reinforcement learning theory and algorithms beyond finite or linearly approximated settings, this paper reframes Markov decision processes (MDPs) as an optimization over linear operators in general function spaces. The method leverages operator perturbation theory to derive gradients of the objective function with respect to these operators, generalizing established policy gradient results to MDPs with general state and action spaces and unbounded costs. Experimentally, this theoretical framework enables the development of new, low-complexity PPO-type algorithms applicable to these broader MDP classes, overcoming prior limitations confined to finite settings or specific approximations.
本文的动机是将强化学习的理论与算法推广到有限状态或线性近似之外的一般场景，其方法是将马尔可夫决策过程重新定义为一般函数空间上线性算子的优化问题。通过运用算子扰动理论，该方法推导出目标函数相对于这些算子的梯度，从而将策略梯度等经典结果推广至具有一般状态与动作空间以及无界成本的MDP中。实验结果表明，这一理论框架催生了适用于此类广义MDP的新型低复杂度PPO算法，突破了以往仅局限于有限设定或特定近似方法的限制。
Procedural Generation of Algorithm Discovery Tasks in Machine Learning
Authors: Alexander D. Goldie, Zilin Wang, Adrian Hayler, Deepak Nathani, Edan Toledo, Ken Thampiratwong, Aleksandra Kalisz, Michael Beukman, Alistair Letcher, Shashank Reddy, Clarisse Wibault, Theo Wolf, Charles O'Neill, Uljad Berdica, Nicholas Roberts, Saeed Rahmani, Hannah Erlebach, Roberta Raileanu, Shimon Whiteson, Jakob N. Foerster
First: 2026-03-18T15:49:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:49:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Automating the development of machine learning algorithms has the potential to unlock new breakthroughs. However, our ability to improve and evaluate algorithm discovery systems has thus far been limited by existing task suites. They suffer from many issues, such as: poor evaluation methodologies; data contamination; and containing saturated or very similar problems. Here, we introduce DiscoGen, a procedural generator of algorithm discovery tasks for machine learning, such as developing optimisers for reinforcement learning or loss functions for image classification. Motivated by the success of procedural generation in reinforcement learning, DiscoGen spans millions of tasks of varying difficulty and complexity from a range of machine learning fields. These tasks are specified by a small number of configuration parameters and can be used to optimise algorithm discovery agents (ADAs). We present DiscoBench, a benchmark consisting of a fixed, small subset of DiscoGen tasks for principled evaluation of ADAs. Finally, we propose a number of ambitious, impactful research directions enabled by DiscoGen, in addition to experiments demonstrating its use for prompt optimisation of an ADA. DiscoGen is released open-source at https://github.com/AlexGoldie/discogen.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器学习中算法发现任务的程序化生成
自动化开发机器学习算法有望开启新的突破。然而，现有任务套件的诸多问题——如评估方法不完善、数据污染、任务饱和或高度相似——限制了算法发现系统的改进与评估能力。本文提出DiscoGen，一种用于机器学习的算法发现任务程序化生成器，可生成如强化学习优化器或图像分类损失函数等任务。受强化学习中程序化生成成功的启发，DiscoGen能够从多个机器学习领域生成数百万个不同难度和复杂度的任务。这些任务由少量配置参数定义，可用于优化算法发现智能体（ADAs）。我们同时推出DiscoBench基准测试，包含DiscoGen任务的固定小型子集，用于对ADAs进行系统性评估。最后，除展示其在ADA提示优化中的应用实验外，我们还提出了由DiscoGen启发的多项前瞻性研究方向。DiscoGen已在https://github.com/AlexGoldie/discogen开源发布。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing task suites for evaluating algorithm discovery systems, which suffer from issues like poor evaluation methodologies and data contamination, this paper introduces DiscoGen, a procedural generator for creating diverse machine learning algorithm discovery tasks. The method involves specifying tasks through a small set of configuration parameters, enabling the generation of millions of tasks across fields such as reinforcement learning and image classification, with varying difficulty and complexity. Experimental results include the release of DiscoBench, a fixed benchmark subset for principled evaluation, and demonstrations of DiscoGen's utility in prompt optimisation for algorithm discovery agents, showcasing its potential to drive new research directions in automated algorithm development.
本文的动机源于现有算法发现系统评估任务套件的局限性，如评估方法不佳和数据污染等问题，为此引入了DiscoGen，一个用于生成多样化机器学习算法发现任务的程序化生成器。该方法通过少量配置参数指定任务，能够生成涵盖强化学习和图像分类等领域的数百万个不同难度和复杂度的任务。实验成果包括发布了DiscoBench这一固定基准子集以进行原则性评估，并展示了DiscoGen在算法发现智能体提示优化中的应用，证明了其在推动自动化算法开发新研究方向方面的潜力。
CBF-RL: Safety Filtering Reinforcement Learning in Training with Control Barrier Functions
Authors: Lizhi Yang, Blake Werner, Massimiliano de Sa, Aaron D. Ames
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2025-10-16T17:58:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:28:16+00:00
Comments: To appear at ICRA 2026; sample code for the navigation example with CBF-RL reward core construction can be found at https://github.com/lzyang2000/cbf-rl-navigation-demo
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL), while powerful and expressive, can often prioritize performance at the expense of safety. Yet safety violations can lead to catastrophic outcomes in real-world deployments. Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) offer a principled method to enforce dynamic safety -- traditionally deployed online via safety filters. While the result is safe behavior, the fact that the RL policy does not have knowledge of the CBF can lead to conservative behaviors. This paper proposes CBF-RL, a framework for generating safe behaviors with RL by enforcing CBFs in training. CBF-RL has two key attributes: (1) minimally modifying a nominal RL policy to encode safety constraints via a CBF term, (2) and safety filtering of the policy rollouts in training. Theoretically, we prove that continuous-time safety filters can be deployed via closed-form expressions on discrete-time roll-outs. Practically, we demonstrate that CBF-RL internalizes the safety constraints in the learned policy -- both enforcing safer actions and biasing towards safer rewards -- enabling safe deployment without the need for an online safety filter. We validate our framework through ablation studies on navigation tasks and on the Unitree G1 humanoid robot, where CBF-RL enables safer exploration, faster convergence, and robust performance under uncertainty, enabling the humanoid robot to avoid obstacles and climb stairs safely in real-world settings without a runtime safety filter.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CBF-RL：基于控制屏障函数的安全过滤强化学习训练框架
强化学习（RL）虽功能强大且表达性强，但常以牺牲安全性为代价追求性能，而安全违规在实际部署中可能导致灾难性后果。控制屏障函数（CBFs）提供了一种强制执行动态安全性的理论方法——传统上通过在线安全过滤器实现。尽管结果能保证行为安全，但RL策略未纳入CBF知识可能导致保守行为。本文提出CBF-RL框架，通过在训练中强制执行CBFs实现安全的RL行为生成。该框架具备两个关键特性：（1）通过CBF项对基础RL策略进行最小化修改以编码安全约束；（2）在训练中对策略展开进行安全过滤。理论上，我们证明了连续时间安全过滤器可通过离散时间展开的闭式表达式实现。实践上，CBF-RL将安全约束内化至学习策略中——既强制执行安全动作，又偏向安全奖励——从而无需在线安全过滤器即可实现安全部署。我们通过导航任务的消融实验及Unitree G1人形机器人验证了该框架：CBF-RL在不确定性环境下实现更安全的探索、更快收敛及鲁棒性能，使人形机器人无需运行时安全过滤器即可在真实场景中避障并安全爬梯。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the safety-performance trade-off in reinforcement learning (RL) by proposing CBF-RL, a framework that integrates Control Barrier Functions (CBFs) directly into the training process to enforce dynamic safety constraints. The method minimally modifies a nominal RL policy by incorporating a CBF term and applies safety filtering to policy rollouts during training, theoretically enabling the deployment of continuous-time safety filters on discrete-time rollouts via closed-form expressions. Experimental results from navigation tasks and real-world deployment on a Unitree G1 humanoid robot demonstrate that CBF-RL leads to safer exploration, faster convergence, and robust performance under uncertainty, allowing the robot to avoid obstacles and climb stairs safely without requiring an online safety filter at runtime.
本文针对强化学习中安全与性能的权衡问题，提出了CBF-RL框架，通过将控制屏障函数直接集成到训练过程中来强制执行动态安全约束。该方法通过融入CBF项对名义强化学习策略进行最小修改，并在训练期间对策略展开进行安全过滤，理论上支持通过闭式表达式在离散时间展开上部署连续时间安全过滤器。在导航任务和Unitree G1人形机器人上的实验结果表明，CBF-RL能够实现更安全的探索、更快的收敛以及在不确定性下的鲁棒性能，使机器人能够在无需运行时安全过滤器的情况下安全避障和爬楼梯。
CodeScout: An Effective Recipe for Reinforcement Learning of Code Search Agents
Authors: Lintang Sutawika, Aditya Bharat Soni, Bharath Sriraam R R, Apurva Gandhi, Taha Yassine, Sanidhya Vijayvargiya, Yuchen Li, Xuhui Zhou, Yilin Zhang, Leander Melroy Maben, Graham Neubig
First: 2026-03-18T15:25:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:25:42+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A prerequisite for coding agents to perform tasks on large repositories is code localization - the identification of relevant files, classes, and functions to work on. While repository-level code localization has been performed using embedding-based retrieval approaches such as vector search, recent work has focused on developing agents to localize relevant code either as a standalone precursor to or interleaved with performing actual work. Most prior methods on agentic code search equip the agent with complex, specialized tools, such as repository graphs derived from static analysis. In this paper, we demonstrate that, with an effective reinforcement learning recipe, a coding agent equipped with nothing more than a standard Unix terminal can be trained to achieve strong results. Our experiments on three benchmarks (SWE-Bench Verified, Pro, and Lite) reveal that our models consistently achieve superior or competitive performance over 2-18x larger base and post-trained LLMs and sometimes approach performance provided by closed models like Claude Sonnet, even when using specialized scaffolds. Our work particularly focuses on techniques for re-purposing existing coding agent environments for code search, reward design, and RL optimization. We release the resulting model family, CodeScout, along with all our code and data for the community to build upon.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CodeScout：强化学习代码搜索智能体的高效方案
编码智能体在大型代码库执行任务的前提是代码定位——即识别需要处理的相关文件、类与函数。虽然基于嵌入检索（如向量搜索）的方法已实现仓库级代码定位，但近期研究聚焦于开发能独立或交替执行实际工作的代码定位智能体。现有智能体代码搜索方法多赋予智能体复杂专用工具（如静态分析生成的仓库图）。本文证明：通过有效的强化学习方案，仅配备标准Unix终端的编码智能体即可训练出优异性能。在三个基准测试（SWE-Bench Verified/Pro/Lite）中，我们的模型持续超越或比肩参数量大2-18倍的基础/后训练大语言模型，有时甚至接近Claude Sonnet等闭源模型在专用框架下的表现。本研究重点关注现有编码智能体环境的重构适配、奖励机制设计与强化学习优化技术。我们开源了CodeScout模型家族及全部代码数据，供社区持续开发。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enable coding agents to effectively localize relevant code within large repositories, a critical precursor to performing tasks, moving beyond traditional embedding-based retrieval or complex specialized tools. The method introduces CodeScout, a reinforcement learning recipe that trains a coding agent using only a standard Unix terminal as its tool, focusing on techniques for adapting existing coding environments for search, reward design, and RL optimization. Experimental results on benchmarks including SWE-Bench Verified, Pro, and Lite show that CodeScout models achieve superior or competitive performance compared to 2-18x larger base and post-trained LLMs, sometimes approaching the performance of closed models like Claude Sonnet, even when those use specialized scaffolds.
本研究的动机是使编码智能体能够在大型代码库中有效定位相关代码，这是执行任务的关键前提，旨在超越传统的基于嵌入的检索或复杂专用工具。方法上提出了CodeScout，一种强化学习方案，仅使用标准Unix终端作为工具来训练编码智能体，重点包括调整现有编码环境用于搜索、奖励设计和RL优化的技术。在SWE-Bench Verified、Pro和Lite等基准测试中的实验结果表明，CodeScout模型相比基础和后训练大2-18倍的大型语言模型，实现了更优或具有竞争力的性能，有时甚至接近如Claude Sonnet等闭源模型在使用专用框架时的表现。
Federated Distributional Reinforcement Learning with Distributional Critic Regularization
Authors: David Millard, Cecilia Alm, Rashid Ali, Pengcheng Shi, Ali Baheri
First: 2026-03-18T15:12:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:12:21+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 Figures, conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Federated reinforcement learning typically aggregates value functions or policies by parameter averaging, which emphasizes expected return and can obscure statistical multimodality and tail behavior that matter in safety-critical settings. We formalize federated distributional reinforcement learning (FedDistRL), where clients parametrize quantile value function critics and federate these networks only. We also propose TR-FedDistRL, which builds a per client, risk-aware Wasserstein barycenter over a temporal buffer. This local barycenter provides a reference region to constrain the parameter averaged critic, ensuring necessary distributional information is not averaged out during the federation process. The distributional trust region is implemented as a shrink-squash step around this reference. Under fixed-policy evaluation, the feasibility map is nonexpansive and the update is contractive in a probe-set Wasserstein metric under evaluation. Experiments on a bandit, multi-agent gridworld, and continuous highway environment show reduced mean-smearing, improved safety proxies (catastrophe/accident rate), and lower critic/policy drift versus mean-oriented and non-federated baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：联邦分布式强化学习与分布式评论家正则化
联邦强化学习通常通过参数平均来聚合价值函数或策略，这种方法强调期望回报，但可能掩盖安全关键场景中重要的统计多模态性和尾部行为。我们形式化了联邦分布式强化学习（FedDistRL），其中客户端参数化分位数价值函数评论家，并仅联邦化这些网络。我们还提出了TR-FedDistRL，该方法为每个客户端在时间缓冲区上构建风险感知的Wasserstein重心。该局部重心提供了一个参考区域，用于约束参数平均后的评论家，确保必要的分布信息在联邦过程中不被平均消除。分布信任区域通过围绕该参考的收缩-压缩步骤实现。在固定策略评估下，可行性映射是非扩张的，且更新在探测集Wasserstein度量下具有压缩性。在老虎机、多智能体网格世界和连续高速公路环境中的实验表明，相较于面向均值的基准方法和非联邦基线，该方法减少了均值模糊效应，提升了安全代理指标（灾难/事故率），并降低了评论家/策略漂移。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard federated reinforcement learning, which aggregates value functions via parameter averaging and can obscure important distributional information like multimodality and tail risks crucial for safety, this paper formalizes Federated Distributional RL (FedDistRL). The method involves clients parameterizing quantile value function critics and federating only these networks, with a proposed TR-FedDistRL variant that builds a per-client, risk-aware Wasserstein barycenter over a temporal buffer to constrain the parameter-averaged critic via a shrink-squash step, preserving distributional details. Experimental results on bandit, gridworld, and continuous highway environments demonstrate reduced mean-smearing, improved safety proxies such as lower catastrophe rates, and reduced critic/policy drift compared to mean-oriented and non-federated baselines.
本文的动机在于标准联邦强化学习通过参数平均聚合价值函数，可能掩盖对安全至关重要的多模态和尾部风险等分布信息，因此形式化了联邦分布强化学习（FedDistRL）。该方法让客户端参数化分位数价值函数评论家并仅联合这些网络，提出了TR-FedDistRL变体，为每个客户端在时间缓冲区上构建风险感知的Wasserstein重心，通过收缩-压缩步骤约束参数平均后的评论家，以保留分布细节。在赌博机、多智能体网格世界和连续高速公路环境上的实验结果表明，与面向均值的和非联邦基线相比，该方法减少了均值模糊现象，提高了安全性代理指标（如降低事故率），并减少了评论家/策略的漂移。
EVA: Aligning Video World Models with Executable Robot Actions via Inverse Dynamics Rewards
Authors: Ruixiang Wang, Qingming Liu, Yueci Deng, Guiliang Liu, Zhen Liu, Kui Jia
First: 2026-03-18T15:02:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T15:02:19+00:00
Comments: Project page: https://eva-project-page.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Video generative models are increasingly used as world models for robotics, where a model generates a future visual rollout conditioned on the current observation and task instruction, and an inverse dynamics model (IDM) converts the generated frames into executable robot actions. However, current video world models lack explicit executability constraints. As a result, visually coherent rollouts may still violate rigid-body and kinematic consistency, producing unstable or infeasible control commands when decoded by an IDM. We refer to this mismatch between visual generation and physically executable control as the executability gap. While this gap can be mitigated at inference time using techniques such as rejection sampling, such approaches are inefficient due to the high cost of video generation. In this paper, we leverage the executability gap as a training signal and introduce Executable Video Alignment (EVA), a reinforcement-learning post-training framework for aligning video world models. EVA trains an inverse dynamics model on real robot trajectories and repurposes it as a reward model that evaluates generated videos through the action sequences they induce, encouraging smooth motions measured by velocity, acceleration, and jerk while penalizing actions that violate embodiment constraints. Importantly, the reward remains informative even when generated videos contain severe visual artifacts, since such artifacts typically translate into unstable or out-of-bound actions. Experiments on the RoboTwin benchmark and a real bimanual robot show that EVA reduces embodiment-specific artifacts in generated rollouts and improves downstream task execution success.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVA：通过逆动力学奖励将视频世界模型与可执行机器人动作对齐
视频生成模型日益用作机器人学的世界模型，此类模型基于当前观测和任务指令生成未来视觉推演，逆动力学模型（IDM）则将生成的帧转换为可执行的机器人动作。然而，现有视频世界模型缺乏明确的可执行性约束，导致视觉连贯的推演仍可能违反刚体与运动学一致性，经IDM解码后产生不稳定或不可行的控制指令。这种视觉生成与物理可执行控制间的失配称为可执行性鸿沟。虽然可通过拒绝采样等技术在推理阶段缓解该问题，但视频生成的高成本使此类方法效率低下。本文利用可执行性鸿沟作为训练信号，提出可执行视频对齐（EVA）——一种基于强化学习的视频世界模型后训练对齐框架。EVA在真实机器人轨迹上训练逆动力学模型，并将其重构为奖励模型，通过生成视频诱导的动作序列评估视频质量：鼓励以速度、加速度和加加速度衡量的平滑运动，惩罚违反具身约束的动作。关键的是，即使生成视频存在严重视觉伪影，该奖励仍保持信息量，因为此类伪影通常转化为不稳定或越界动作。在RoboTwin基准和真实双臂机器人上的实验表明，EVA能减少生成推演中具身相关的伪影，并提升下游任务执行成功率。

The paper addresses the executability gap in video world models for robotics, where visually coherent generated rollouts may lack physical consistency, leading to infeasible robot actions when decoded by an inverse dynamics model. To bridge this gap, the authors propose Executable Video Alignment (EVA), a reinforcement-learning post-training framework that uses an inverse dynamics model trained on real robot trajectories as a reward model to evaluate generated videos based on the induced action sequences, encouraging smooth motions and penalizing violations of embodiment constraints. Experimental results on the RoboTwin benchmark and a real bimanual robot demonstrate that EVA reduces embodiment-specific artifacts in generated rollouts and improves downstream task execution success.
该论文针对机器人学中视频世界模型的可执行性差距问题，即视觉上连贯的生成轨迹可能缺乏物理一致性，导致通过逆动力学模型解码时产生不可行的机器人动作。为弥合这一差距，作者提出了可执行视频对齐（EVA），这是一个强化学习后训练框架，利用在真实机器人轨迹上训练的逆动力学模型作为奖励模型，根据生成视频诱导的动作序列进行评估，鼓励平滑运动并惩罚违反本体约束的行为。在RoboTwin基准测试和真实双臂机器人上的实验结果表明，EVA减少了生成轨迹中特定于本体的伪影，并提高了下游任务执行的成功率。
Beware Untrusted Simulators -- Reward-Free Backdoor Attacks in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ethan Rathbun, Wo Wei Lin, Alina Oprea, Christopher Amato
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-04T22:17:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T14:45:34+00:00
Comments: 10 pages main body, ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Simulated environments are a key piece in the success of Reinforcement Learning (RL), allowing practitioners and researchers to train decision making agents without running expensive experiments on real hardware. Simulators remain a security blind spot, however, enabling adversarial developers to alter the dynamics of their released simulators for malicious purposes. Therefore, in this work we highlight a novel threat, demonstrating how simulator dynamics can be exploited to stealthily implant action-level backdoors into RL agents. The backdoor then allows an adversary to reliably activate targeted actions in an agent upon observing a predefined ``trigger'', leading to potentially dangerous consequences. Traditional backdoor attacks are limited in their strong threat models, assuming the adversary has near full control over an agent's training pipeline, enabling them to both alter and observe agent's rewards. As these assumptions are infeasible to implement within a simulator, we propose a new attack ``Daze'' which is able to reliably and stealthily implant backdoors into RL agents trained for real world tasks without altering or even observing their rewards. We provide formal proof of Daze's effectiveness in guaranteeing attack success across general RL tasks along with extensive empirical evaluations on both discrete and continuous action space domains. We additionally provide the first example of RL backdoor attacks transferring to real, robotic hardware. These developments motivate further research into securing all components of the RL training pipeline to prevent malicious attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：警惕不可信模拟器——强化学习中的无奖励后门攻击
模拟环境是强化学习（RL）成功的关键，使从业者和研究人员无需在真实硬件上进行昂贵实验即可训练决策智能体。然而，模拟器仍是一个安全盲区，恶意开发者可通过修改其发布的模拟器动态实现有害目的。为此，本文揭示了一种新型威胁，展示了如何利用模拟器动态向RL智能体隐蔽植入动作级后门。该后门使攻击者能在观察到预设“触发器”时，可靠地激活智能体中的目标动作，可能导致危险后果。传统后门攻击受限于其强威胁模型，假设攻击者几乎完全控制智能体训练流程，既能修改也能观察智能体奖励。由于这些假设在模拟器中难以实现，我们提出新型攻击方法“Daze”，该方法能在不修改甚至不观察奖励的情况下，可靠且隐蔽地向面向真实世界任务的RL智能体植入后门。我们通过形式化证明验证了Daze在通用RL任务中保证攻击成功的有效性，并在离散与连续动作空间领域进行了广泛实证评估。此外，我们首次展示了RL后门攻击可迁移至真实机器人硬件。这些进展推动了对RL训练全流程安全防护的进一步研究，以防范恶意攻击。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a security vulnerability in reinforcement learning (RL) where untrusted simulators can be maliciously altered to implant stealthy backdoors into trained agents, a threat not previously considered under traditional strong threat models. The authors propose a novel reward-free attack method named 'Daze', which exploits simulator dynamics to implant action-level backdoors without needing to alter or observe the agent's rewards, thereby operating under a more feasible threat model. Experimental results demonstrate the attack's effectiveness across both discrete and continuous action spaces, supported by formal proofs, and include the first demonstration of such a backdoor successfully transferring to real robotic hardware, highlighting the urgent need for securing the entire RL training pipeline.
本文针对强化学习中的安全漏洞，指出不可信的模拟器可能被恶意篡改，从而在训练好的智能体中植入隐蔽的后门，这一威胁在传统强威胁模型中未被充分考虑。作者提出了一种名为'Daze'的新型无奖励攻击方法，该方法通过利用模拟器动态植入动作级后门，无需修改或观察智能体的奖励，从而在更可行的威胁模型下运作。实验结果表明，该攻击在离散和连续动作空间均有效，并有形式化证明支持，同时首次展示了此类后门可成功迁移到真实机器人硬件上，这凸显了保障整个强化学习训练流程安全的迫切性。
CoVerRL: Breaking the Consensus Trap in Label-Free Reasoning via Generator-Verifier Co-Evolution
Authors: Teng Pan, Yuchen Yan, Zixuan Wang, Ruiqing Zhang, Gaiyang Han, Wanqi Zhang, Weiming Lu, Jun Xiao, Yongliang Shen
First: 2026-03-18T14:38:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T14:38:55+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://zju-real.github.io/CoVerRL Code: https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/CoVerRL
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Label-free reinforcement learning enables large language models to improve reasoning capabilities without ground-truth supervision, typically by treating majority-voted answers as pseudo-labels. However, we identify a critical failure mode: as training maximizes self-consistency, output diversity collapses, causing the model to confidently reinforce systematic errors that evade detection. We term this the consensus trap. To escape it, we propose CoVerRL, a framework where a single model alternates between generator and verifier roles, with each capability bootstrapping the other. Majority voting provides noisy but informative supervision for training the verifier, while the improving verifier progressively filters self-consistent errors from pseudo-labels. This co-evolution creates a virtuous cycle that maintains high reward accuracy throughout training. Experiments across Qwen and Llama model families demonstrate that CoVerRL outperforms label-free baselines by 4.7-5.9\% on mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Moreover, self-verification accuracy improves from around 55\% to over 85\%, confirming that both capabilities genuinely co-evolve.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoVerRL：通过生成器-验证器协同进化突破无标签推理中的共识陷阱
无标签强化学习使大语言模型无需真实标注即可提升推理能力，通常将多数投票答案作为伪标签。然而我们发现一个关键失效模式：当训练最大化自洽性时，输出多样性会坍缩，导致模型自信地强化难以察觉的系统性错误——我们称之为共识陷阱。为突破此陷阱，我们提出CoVerRL框架：单一模型在生成器与验证器角色间交替，两种能力相互引导提升。多数投票为验证器训练提供带噪声但信息丰富的监督，而持续改进的验证器逐步从伪标签中过滤自洽性错误。这种协同进化形成良性循环，在训练全程保持高奖励准确率。在Qwen和Llama系列模型上的实验表明，CoVerRL在数学推理基准上比无标签基线提升4.7-5.9%。此外，自我验证准确率从约55%提升至85%以上，证实两种能力真正实现了协同进化。

Machine Learning for Network Attacks Classification and Statistical Evaluation of Machine Learning for Network Attacks Classification and Adversarial Learning Methodologies for Synthetic Data Generation
Authors: Iakovos-Christos Zarkadis, Christos Douligeris
First: 2026-03-18T13:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:35:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Supervised detection of network attacks has always been a critical part of network intrusion detection systems (NIDS). Nowadays, in a pivotal time for artificial intelligence (AI), with even more sophisticated attacks that utilize advanced techniques, such as generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) and reinforcement learning, it has become a vital component if we wish to protect our personal data, which are scattered across the web. In this paper, we address two tasks, in the first unified multi-modal NIDS dataset, which incorporates flow-level data, packet payload information and temporal contextual features, from the reprocessed CIC-IDS-2017, CIC-IoT-2023, UNSW-NB15 and CIC-DDoS-2019, with the same feature space. In the first task we use machine learning (ML) algorithms, with stratified cross validation, in order to prevent network attacks, with stability and reliability. In the second task we use adversarial learning algorithms to generate synthetic data, compare them with the real ones and evaluate their fidelity, utility and privacy using the SDV framework, f-divergences, distinguishability and non-parametric statistical tests. The findings provide stable ML models for intrusion detection and generative models with high fidelity and utility, by combining the Synthetic Data Vault framework, the TRTS and TSTR tests, with non-parametric statistical tests and f-divergence measures.

标题：机器学习用于网络攻击分类及其统计评估与对抗学习合成数据生成方法
网络攻击的监督检测一直是网络入侵检测系统（NIDS）的关键组成部分。当前正值人工智能（AI）发展的关键时期，面对利用生成式人工智能（GenAI）和强化学习等先进技术发起的更复杂攻击，保护散落在网络中的个人数据已成为至关重要的任务。本文基于首个统一多模态NIDS数据集（整合了流级数据、数据包载荷信息和时序上下文特征，源自经预处理的CIC-IDS-2017、CIC-IoT-2023、UNSW-NB15和CIC-DDoS-2019数据集，并具有统一特征空间）开展两项研究：首先采用分层交叉验证的机器学习（ML）算法，以稳定可靠的方式实现网络攻击防御；其次运用对抗学习算法生成合成数据，通过SDV框架、f-散度、可区分性检验及非参数统计方法，将其与真实数据对比并评估其保真度、实用性和隐私性。研究结合合成数据保险库框架、TRTS与TSTR测试、非参数统计检验及f-散度度量，最终构建出稳定的入侵检测机器学习模型，以及兼具高保真度与实用性的生成模型。

Edge-Cloud Collaborative Computing on Distributed Intelligence and Model Optimization: A Survey
Authors: Jing Liu, Yao Du, Kun Yang, Jiaqi Wu, Yan Wang, Xiping Hu, Zehua Wang, Yang Liu, Peng Sun, Azzedine Boukerche, Victor C. M. Leung
First: 2025-05-03T13:55:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:31:23+00:00
Comments: Accepted by IEEE ComST. 45 pages, 13 figures, 10 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Edge-cloud collaborative computing (ECCC) has emerged as a pivotal paradigm for addressing the computational demands of modern intelligent applications, integrating cloud resources with edge devices to enable efficient, low-latency processing. Recent advancements in AI, particularly deep learning and large language models (LLMs), have dramatically enhanced the capabilities of these distributed systems, yet introduce significant challenges in model deployment and resource management. In this survey, we comprehensive examine the intersection of distributed intelligence and model optimization within edge-cloud environments, providing a structured tutorial on fundamental architectures, enabling technologies, and emerging applications. Additionally, we systematically analyze model optimization approaches, including compression, adaptation, and neural architecture search, alongside AI-driven resource management strategies that balance performance, energy efficiency, and latency requirements. We further explore critical aspects of privacy protection and security enhancement within ECCC systems and examines practical deployments through diverse applications, spanning autonomous driving, healthcare, and industrial automation. Performance analysis and benchmarking techniques are also thoroughly explored to establish evaluation standards for these complex systems. Furthermore, the review identifies critical research directions including LLMs deployment, 6G integration, neuromorphic computing, and quantum computing, offering a roadmap for addressing persistent challenges in heterogeneity management, real-time processing, and scalability. By bridging theoretical advancements and practical deployments, this survey offers researchers and practitioners a holistic perspective on leveraging AI to optimize distributed computing environments, fostering innovation in next-generation intelligent systems.

GIFT: Reconciling Post-Training Objectives via Finite-Temperature Gibbs Initialization
Authors: Zhengyang Zhao, Lu Ma, Yizhen Jiang, Xiaochen Ma, Zimo Meng, Chengyu Shen, Lexiang Tang, Haoze Sun, Peng Pei, Wentao Zhang
First: 2026-01-14T07:13:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:05:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The prevailing post-training paradigm for Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) - Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) followed by Reinforcement Learning (RL) - suffers from an intrinsic optimization mismatch: the rigid supervision inherent in SFT induces distributional collapse, thereby exhausting the exploration space necessary for subsequent RL. In this paper, we reformulate SFT to reconcile post-training objectives and propose Gibbs Initialization with Finite Temperature (GIFT). We characterize standard SFT as a degenerate zero-temperature limit that suppresses base priors. Conversely, GIFT incorporates supervision as a finite-temperature energy potential, establishing a distributional bridge that promotes objective consistency throughout the post-training pipeline. Our experiments demonstrate that GIFT significantly outperforms standard SFT and other competitive baselines when utilized for RL initialization, providing a mathematically principled pathway to preserve exploration and align the two post-training stages. Our code is available at https://github.com/zzy1127/GIFT.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIFT：通过有限温度吉布斯初始化实现后训练目标的对齐
当前大型推理模型（LRM）的主流后训练范式——监督微调（SFT）后接强化学习（RL）——存在内在的优化失配问题：SFT固有的刚性监督会导致分布坍缩，从而耗尽后续RL所需的探索空间。本文通过重构SFT来协调后训练目标，提出了有限温度吉布斯初始化（GIFT）方法。我们将标准SFT描述为抑制基础先验的零温度退化极限，而GIFT则将监督作为有限温度能量势引入，构建了一个分布桥梁，以促进整个后训练流程中的目标一致性。实验表明，当用于RL初始化时，GIFT显著优于标准SFT及其他竞争基线，为保持探索性和对齐两个后训练阶段提供了数学原理清晰的路径。代码已开源：https://github.com/zzy1127/GIFT。

The paper addresses the optimization mismatch in the standard post-training pipeline for Large Reasoning Models, where Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) causes distributional collapse and hinders subsequent Reinforcement Learning (RL) exploration. To reconcile these objectives, the authors propose GIFT (Gibbs Initialization with Finite Temperature), which reformulates SFT by incorporating supervision as a finite-temperature energy potential rather than a rigid zero-temperature limit, thereby preserving base priors and creating a distributional bridge. Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization
Authors: Ting Gao, Stavros Orfanoudakis, Nan Lin, Elvin Isufi, Winnie Daamen, Serge Hoogendoorn
First: 2026-03-18T13:00:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T13:00:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Diffusion-based policies have gained significant popularity in Reinforcement Learning (RL) due to their ability to represent complex, non-Gaussian distributions. Stochastic Differential Equation (SDE)-based diffusion policies often rely on indirect entropy control due to the intractability of the exact entropy, while also suffering from computationally prohibitive policy gradients through the iterative denoising chain. To overcome these issues, we propose Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an Ordinary Differential Equation (ODE)-based online RL framework. FMER parameterizes the policy via flow matching and samples actions along a straight probability path, motivated by optimal transport. FMER leverages the model's generative nature to construct an advantage-weighted target velocity field from a candidate set, steering policy updates toward high-value regions. By deriving a tractable entropy objective, FMER enables principled maximum-entropy optimization for enhanced exploration. Experiments on sparse multi-goal FrankaKitchen benchmarks demonstrate that FMER outperforms state-of-the-art methods, while remaining competitive on standard MuJoco benchmarks. Moreover, FMER reduces training time by 7x compared to heavy diffusion baselines (QVPO) and 10-15% relative to efficient variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于熵正则化的流匹配策略
基于扩散的策略因其能表示复杂的非高斯分布，在强化学习中广受欢迎。基于随机微分方程的扩散策略常因精确熵难以计算而依赖间接熵控制，且需通过迭代去噪链计算代价高昂的策略梯度。为克服这些问题，我们提出基于熵正则化的流匹配策略——一种基于常微分方程的在线强化学习框架。该策略通过流匹配参数化策略，并沿最优传输启发的直线概率路径采样动作。其利用模型的生成特性，从候选集构建优势加权目标速度场，引导策略更新至高价值区域。通过推导可处理的熵目标，该策略实现了增强探索的最大熵优化。在稀疏多目标FrankaKitchen基准测试中，该策略优于现有最优方法，在标准MuJoco基准上保持竞争力。相比重型扩散基线，训练时间减少7倍；相比高效变体，减少10-15%。

The paper is motivated by the limitations of diffusion-based policies in reinforcement learning, which often rely on indirect entropy control and suffer from high computational costs due to iterative denoising. To address this, the authors propose Flow Matching Policy with Entropy Regularization (FMER), an ODE-based online RL framework that parameterizes the policy via flow matching, sampling actions along a straight probability path inspired by optimal transport, and constructs an advantage-weighted target velocity field to steer updates toward high-value regions. Experimental results on sparse multi-goal FrankaKitchen benchmarks show that FMER outperforms state-of-the-art methods, remains competitive on standard MuJoco benchmarks, and reduces training time by 7x compared to heavy diffusion baselines and 10-15% relative to efficient variants.
本文的动机是解决强化学习中基于扩散的策略的局限性，这些策略通常依赖间接熵控制，且因迭代去噪而计算成本高昂。为此，作者提出了带熵正则化的流匹配策略（FMER），这是一个基于常微分方程的在线强化学习框架，通过流匹配参数化策略，沿最优传输启发的直线概率路径采样动作，并构建优势加权目标速度场以引导策略更新朝向高价值区域。在稀疏多目标FrankaKitchen基准测试中，FMER优于最先进方法，在标准MuJoco基准上保持竞争力，并将训练时间相比重型扩散基线减少7倍，相比高效变体减少10-15%。
Post-Training Local LLM Agents for Linux Privilege Escalation with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Philipp Normann, Andreas Happe, Jürgen Cito, Daniel Arp
First: 2026-03-18T12:52:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T12:52:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM agents are increasingly relevant to research domains such as vulnerability discovery. Yet, the strongest systems remain closed and cloud-only, making them resource-intensive, difficult to reproduce, and unsuitable for work involving proprietary code or sensitive data. Consequently, there is an urgent need for small, local models that can perform security tasks under strict resource budgets, but methods for developing them remain underexplored. In this paper, we address this gap by proposing a two-stage post-training pipeline. We focus on the problem of Linux privilege escalation, where success is automatically verifiable and the task requires multi-step interactive reasoning. Using an experimental setup that prevents data leakage, we post-train a 4B model in two stages: supervised fine-tuning on traces from procedurally generated privilege-escalation environments, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards. On a held-out benchmark of 12 Linux privilege-escalation scenarios, supervised fine-tuning alone more than doubles the baseline success rate at 20 rounds, and reinforcement learning further lifts our resulting model, PrivEsc-LLM, to 95.8%, nearly matching Claude Opus 4.6 at 97.5%. At the same time, the expected inference cost per successful escalation is reduced by over 100x.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向Linux权限提升的可验证奖励后训练本地LLM智能体

Automated Grammar-based Algebraic Multigrid Design With Evolutionary Algorithms
Authors: Dinesh Parthasarathy, Wayne Mitchell, Arjun Gambhir, Harald Köstler, Ulrich Rüde
First: 2026-03-18T12:02:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T12:02:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although multigrid is asymptotically optimal for solving many important partial differential equations, its efficiency relies heavily on the careful selection of the individual algorithmic components. In contrast to recent approaches that can optimize certain multigrid components using deep learning techniques, we adopt a complementary strategy, employing evolutionary algorithms to construct efficient multigrid cycles from proven algorithmic building blocks. Here, we will present its application to generate efficient algebraic multigrid methods with so-called \emph{flexible cycling}, that is, level-specific smoothing sequences and non-recursive cycling patterns. The search space with such non-standard cycles is intractable to navigate manually, and is generated using genetic programming (GP) guided by context-free grammars. Numerical experiments with the linear algebra library, \emph{hypre}, demonstrate the potential of these non-standard GP cycles to improve multigrid performance both as a solver and a preconditioner.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于语法和进化算法的代数多重网格自动设计方法
尽管多重网格方法在求解许多重要偏微分方程时具有渐近最优性，但其效率高度依赖于对各算法组件的精心选择。与近期采用深度学习技术优化特定多重网格组件的方法不同，本研究采用互补策略，运用进化算法从已验证的算法模块中构建高效的多重网格循环。本文将展示该方法在生成具有所谓“灵活循环”的高效代数多重网格方法中的应用，即支持层级特定的平滑序列和非递归循环模式。此类非标准循环的搜索空间难以通过人工方式遍历，本研究采用基于上下文无关文法的遗传编程方法进行生成。通过线性代数库hypre进行的数值实验表明，这些非标准遗传编程循环在作为求解器和预处理器时，均具备提升多重网格性能的潜力。

This paper addresses the challenge of manually designing efficient algebraic multigrid (AMG) methods, which are asymptotically optimal for solving partial differential equations but require careful component selection. The authors propose an automated design strategy using evolutionary algorithms, specifically genetic programming guided by context-free grammars, to construct non-standard multigrid cycles with flexible, level-specific smoothing sequences and non-recursive patterns. Numerical experiments conducted with the hypre linear algebra library demonstrate that these automatically generated cycles can improve multigrid performance both as a standalone solver and as a preconditioner.
本文针对代数多重网格方法设计效率依赖人工经验的问题，提出了一种自动化设计策略。研究动机在于手动设计非标准循环模式（如灵活平滑序列和非递归结构）的搜索空间巨大且难以处理，因此作者采用进化算法，特别是基于上下文无关文法的遗传编程，来自动构建高效的多重网格循环。实验使用hypre线性代数库进行数值验证，结果表明这些自动生成的循环模式能够提升多重网格作为求解器和预条件子的性能。
Benchmarking Reinforcement Learning via Stochastic Converse Optimality: Generating Systems with Known Optimal Policies
Authors: Sinan Ibrahim, Grégoire Ouerdane, Hadi Salloum, Henni Ouerdane, Stefan Streif, Pavel Osinenko
First: 2026-03-18T11:52:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:52:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The objective comparison of Reinforcement Learning (RL) algorithms is notoriously complex as outcomes and benchmarking of performances of different RL approaches are critically sensitive to environmental design, reward structures, and stochasticity inherent in both algorithmic learning and environmental dynamics. To manage this complexity, we introduce a rigorous benchmarking framework by extending converse optimality to discrete-time, control-affine, nonlinear systems with noise. Our framework provides necessary and sufficient conditions, under which a prescribed value function and policy are optimal for constructed systems, enabling the systematic generation of benchmark families via homotopy variations and randomized parameters. We validate it by automatically constructing diverse environments, demonstrating our framework's capacity for a controlled and comprehensive evaluation across algorithms. By assessing standard methods against a ground-truth optimum, our work delivers a reproducible foundation for precise and rigorous RL benchmarking.
中文标题/摘要

强化学习算法的客观比较极为复杂，因为不同方法的性能结果与基准测试对环境设计、奖励结构以及算法学习和环境动态中固有的随机性高度敏感。为应对这一复杂性，我们通过将逆最优性扩展至离散时间、控制仿射、含噪声非线性系统，提出了一个严格的基准测试框架。该框架提供了充分必要条件，使得预设的价值函数和策略在构造系统中达到最优，从而能够通过同伦变换和随机化参数系统生成基准测试族。我们通过自动构建多样化环境验证了该框架，展示了其在算法间进行受控且全面评估的能力。通过以真实最优解为基准评估标准方法，本研究为精确严谨的强化学习基准测试提供了可复现的基础。

Physics-Informed Evolution: An Evolutionary Framework for Solving Quantum Control Problems Involving the Schrödinger Equation
Authors: Kaichen Ouyang, Mingyang Yu
First: 2025-02-06T08:43:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:46:04+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) have demonstrated that embedding physical laws directly into the learning objective can significantly enhance the efficiency and physical consistency of neural network solutions. Inspired by this principle, we ask a natural question: can physical information be similarly embedded into the fitness function of evolutionary algorithms? In this work, we propose Physics-Informed Evolution (PIE), a novel framework that incorporates physical information derived from governing physical laws into the evolutionary fitness landscape, bridging the long-standing connection between learning and evolution in artificial intelligence. As a concrete instantiation, we apply PIE to quantum control problems governed by the Schrödinger equation, where the goal is to find optimal control fields that drive quantum systems from initial states to desired target states. We validate PIE on three representative quantum control benchmarks: state preparation in V-type three-level systems, entangled state generation in superconducting quantum circuits, and two-atom cavity QED systems, under varying levels of system uncertainty. Extensive comparisons against ten single-objective and five multi-objective evolutionary baselines demonstrate that PIE consistently achieves higher fidelity, lower state deviation, and improved robustness. Our results suggest that the physics-informed principle extends naturally beyond neural network training to the broader domain of evolutionary computation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：物理信息进化：一种求解含薛定谔方程量子控制问题的进化框架
物理信息神经网络（PINNs）已证明，将物理定律直接嵌入学习目标能显著提升神经网络解的效率和物理一致性。受此启发，我们提出一个自然问题：物理信息能否类似地嵌入进化算法的适应度函数？本文提出物理信息进化（PIE）这一新颖框架，将源自支配性物理定律的物理信息融入进化适应度景观，从而在人工智能领域架起学习与进化之间的长期关联。作为具体实例，我们将PIE应用于薛定谔方程描述的量子控制问题，其目标是寻找最优控制场以驱动量子系统从初始态演化至目标态。我们在三个代表性量子控制基准上验证PIE：V型三能级系统的态制备、超导量子电路中的纠缠态生成，以及双原子腔QED系统，并涵盖不同级别的系统不确定性。与十种单目标和五种多目标进化基线的广泛对比表明，PIE始终能实现更高保真度、更低态偏差及更强鲁棒性。研究结果揭示，物理信息原则可自然拓展至神经网络训练之外的更广泛进化计算领域。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the success of Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) in embedding physical laws into learning objectives, this work explores whether similar principles can enhance evolutionary algorithms by integrating physical information into their fitness functions. The authors propose Physics-Informed Evolution (PIE), a framework that incorporates governing physical laws, specifically the Schrödinger equation, into the evolutionary fitness landscape to solve quantum control problems, aiming to find optimal control fields that drive quantum systems from initial to target states. Experimental validation on three quantum control benchmarks—state preparation in V-type three-level systems, entangled state generation in superconducting circuits, and two-atom cavity QED systems—shows that PIE outperforms ten single-objective and five multi-objective evolutionary baselines, achieving higher fidelity, lower state deviation, and improved robustness under system uncertainties.
受物理信息神经网络（PINNs）将物理定律嵌入学习目标的成功启发，本研究探讨了类似原理是否可通过将物理信息整合到适应度函数中来增强进化算法。作者提出了物理信息进化（PIE）框架，该框架将薛定谔方程等支配性物理定律融入进化适应度景观，以解决量子控制问题，目标是寻找驱动量子系统从初始态到目标态的最优控制场。在三个量子控制基准上的实验验证——V型三能级系统的态制备、超导电路中的纠缠态生成以及双原子腔QED系统——表明，PIE在系统不确定性下优于十个单目标和五个多目标进化基线，实现了更高的保真度、更低的状态偏差和更强的鲁棒性。
Reinforcement learning with learned gadgets to tackle hard quantum problems on real hardware
Authors: Akash Kundu, Leopoldo Sarra
Venue: Communications Physics 9, 44 (2026)
First: 2024-10-31T22:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:44:03+00:00
Comments: 28 page: Gadget reinforcement learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum computing offers exciting opportunities for simulating complex quantum systems and optimizing large scale combinatorial problems, but its practical use is limited by device noise and constrained connectivity. Designing quantum circuits, which are fundamental to quantum algorithms, is therefore a central challenge in current quantum hardware. Existing reinforcement learning based methods for circuit design lose accuracy when restricted to hardware native gates and device level compilation. Here, we introduce gadget reinforcement learning (GRL), which combines learning with program synthesis to automatically construct composite gates that expand the action space while respecting hardware constraints. We show that this approach improves accuracy, hardware compatibility, and scalability for transverse-field Ising and quantum chemistry problems, reaching systems of up to ten qubits within realistic computational budgets. This framework demonstrates how learned, reusable circuit building blocks can guide the co-design of algorithms and hardware for quantum processors.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于学习型量子门控的强化学习解决真实硬件上的困难量子问题
量子计算为模拟复杂量子系统和优化大规模组合问题提供了激动人心的机遇，但其实际应用受限于设备噪声和受限的连接性。量子电路设计作为量子算法的核心基础，成为当前量子硬件面临的关键挑战。现有基于强化学习的电路设计方法在受限于硬件原生门控和设备级编译时会损失精度。本文提出门控强化学习（GRL）方法，将学习与程序合成相结合，自动构建符合硬件约束的复合门控以扩展动作空间。研究表明，该方法在横场伊辛模型和量子化学问题上显著提升了精度、硬件兼容性和可扩展性，在现实计算资源下可处理多达十个量子比特的系统。该框架展示了通过学习可复用的电路构建模块，如何引导量子处理器算法与硬件的协同设计。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of quantum computing, such as device noise and constrained connectivity, which hinder the design of effective quantum circuits on real hardware. The method introduces gadget reinforcement learning (GRL), which combines reinforcement learning with program synthesis to automatically construct composite gates, or gadgets, that expand the action space while adhering to hardware-native constraints. The main experimental results demonstrate that GRL improves accuracy, hardware compatibility, and scalability for problems like transverse-field Ising models and quantum chemistry, successfully scaling to systems of up to ten qubits within practical computational budgets, thereby showcasing how learned, reusable circuit blocks can facilitate algorithm-hardware co-design.

Complementary Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dilxat Muhtar, Jiashun Liu, Wei Gao, Weixun Wang, Shaopan Xiong, Ju Huang, Siran Yang, Wenbo Su, Jiamang Wang, Ling Pan, Bo Zheng
First: 2026-03-18T11:38:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:38:01+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 14 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for training LLM-based agents, yet remains limited by low sample efficiency, stemming not only from sparse outcome feedback but also from the agent's inability to leverage prior experience across episodes. While augmenting agents with historical experience offers a promising remedy, existing approaches suffer from a critical weakness: the experience distilled from history is either stored statically or fail to coevolve with the improving actor, causing a progressive misalignment between the experience and the actor's evolving capability that diminishes its utility over the course of training. Inspired by complementary learning systems in neuroscience, we present Complementary RL to achieve seamless co-evolution of an experience extractor and a policy actor within the RL optimization loop. Specifically, the actor is optimized via sparse outcome-based rewards, while the experience extractor is optimized according to whether its distilled experiences demonstrably contribute to the actor's success, thereby evolving its experience management strategy in lockstep with the actor's growing capabilities. Empirically, Complementary RL outperforms outcome-based agentic RL baselines that do not learn from experience, achieving 10% performance improvement in single-task scenarios and exhibits robust scalability in multi-task settings. These results establish Complementary RL as a paradigm for efficient experience-driven agent learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：互补强化学习
强化学习已成为训练基于大语言模型的智能体的强大范式，但其样本效率低下的问题依然存在。这不仅源于稀疏的结果反馈，还因为智能体无法跨回合利用先验经验。虽然通过历史经验增强智能体是一种有前景的解决方案，但现有方法存在一个关键缺陷：从历史中提炼的经验要么静态存储，要么未能与持续改进的执行器协同进化，导致经验与执行器进化能力之间逐渐失配，从而在训练过程中削弱了经验的效用。受神经科学中互补学习系统的启发，我们提出互补强化学习，旨在强化学习优化循环内实现经验提取器与策略执行器的无缝协同进化。具体而言，执行器通过稀疏的结果奖励进行优化，而经验提取器则根据其提炼的经验是否显著促进执行器的成功进行优化，从而使经验管理策略与执行器增长的能力同步进化。实验表明，互补强化学习优于不从经验中学习的基于结果的智能体强化学习基线，在单任务场景中实现了10%的性能提升，并在多任务设置中展现出强大的可扩展性。这些结果确立了互补强化学习作为高效经验驱动智能体学习的新范式。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the low sample efficiency in reinforcement learning for LLM-based agents, which stems from sparse feedback and an inability to effectively leverage historical experience across episodes. To overcome the misalignment between static experience and the improving actor, the authors propose Complementary RL, a method inspired by complementary learning systems in neuroscience that co-evolves an experience extractor and a policy actor within the RL optimization loop—the actor learns from sparse rewards while the extractor is optimized based on how much its distilled experiences contribute to the actor's success. Experimental results show that Complementary RL outperforms baseline outcome-based RL methods without experience learning, achieving a 10% performance improvement in single-task scenarios and demonstrating robust scalability in multi-task settings, establishing it as an efficient paradigm for experience-driven agent learning.
本文针对基于大语言模型的智能体在强化学习中样本效率低下的问题，该问题源于稀疏反馈和无法跨回合有效利用历史经验。为解决静态经验与改进中的行动者之间的错位，作者受神经科学中互补学习系统的启发，提出了互补强化学习方法，该方法在强化学习优化循环中协同演化经验提取器和策略行动者——行动者从稀疏奖励中学习，而提取器则根据其提炼的经验对行动者成功的贡献程度进行优化。实验结果表明，互补强化学习优于不学习经验的基于结果的基线强化学习方法，在单任务场景中实现了10%的性能提升，并在多任务设置中展现出强大的可扩展性，从而确立其为一种高效的经验驱动智能体学习范式。
Offline Reinforcement Learning via Inverse Optimization
Authors: Ioannis Dimanidis, Tolga Ok, Peyman Mohajerin Esfahani
First: 2025-02-27T12:11:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T11:19:02+00:00
Comments: preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Inspired by the recent successes of Inverse Optimization (IO) across various application domains, we propose a novel offline Reinforcement Learning (ORL) algorithm for continuous state and action spaces, leveraging the convex loss function called ``sub-optimality loss'' from the IO literature. To mitigate the distribution shift commonly observed in ORL problems, we further employ a robust and non-causal Model Predictive Control (MPC) expert steering a nominal model of the dynamics using in-hindsight information stemming from the model mismatch. Unlike the existing literature, our robust MPC expert enjoys an exact and tractable convex reformulation. In the second part of this study, we show that the IO hypothesis class, trained by the proposed convex loss function, enjoys ample expressiveness and {reliably recovers teacher behavior in MuJoCo benchmarks. The method achieves competitive results compared to widely-used baselines in sample-constrained settings, despite using} orders of magnitude fewer parameters. To facilitate the reproducibility of our results, we provide an open-source package implementing the proposed algorithms and the experiments. The code is available at https://github.com/TolgaOk/offlineRLviaIO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于逆优化的离线强化学习

The method demonstrates that the IO hypothesis class is expressive and reliably recovers expert behavior in MuJoCo benchmarks, achieving competitive results with widely-used baselines in sample-constrained settings while using far fewer parameters.

Tree Search for LLM Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuxiang Ji, Ziyu Ma, Yong Wang, Guanhua Chen, Xiangxiang Chu, Liaoni Wu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-25T14:37:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T09:49:32+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026, Code: https://github.com/AMAP-ML/Tree-GRPO
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advances in reinforcement learning (RL) have significantly enhanced the agentic capabilities of large language models (LLMs). In long-term and multi-turn agent tasks, existing approaches driven solely by outcome rewards often suffer from the problem of sparse supervision. To address the challenge, we propose Tree-based Group Relative Policy Optimization (Tree-GRPO), a grouped agent RL method based on tree search, where each tree node represents the complete agent interaction step. By sharing common prefixes, the tree search sampling increases the number of rollouts achievable within a fixed budget of tokens or tool calls. Moreover, we find that the tree-structured trajectory naturally allows the construction of step-wise process supervised signals even using only the outcome reward. Based on this, Tree-GRPO estimates the grouped relative advantages both on intra-tree and inter-tree levels. Through theoretical analysis, we demonstrate that the objective of intra-tree level group relative policy optimization is equivalent to that of step-level direct preference learning. Experiments across 11 datasets and 3 types of QA tasks demonstrate the superiority of the proposed tree-based RL over the chain-based RL method.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于树搜索的大语言模型智能体强化学习方法
强化学习的最新进展显著提升了大语言模型的智能体能力。在长期多轮智能体任务中，仅依赖结果奖励的现有方法常面临监督信号稀疏的问题。为此，我们提出基于树搜索的分组智能体强化学习方法——树结构分组相对策略优化（Tree-GRPO），其中每个树节点代表完整的智能体交互步骤。通过共享公共前缀，树搜索采样能在固定令牌或工具调用预算内实现更多轨迹展开。此外，我们发现树结构轨迹天然支持构建逐步过程监督信号，即使仅使用结果奖励。基于此，Tree-GRPO在树内与树间两个层面估计分组相对优势。理论分析表明，树内层面分组相对策略优化的目标等价于步骤级直接偏好学习的目标。在11个数据集和3类问答任务上的实验验证了所提树基强化学习方法相对于链式强化学习方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sparse supervision problem in long-term, multi-turn agent tasks where existing reinforcement learning (RL) methods rely solely on outcome rewards, this paper introduces Tree-based Group Relative Policy Optimization (Tree-GRPO), a grouped agent RL method leveraging tree search. The method represents each agent interaction step as a tree node, sharing common prefixes to increase rollouts within fixed token or tool-call budgets, and constructs step-wise process supervision from outcome rewards to estimate grouped relative advantages at intra-tree and inter-tree levels. Theoretically, it shows equivalence to step-level direct preference learning, and experiments across 11 datasets and three QA task types demonstrate its superiority over chain-based RL methods.
针对现有强化学习方法在长期多轮智能体任务中仅依赖结果奖励导致的监督稀疏问题，本文提出了基于树搜索的分组智能体强化学习方法——树基分组相对策略优化（Tree-GRPO）。该方法将每个智能体交互步骤表示为树节点，通过共享公共前缀在固定令牌或工具调用预算内增加轨迹采样，并利用结果奖励构建逐步过程监督，以估计树内和树间的分组相对优势。理论分析表明其目标等价于步骤级直接偏好学习，在11个数据集和三种问答任务上的实验验证了该方法优于链式强化学习方法。
Stepwise Think-Critique: A Unified Framework for Robust and Interpretable LLM Reasoning
Authors: Jiaqi Xu, Cuiling Lan, Xuejin Chen, Yan Lu
First: 2025-12-17T18:15:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T09:31:44+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human beings solve complex problems through critical thinking, where reasoning and evaluation are intertwined to converge toward correct solutions. However, most existing large language models (LLMs) treat the reasoning and verification as separate processes: they either generate reasoning without explicit self-checking or rely on external verifiers to detect errors post hoc. The former lacks immediate feedback, while the latter increases system complexity and hinders synchronized learning. Motivated by human critical thinking, we propose Stepwise Think-Critique (STC), a unified and end-to-end trainable framework that interleaves reasoning and self-critique at every intermediate step within a single model. STC is trained with a hybrid reinforcement learning objective that integrates reasoning rewards and critique-consistency rewards, thereby jointly optimizing solution correctness and reliability of self-evaluation. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that STC demonstrates strong critical-thinking capabilities and produces more interpretable reasoning traces, representing a step toward LLMs with built-in critical thinking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：逐步思考-批判：面向鲁棒可解释大语言模型推理的统一框架
人类通过批判性思维解决复杂问题，其推理与评估过程相互交织以趋近正确解。然而现有大语言模型大多将推理与验证视为独立过程：要么生成缺乏显式自检的推理，要么依赖外部验证器进行事后纠错。前者缺乏即时反馈，后者则增加系统复杂度并阻碍协同学习。受人类批判性思维启发，我们提出逐步思考-批判框架——一种统一且端到端可训练的架构，在单一模型内部实现每个中间步骤的推理与自批判交错执行。该框架通过融合推理奖励与批判一致性奖励的混合强化学习目标进行训练，从而协同优化解的正确性与自评估可靠性。数学推理基准实验表明，该框架展现出强大的批判性思维能力，并生成更具可解释性的推理轨迹，标志着向具备内置批判性思维的大语言模型迈进了一步。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to emulate human critical thinking where reasoning and evaluation are intertwined, this paper proposes Stepwise Think-Critique (STC), a unified framework that interleaves reasoning and self-critique at each step within a single large language model. The method employs a hybrid reinforcement learning objective combining reasoning and critique-consistency rewards to jointly optimize solution correctness and self-evaluation reliability. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that STC enhances critical-thinking capabilities and yields more interpretable reasoning traces compared to approaches that separate reasoning and verification.
受人类批判性思维中推理与评估交织的启发，本文提出了逐步思考-批判框架，该统一框架在单个大语言模型内于每个中间步骤交织进行推理与自我批判。该方法采用结合了推理奖励和批判一致性奖励的混合强化学习目标，以共同优化解答的正确性和自我评估的可靠性。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，该框架展现出强大的批判性思维能力，并产生了比将推理与验证分离的方法更具可解释性的推理轨迹。
Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference with Conditional Lagrangian Optimal Transport
Authors: Harry Amad, Mihaela van der Schaar
First: 2026-03-02T11:55:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T09:09:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks (NNs) often have critical behavioural trade-offs that are set at design time with hyperparameters-such as reward weights in reinforcement learning or quantile targets in regression. Post-deployment, however, user preferences can evolve, making initial settings undesirable, necessitating potentially expensive retraining. To circumvent this, we introduce the task of Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI): to learn, from observed data, how a NN's conditional output distribution changes with its hyperparameters, and construct a surrogate model that approximates the NN at unobserved hyperparameter settings. HTI requires extending existing trajectory inference approaches to incorporate conditions, exacerbating the challenge of ensuring inferred paths are feasible. We propose an approach based on conditional Lagrangian optimal transport, jointly learning the Lagrangian function governing hyperparameter-induced dynamics along with the associated optimal transport maps and geodesics between observed marginals, which form the surrogate model. We incorporate inductive biases based on the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles into the learned Lagrangian, improving surrogate model feasibility. We empirically demonstrate that our approach reconstructs NN outputs across various hyperparameter spectra better than other alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的超参数轨迹推断
神经网络（NNs）常存在关键的行为权衡，这些权衡在设计时通过超参数（如强化学习中的奖励权重或回归中的分位数目标）设定。然而，部署后用户偏好可能变化，导致初始设置不再适用，从而需要可能代价高昂的重新训练。为规避此问题，我们提出超参数轨迹推断（HTI）任务：从观测数据中学习神经网络的条件输出分布如何随超参数变化，并构建一个在未观测超参数设置下近似神经网络的代理模型。HTI需扩展现有轨迹推断方法以纳入条件，这加剧了确保推断路径可行的挑战。我们提出一种基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的方法，联合学习控制超参数诱导动态的拉格朗日函数，以及观测边缘分布间的最优传输映射和测地线（构成代理模型）。我们将基于流形假设和最小作用原理的归纳偏置融入所学拉格朗日函数，以提升代理模型的可行性。实验表明，我们的方法在多种超参数谱上重建神经网络输出的效果优于其他替代方案。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the issue where neural networks, once deployed with fixed hyperparameters, become suboptimal as user preferences change, and retraining is costly. The method introduces Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI), which uses conditional Lagrangian optimal transport to learn how a neural network's output distribution varies with hyperparameters, constructing a surrogate model that approximates the network at unseen settings by jointly learning a Lagrangian function, optimal transport maps, and geodesics between observed data. The main experimental results show that this approach, incorporating inductive biases from the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles, reconstructs neural network outputs across hyperparameter spectra more effectively than alternative methods.
本研究的动机是解决神经网络在部署后因用户偏好变化而固定超参数设置不再理想，且重新训练成本高昂的问题。方法上提出了超参数轨迹推断（HTI），基于条件拉格朗日最优传输来学习神经网络输出分布随超参数的变化，通过联合学习拉格朗日函数、最优传输映射和观测数据间的测地线，构建一个在未观测超参数设置下近似原网络的代理模型。主要实验结果表明，该方法结合了流形假设和最小作用原理的归纳偏置，在多种超参数谱上重建神经网络输出的效果优于其他替代方案。
Efficient Soft Actor-Critic with LLM-Based Action-Level Guidance for Continuous Control
Authors: Hao Ma, Zhiqiang Pu, Xiaolin Ai, Huimu Wang
First: 2026-03-18T08:22:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T08:22:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present GuidedSAC, a novel reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm that facilitates efficient exploration in vast state-action spaces. GuidedSAC leverages large language models (LLMs) as intelligent supervisors that provide action-level guidance for the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm. The LLM-based supervisor analyzes the most recent trajectory using state information and visual replays, offering action-level interventions that enable targeted exploration. Furthermore, we provide a theoretical analysis of GuidedSAC, proving that it preserves the convergence guarantees of SAC while improving convergence speed. Through experiments in both discrete and continuous control environments, including toy text tasks and complex MuJoCo benchmarks, we demonstrate that GuidedSAC consistently outperforms standard SAC and state-of-the-art exploration-enhanced variants (e.g., RND, ICM, and E3B) in terms of sample efficiency and final performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型动作级引导的高效软演员-评论家连续控制算法
本文提出GuidedSAC——一种新型强化学习算法，通过大语言模型作为智能监督器为软演员-评论家算法提供动作级引导，从而提升在广阔状态-动作空间中的探索效率。该模型通过分析包含状态信息与视觉回放的最新轨迹，实施精准的动作级干预以实现定向探索。理论分析证明GuidedSAC在保持原算法收敛性的同时提升收敛速度。在离散/连续控制环境（包括文本任务与复杂MuJoCo基准测试）的实验中，GuidedSAC在样本效率与最终性能上均稳定优于标准SAC及前沿探索增强变体（如RND、ICM、E3B）。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces GuidedSAC, a reinforcement learning algorithm designed to improve exploration efficiency in large state-action spaces by integrating large language models (LLMs) as intelligent supervisors. The method enhances the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) algorithm by using an LLM to analyze recent trajectories, including state data and visual replays, to provide targeted action-level guidance that directs exploration. Experimental results on both discrete and continuous control tasks, such as text-based environments and MuJoCo benchmarks, show that GuidedSAC achieves higher sample efficiency and final performance compared to standard SAC and other advanced exploration methods like RND, ICM, and E3B, with theoretical analysis confirming it maintains SAC's convergence guarantees while accelerating convergence.
本文提出了GuidedSAC，一种强化学习算法，旨在通过集成大型语言模型（LLMs）作为智能监督器，提升在大规模状态-动作空间中的探索效率。该方法通过LLM分析包含状态信息和视觉回放的最新轨迹，为软演员-评论家（SAC）算法提供针对性的动作级指导，从而引导探索方向。在离散和连续控制环境（如文本任务和MuJoCo基准测试）中的实验结果表明，GuidedSAC在样本效率和最终性能上均优于标准SAC及其他先进的探索增强变体（如RND、ICM和E3B），理论分析证实其在保持SAC收敛保证的同时加快了收敛速度。
Meta-Reinforcement Learning with Self-Reflection for Agentic Search
Authors: Teng Xiao, Yige Yuan, Hamish Ivison, Huaisheng Zhu, Faeze Brahman, Nathan Lambert, Pradeep Dasigi, Noah A. Smith, Hannaneh Hajishirzi
First: 2026-03-11T21:40:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T07:07:34+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper introduces MR-Search, an in-context meta reinforcement learning (RL) formulation for agentic search with self-reflection. Instead of optimizing a policy within a single independent episode with sparse rewards, MR-Search trains a policy that conditions on past episodes and adapts its search strategy across episodes. MR-Search learns to learn a search strategy with self-reflection, allowing search agents to improve in-context exploration at test-time. Specifically, MR-Search performs cross-episode exploration by generating explicit self-reflections after each episode and leveraging them as additional context to guide subsequent attempts, thereby promoting more effective exploration during test-time. We further introduce a multi-turn RL algorithm that estimates a dense relative advantage at the turn level, enabling fine-grained credit assignment on each episode. Empirical results across various benchmarks demonstrate the advantages of MR-Search over baselines based RL, showing strong generalization and relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% across eight benchmarks. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/tengxiao1/MR-Search.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具备自反思能力的元强化学习在智能搜索中的应用
本文提出MR-Search，一种基于上下文元强化学习的智能搜索框架，具备自反思能力。与在稀疏奖励的独立单次任务中优化策略不同，MR-Search训练的策略能够基于历史任务进行条件化调整，实现跨任务的自适应搜索策略。该方法通过自反思机制学习搜索策略，使智能体在测试阶段能够提升上下文探索能力。具体而言，MR-Search通过在每个任务后生成显式自反思记录，并将其作为后续尝试的附加上下文指导，实现跨任务探索，从而在测试阶段促进更有效的探索。我们进一步提出多轮次强化学习算法，在轮次层面估计密集相对优势，实现对每个任务的细粒度信用分配。多个基准测试的实验结果表明，MR-Search相较于基线强化学习方法具有显著优势，在八个基准测试中展现出强大的泛化能力，相对性能提升达9.2%至19.3%。代码与数据已开源：https://github.com/tengxiao1/MR-Search。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of sparse rewards in traditional reinforcement learning for search tasks, proposing MR-Search, a meta-reinforcement learning framework that enables agents to adapt their search strategies across episodes through self-reflection. The method conditions policies on past episodes, using explicit self-reflections generated after each episode as additional context to guide subsequent attempts, and employs a multi-turn RL algorithm with dense relative advantage estimation for fine-grained credit assignment. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that MR-Search outperforms baseline RL methods, achieving relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% and demonstrating strong generalization capabilities.
本文针对传统强化学习在搜索任务中奖励稀疏的挑战，提出了MR-Search，一种通过自我反思实现跨回合策略适应的元强化学习框架。该方法基于历史回合调整策略，利用每回合后生成的显式自我反思作为额外上下文来指导后续尝试，并采用具有密集相对优势估计的多回合强化学习算法进行细粒度信用分配。在八个基准测试上的实验结果表明，MR-Search优于基线强化学习方法，取得了9.2%至19.3%的相对性能提升，并展现出强大的泛化能力。
Detecting Data Contamination from Reinforcement Learning Post-training for Large Language Models
Authors: Yongding Tao, Tian Wang, Yihong Dong, Huanyu Liu, Kechi Zhang, Xiaolong Hu, Ge Li
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-10T10:58:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:50:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026. Code is available at https://github.com/yongding-tao/RL-Data-Contamination
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Data contamination poses a significant threat to the reliable evaluation of Large Language Models (LLMs). This issue arises when benchmark samples may inadvertently appear in training sets, compromising the validity of reported performance. While detection methods have been developed for the pre-training and Supervised Fine-Tuning stages, a critical research gap exists for the increasingly significant phase of Reinforcement Learning (RL) post-training. As RL post-training becomes pivotal for advancing LLM reasoning, the absence of specialized contamination detection methods in this paradigm presents a critical vulnerability. To address this, we conduct the first systematic study of data detection within RL post-training scenario and propose Self-Critique. Our method is motivated by a key observation: after RL phase, the output entropy distribution of LLMs tends to collapse into highly specific and sparse modes. Self-Critique probes for the underlying policy collapse, i.e., the model's convergence to a narrow reasoning path, which causes this entropy reduction. To facilitate this research, we also introduce RL-MIA, a benchmark constructed to simulate this specific contamination scenario. Extensive experiments show that Self-Critique significantly outperforms baseline methods across multiple models and contamination tasks, achieving an AUC improvement of up to 30%. Whereas existing methods are close to a random guess for RL-phase contamination, our method makes detection possible.
中文标题/摘要
标题：检测大语言模型强化学习后训练阶段的数据污染
数据污染对大语言模型（LLMs）的可靠评估构成重大威胁。当基准样本无意中出现在训练集中时，会导致报告性能的有效性受损。虽然已有针对预训练和监督微调阶段的检测方法，但在日益重要的强化学习（RL）后训练阶段仍存在关键研究空白。随着RL后训练成为提升LLM推理能力的关键环节，该范式下缺乏专门的污染检测方法构成了严重漏洞。为此，我们首次系统研究了RL后训练场景下的数据检测问题，并提出“自我批判”方法。该方法基于关键观察：经过RL阶段后，LLM的输出熵分布倾向于坍缩为高度特定且稀疏的模态。“自我批判”通过探查潜在策略坍缩（即模型收敛至狭窄推理路径导致熵减的现象）实现检测。为推进该研究，我们还构建了RL-MIA基准来模拟此类特定污染场景。大量实验表明，“自我批判”在多个模型和污染任务中显著优于基线方法，AUC提升最高达30%。现有方法对RL阶段污染的检测近乎随机猜测，而我们的方法实现了有效检测。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the critical issue of data contamination in the evaluation of Large Language Models (LLMs), specifically focusing on the underexplored phase of Reinforcement Learning (RL) post-training, where existing detection methods are inadequate. The authors propose a novel method called Self-Critique, which is motivated by the observation that RL post-training causes LLM output entropy distributions to collapse into sparse modes; the method detects this underlying policy collapse to identify contamination. To support this research, they introduce the RL-MIA benchmark for simulating RL-phase contamination, and experimental results demonstrate that Self-Critique significantly outperforms baseline methods, achieving up to a 30% improvement in AUC and making detection feasible where previous methods were nearly random.
本文针对大型语言模型评估中的数据污染问题展开研究，特别关注了强化学习后训练这一尚未充分探索的阶段，该阶段现有检测方法存在不足。作者提出了一种名为Self-Critique的新方法，其动机是观察到强化学习后训练会导致模型输出熵分布坍缩为稀疏模式；该方法通过检测这种潜在策略坍缩来识别污染数据。为支持研究，他们引入了RL-MIA基准来模拟强化学习阶段的污染场景，实验结果表明，Self-Critique显著优于基线方法，AUC提升高达30%，在以往方法接近随机猜测的情况下实现了有效检测。
In-Context Compositional Q-Learning for Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qiushui Xu, Yuhao Huang, Yushu Jiang, Lei Song, Jinyu Wang, Wenliang Zheng, Jiang Bian
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-28T20:55:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-18T06:31:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted by The Fourteenth International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurate estimation of the Q-function is a central challenge in offline reinforcement learning. However, existing approaches often rely on a shared global Q-function, which is inadequate for capturing the compositional structure of tasks that consist of diverse subtasks. We propose In-context Compositional Q-Learning (ICQL), an offline RL framework that formulates Q-learning as a contextual inference problem and uses linear Transformers to adaptively infer local Q-functions from retrieved transitions without explicit subtask labels. Theoretically, we show that, under two assumptions -- linear approximability of the local Q-function and accurate inference of weights from retrieved context -- ICQL achieves a bounded approximation error for the Q-function and enables near-optimal policy extraction. Empirically, ICQL substantially improves performance in offline settings, achieving gains of up to 16.4% on kitchen tasks and up to 8.8% and 6.3% on MuJoCo and Adroit tasks, respectively. These results highlight the underexplored potential of in-context learning for robust and compositional value estimation and establish ICQL as a principled and effective framework for offline RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向离线强化学习的上下文组合Q学习
Q函数的准确估计是离线强化学习的核心挑战。现有方法通常依赖共享的全局Q函数，难以捕捉由多样化子任务构成的任务组合结构。本文提出上下文组合Q学习（ICQL），该离线强化学习框架将Q学习建模为上下文推断问题，利用线性Transformer从检索到的转移样本中自适应推断局部Q函数，无需显式子任务标签。理论分析表明，在局部Q函数线性可近似与上下文权重推断准确两个假设下，ICQL可实现有界的Q函数近似误差，并支持近最优策略提取。实验证明，ICQL在离线场景中显著提升性能：厨房任务提升达16.4%，MuJoCo与Adroit任务分别提升8.8%和6.3%。这些结果揭示了上下文学习在鲁棒组合价值估计中尚未充分挖掘的潜力，确立了ICQL作为离线强化学习理论严谨且高效的方法框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of accurate Q-function estimation in offline reinforcement learning, where existing methods using a shared global Q-function fail to capture the compositional structure of tasks with diverse subtasks. The authors propose In-context Compositional Q-Learning (ICQL), a framework that formulates Q-learning as a contextual inference problem, using linear Transformers to adaptively infer local Q-functions from retrieved transitions without explicit subtask labels. Theoretically, under assumptions of linear approximability and accurate weight inference, ICQL achieves bounded Q-function error and near-optimal policy extraction; empirically, it substantially improves performance, with gains up to 16.4% on kitchen tasks and up to 8.8% and 6.3% on MuJoCo and Adroit tasks, demonstrating the potential of in-context learning for robust value estimation.
