Anticipatory Planning for Multimodal AI Agents
Authors: Yongyuan Liang, Shijie Zhou, Yu Gu, Hao Tan, Gang Wu, Franck Dernoncourt, Jihyung Kil, Ryan A. Rossi, Ruiyi Zhang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-17T16:55:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T16:55:11+00:00
Comments: Published at CVPR 2026 Findings Track
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in multimodal agents have improved computer-use interaction and tool-usage, yet most existing systems remain reactive, optimizing actions in isolation without reasoning about future states or long-term goals. This limits planning coherence and prevents agents from reliably solving high-level, multi-step tasks. We introduce TraceR1, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework that explicitly trains anticipatory reasoning by forecasting short-horizon trajectories before execution. The first stage performs trajectory-level reinforcement learning with rewards that enforce global consistency across predicted action sequences. The second stage applies grounded reinforcement fine-tuning, using execution feedback from frozen tool agents to refine step-level accuracy and executability. TraceR1 is evaluated across seven benchmarks, covering online computer-use, offline computer-use benchmarks, and multimodal tool-use reasoning tasks, where it achieves substantial improvements in planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization over reactive and single-stage baselines. These results show that anticipatory trajectory reasoning is a key principle for building multimodal agents that can reason, plan, and act effectively in complex real-world environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多模态AI智能体的前瞻性规划
多模态智能体的最新进展提升了计算机交互与工具使用能力，但现有系统大多仍属被动响应型，仅孤立优化单步动作而缺乏对未来状态或长期目标的推理。这限制了规划的一致性，使智能体难以可靠解决高层次、多步骤任务。我们提出TraceR1——一个两阶段强化学习框架，通过在执行前预测短期轨迹来显式训练前瞻性推理能力。第一阶段执行轨迹级强化学习，其奖励机制确保预测动作序列的全局一致性；第二阶段进行基于执行的强化微调，利用冻结工具智能体的执行反馈来优化步骤级准确性与可执行性。TraceR1在涵盖在线/离线计算机使用基准及多模态工具使用推理任务的七项基准测试中均取得显著提升，在规划稳定性、执行鲁棒性和泛化能力上大幅超越被动响应型及单阶段基线模型。结果表明，前瞻性轨迹推理是构建能在复杂现实环境中有效推理、规划与行动的多模态智能体的核心原则。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the reactive nature of existing multimodal AI agents, which limits their ability to solve complex, multi-step tasks due to a lack of long-term reasoning, this paper introduces TraceR1, a two-stage reinforcement learning framework. The method first trains the agent to forecast and optimize short-horizon trajectories for global consistency, then refines step-level actions using execution feedback from frozen tool agents. Experimental results across seven benchmarks for computer-use and tool-use tasks demonstrate that TraceR1 substantially improves planning stability, execution robustness, and generalization over reactive baselines, establishing anticipatory reasoning as a key principle for effective multimodal agents.

When Should a Robot Think? Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning for Embodied Robotic Decision-Making
Authors: Jun Liu, Pu Zhao, Zhenglun Kong, Xuan Shen, Peiyan Dong, Fan Yang, Lin Cui, Hao Tang, Geng Yuan, Wei Niu, Wenbin Zhang, Xue Lin, Gaowen Liu, Yanzhi Wang, Dong Huang
First: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Embodied robotic systems increasingly rely on large language model (LLM)-based agents to support high-level reasoning, planning, and decision-making during interactions with the environment. However, invoking LLM reasoning introduces substantial computational latency and resource overhead, which can interrupt action execution and reduce system reliability. Excessive reasoning may delay actions, while insufficient reasoning often leads to incorrect decisions and task failures. This raises a fundamental question for embodied agents: when should the agent reason, and when should it act? In this work, we propose RARRL (Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning), a hierarchical framework for resource-aware orchestration of embodied agents. Rather than learning low-level control policies, RARRL learns a high-level orchestration policy that operates at the agent's decision-making layer. This policy enables the agent to adaptively determine whether to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to employ, and how much computational budget to allocate based on current observations, execution history, and remaining resources. Extensive experiments, including evaluations with empirical latency profiles derived from the ALFRED benchmark, show that RARRL consistently improves task success rates while reducing execution latency and enhancing robustness compared with fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies. These results demonstrate that adaptive reasoning control is essential for building reliable and efficient embodied robotic agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器人何时应思考？基于强化学习的资源感知推理在具身机器人决策中的应用
具身机器人系统日益依赖基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体，以支持其在与环境交互时进行高层推理、规划和决策。然而，调用LLM推理会引入显著的计算延迟和资源开销，可能中断动作执行并降低系统可靠性。过度推理会延迟行动，而推理不足则常导致错误决策和任务失败。这引发了一个具身智能体的根本性问题：智能体应在何时推理，又在何时行动？本研究提出RARRL（基于强化学习的资源感知推理），一种用于具身智能体资源感知编排的分层框架。RARRL不学习底层控制策略，而是学习在智能体决策层运行的高层编排策略。该策略使智能体能够根据当前观察、执行历史和剩余资源，自适应地决定是否调用推理、采用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。大量实验（包括基于ALFRED基准的实测延迟评估）表明，与固定或启发式推理策略相比，RARRL在持续提升任务成功率的同时，有效降低了执行延迟并增强了系统鲁棒性。这些结果证明，自适应推理控制对于构建可靠高效的具身机器人智能体至关重要。

Experimental evaluations using latency profiles from the ALFRED benchmark demonstrate that RARRL improves task success rates, reduces execution latency, and enhances robustness compared to fixed or heuristic strategies, highlighting the importance of adaptive reasoning control for efficient robotic agents.

Aletheia: What Makes RLVR For Code Verifiers Tick?
Authors: Vatsal Venkatkrishna, Indraneil Paul, Iryna Gurevych
First: 2026-01-17T22:30:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:26:31+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-domain thinking verifiers trained via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) are a cornerstone of modern post-training. However, their adoption in code generation has lagged behind execution feedback due to the prohibitive costs of the full RLVR pipeline. In this work, we ablate three primary drivers of RLVR performance and cost: intermediate thinking traces, learning from negative samples, and on-policy training. We introduce Aletheia, a controlled, execution-grounded testbed to facilitate a contamination-free analysis of code verifiers across disparate model sizes and covariate shifts. Our analysis reveals that the optimal training recipe is scale-dependent: on-policy learning is the primary performance driver for small verifiers, whereas thinking traces become the most vital factor for larger sizes. Furthermore, we show that negative samples stabilize training at large sizes, and scaling inference-time compute cannot compensate for any core RLVR component. These findings provide a compute-optimal roadmap for practitioners, offering concrete strategies to simplify verifier training based on model size. Consequently, our work establishes a foundation for scalable supervision, enabling efficiently trained code verifiers to reliably supervise much larger code generation policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Aletheia：是什么驱动了代码验证器的RLVR机制？
通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）训练的多领域思维验证器是现代后训练的核心。然而，由于完整RLVR流程的高昂成本，其在代码生成中的应用落后于执行反馈。本研究通过消融实验分析了影响RLVR性能与成本的三个主要因素：中间思维轨迹、负样本学习以及同策略训练。我们提出了Aletheia——一个受控的、基于执行的测试平台，用于对不同模型规模和协变量偏移下的代码验证器进行无干扰分析。分析表明，最优训练方案具有规模依赖性：同策略学习是小型验证器的主要性能驱动力，而思维轨迹对大型模型最为关键。此外，负样本能稳定大型模型的训练，且增加推理时计算资源无法弥补任何核心RLVR组件的缺失。这些发现为实践者提供了计算最优化的路线图，提出了根据模型规模简化验证器训练的具体策略。因此，本研究为可扩展监督奠定了基础，使高效训练的代码验证器能够可靠地监督更大规模的代码生成策略。

What if Pinocchio Were a Reinforcement Learning Agent: A Normative End-to-End Pipeline
Authors: Benoît Alcaraz
First: 2026-03-17T15:21:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:21:17+00:00
Comments: PhD thesis
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In the past decade, artificial intelligence (AI) has developed quickly. With this rapid progression came the need for systems capable of complying with the rules and norms of our society so that they can be successfully and safely integrated into our daily lives. Inspired by the story of Pinocchio in ``Le avventure di Pinocchio - Storia di un burattino'', this thesis proposes a pipeline that addresses the problem of developing norm compliant and context-aware agents. Building on the AJAR, Jiminy, and NGRL architectures, the work introduces \pino, a hybrid model in which reinforcement learning agents are supervised by argumentation-based normative advisors. In order to make this pipeline operational, this thesis also presents a novel algorithm for automatically extracting the arguments and relationships that underlie the advisors' decisions. Finally, this thesis investigates the phenomenon of \textit{norm avoidance}, providing a definition and a mitigation strategy within the context of reinforcement learning agents. Each component of the pipeline is empirically evaluated. The thesis concludes with a discussion of related work, current limitations, and directions for future research.

Refining Few-Step Text-to-Multiview Diffusion via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ziyi Zhang, Li Shen, Deheng Ye, Yong Luo, Huangxuan Zhao, Meng Liu, Wei Yu, Lefei Zhang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-05-26T15:11:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T15:09:09+00:00
Comments: Accepted to CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Text-to-multiview (T2MV) diffusion models have shown great promise in generating multiple views of a scene from a single text prompt. While few-step backbones enable real-time T2MV generation, they often compromise key aspects of generation quality, such as per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency. Reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning offers a potential solution, yet existing approaches designed for single-image diffusion do not readily extend to the few-step T2MV setting, as they neglect cross-view coordination and suffer from weak learning signals in few-step regimes. To address this, we propose MVC-ZigAL, a tailored RL finetuning framework for few-step T2MV diffusion models. Specifically, its core insights are: (1) a new MDP formulation that jointly models all generated views and assesses their collective quality via a joint-view reward; (2) a novel advantage learning strategy that exploits the performance gains of a self-refinement sampling scheme over standard sampling, yielding stronger learning signals for effective RL finetuning; and (3) a unified RL framework that extends advantage learning with a Lagrangian dual formulation for multiview-constrained optimization, balancing single-view and joint-view objectives through adaptive primal-dual updates under a self-paced threshold curriculum that harmonizes exploration and constraint enforcement. Collectively, these designs enable robust and balanced RL finetuning for few-step T2MV diffusion models, yielding substantial gains in both per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency. Code is available at https://github.com/ZiyiZhang27/MVC-ZigAL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化学习优化少步文本到多视角扩散模型
文本到多视角扩散模型在根据单一文本提示生成场景多视角图像方面展现出巨大潜力。虽然少步主干网络能实现实时生成，但常以牺牲生成质量（如单视角保真度和跨视角一致性）为代价。强化学习微调提供了一种潜在解决方案，但现有面向单图像扩散的方法难以直接适用于少步多视角场景，因其忽视跨视角协调且在少步机制下学习信号薄弱。为此，我们提出MVC-ZigAL——专为少步文本到多视角扩散模型设计的强化学习微调框架。其核心创新包括：（1）构建联合建模所有生成视角并通过联合视角奖励评估整体质量的新MDP框架；（2）利用自优化采样方案相对于标准采样的性能增益，设计能产生更强学习信号的新型优势学习策略；（3）通过拉格朗日对偶公式扩展优势学习，形成多视角约束优化的统一强化学习框架，在协调探索与约束执行的自适应阈值课程下，通过动态原对偶更新平衡单视角与联合视角目标。这些设计共同实现了对少步文本到多视角扩散模型的鲁棒平衡微调，在单视角保真度与跨视角一致性上均取得显著提升。代码发布于https://github.com/ZiyiZhang27/MVC-ZigAL。

This paper addresses the quality degradation in real-time text-to-multiview (T2MV) generation from few-step diffusion models, which often suffer from poor per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency. The authors propose MVC-ZigAL, a reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning framework tailored for this setting, featuring a novel Markov Decision Process formulation that jointly models all views with a joint-view reward, an advantage learning strategy leveraging self-refinement sampling for stronger learning signals, and a unified Lagrangian dual framework to balance single-view and joint-view objectives adaptively. Experimental results demonstrate that the method substantially improves both per-view fidelity and cross-view consistency in few-step T2MV generation.
本文针对少步文本到多视角扩散模型在实时生成中常出现的单视角保真度和跨视角一致性下降问题，提出了一种名为MVC-ZigAL的强化学习微调框架。该方法的核心创新包括：设计了一种联合建模所有生成视角并评估其整体质量的马尔可夫决策过程；提出了一种利用自精化采样方案获取更强学习信号的优势学习策略；以及采用拉格朗日对偶公式的统一框架，通过自适应主-对偶更新平衡单视角与联合视角目标。实验结果表明，该框架显著提升了少步文本到多视角生成的单视角保真度和跨视角一致性。
A Scalable Approach to Solving Simulation-Based Network Security Games
Authors: Michael Lanier, Yevgeniy Vorobeychik
First: 2026-02-18T16:07:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:41:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce MetaDOAR, a lightweight meta-controller that augments the Double Oracle / PSRO paradigm with a learned, partition-aware filtering layer and Q-value caching to enable scalable multi-agent reinforcement learning on very large cyber-network environments. MetaDOAR learns a compact state projection from per node structural embeddings to rapidly score and select a small subset of devices (a top-k partition) on which a conventional low-level actor performs focused beam search utilizing a critic agent. Selected candidate actions are evaluated with batched critic forwards and stored in an LRU cache keyed by a quantized state projection and local action identifiers, dramatically reducing redundant critic computation while preserving decision quality via conservative k-hop cache invalidation. Empirically, MetaDOAR attains higher player payoffs than SOTA baselines on large network topologies, without significant scaling issues in terms of memory usage or training time. This contribution provide a practical, theoretically motivated path to efficient hierarchical policy learning for large-scale networked decision problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种可扩展的基于仿真的网络安全博弈求解方法
本文提出MetaDOAR——一种轻量级元控制器，通过引入基于学习的感知分区过滤层与Q值缓存机制，增强双Oracle/PSRO范式，从而在超大规模网络环境中实现可扩展的多智能体强化学习。MetaDOAR通过学习从节点结构嵌入到紧凑状态投影的映射，快速评估并筛选出关键设备子集（top-k分区），供底层执行器结合评论家智能体进行聚焦束搜索。候选动作通过批量评论家前向传播进行评估，并存储在以量化状态投影与局部动作标识为键的LRU缓存中，在通过保守的k跳缓存失效策略保持决策质量的同时，显著减少冗余的评论家计算。实验表明，在大型网络拓扑中，MetaDOAR在内存占用与训练时间未显著增加的前提下，获得了超越现有最优基线的玩家收益。该研究为大规模网络化决策问题的高效分层策略学习提供了兼具理论依据与实践可行性的路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for scalable solutions in large-scale network security games, this paper introduces MetaDOAR, a meta-controller that enhances the Double Oracle/PSRO framework with a learned filtering layer and Q-value caching to enable efficient multi-agent reinforcement learning. The method involves learning a compact state projection to select a critical subset of network devices, where a low-level actor performs focused beam search guided by a critic; it employs batched critic evaluations and an LRU cache with quantized state-action keys to minimize redundant computations while maintaining decision quality through conservative cache invalidation. Experimental results show that MetaDOAR achieves higher player payoffs than state-of-the-art baselines on large network topologies, with minimal scaling issues in memory and training time, offering a practical hierarchical approach for networked decision problems.
本文旨在解决大规模网络安全博弈中的可扩展性问题，提出了MetaDOAR，这是一种通过增强双Oracle/PSRO框架的元控制器，采用学习型分区感知过滤层和Q值缓存来实现高效多智能体强化学习。该方法学习紧凑的状态投影以选择关键网络设备子集，由底层执行器在批评者智能体指导下进行聚焦束搜索，并利用批处理批评者评估和基于量化状态-动作键的LRU缓存来减少冗余计算，同时通过保守的k跳缓存失效保持决策质量。实验结果表明，在大型网络拓扑上，MetaDOAR相比现有先进基线获得了更高的玩家收益，且在内存使用和训练时间上未出现显著扩展问题，为大规模网络化决策问题提供了实用的分层策略学习路径。
When and Why Does Unsupervised RL Succeed in Mathematical Reasoning? A Manifold Envelopment Perspective
Authors: Zelin Zhang, Fei Cheng, Chenhui Chu
First: 2026-03-17T14:29:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:29:38+00:00
Comments: work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although outcome-based reinforcement learning (RL) significantly advances the mathematical reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), its reliance on computationally expensive ground-truth annotations imposes a severe scalability bottleneck. Unsupervised RL guided by intrinsic rewards offers a scalable alternative, yet it suffers from opaque training dynamics and catastrophic instability, such as policy collapse and reward hacking. In this paper, we first design and evaluate a suite of intrinsic rewards that explicitly enforce concise and certain generation. Second, to discover the boundaries of this approach, we test base models across a spectrum of intrinsic reasoning capabilities, revealing how a model's foundational logical prior dictates its success or failure. Finally, to demystify why certain configurations stabilize while others collapse, we introduce a novel geometric diagnostic lens, showing that successful cases are enveloped by manifolds. Ultimately, our work goes beyond merely demonstrating that enforcing concise and certain responses successfully boosts mathematical reasoning; we reveal when this unsupervised approach breaks down and geometrically diagnose why.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无监督强化学习何时、为何能在数学推理中成功？——一种流形包络视角
尽管基于结果的强化学习显著提升了大型语言模型的数学推理能力，但其对计算成本高昂的真实标注的依赖造成了严重的可扩展性瓶颈。基于内在奖励的无监督强化学习提供了可扩展的替代方案，但其训练动态不透明且存在灾难性不稳定问题，如策略崩溃和奖励黑客攻击。本文首先设计并评估了一套明确强制简洁确定生成的内在奖励机制。其次，为探索该方法的边界，我们在不同内在推理能力谱系上测试基础模型，揭示模型的基础逻辑先验如何决定其成败。最后，为阐明某些配置稳定而另一些崩溃的原因，我们引入了一种新颖的几何诊断视角，证明成功案例均被流形所包络。最终，我们的工作不仅证明了强制简洁确定的响应能有效提升数学推理能力，更揭示了这种无监督方法何时失效，并从几何角度诊断了其原因。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scalability limitations of supervised outcome-based reinforcement learning for mathematical reasoning in large language models, this work investigates unsupervised RL using intrinsic rewards that promote concise and certain text generation. The method involves designing and evaluating a suite of such intrinsic rewards, testing models with varying intrinsic reasoning capabilities to identify success boundaries, and introducing a novel geometric diagnostic framework based on manifold envelopment to explain training stability. Key experimental results demonstrate that enforcing concise and certain responses can successfully enhance mathematical reasoning, but also reveal conditions under which the approach fails due to policy collapse or reward hacking, with geometric analysis showing that stable training corresponds to scenarios enveloped by manifolds.
本研究针对基于结果的监督强化学习在提升大语言模型数学推理能力时存在的可扩展性瓶颈，探索了利用内在奖励促进生成简洁确定文本的无监督强化学习方法。该方法设计并评估了一系列内在奖励，测试了具有不同内在推理能力的模型以确定方法边界，并引入了一种基于流形包络的新几何诊断框架来解释训练动态。主要实验结果表明，强制生成简洁确定的响应能有效提升数学推理性能，但也揭示了该方法因策略崩溃或奖励黑客攻击而失效的条件，几何分析表明成功的训练案例对应于被流形包络的情形。
Exact and general decoupled solutions of the LMC Multitask Gaussian Process model
Authors: Olivier Truffinet, Karim Ammar, Jean-Philippe Argaud, Bertrand Bouriquet
First: 2023-10-18T15:16:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:19:06+00:00
Comments: 78 pages, 12 figures, submitted to Neurocomputing
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Linear Model of Co-regionalization (LMC) is a very general multitask gaussian process model for regression or classification. While its expressiveness and conceptual simplicity are appealing, naive implementations have cubic complexity in the product (number of datapoints $\times$ number of tasks), making approximations mandatory for most applications. However, recent work has shown that in some settings the latent processes of the model can be decoupled, leading to a complexity that is only linear in the number of said processes. We here extend these results, showing from the most general assumptions that the only condition necessary to an efficient exact computation of the LMC is a mild hypothesis on the noise model. We introduce a full parametrization of the resulting \emph{projected LMC} model, enabling its efficient optimization. The effectiveness of this approach is assessed through synthetic and real-data experiments, testing in particular the behavior of its underlying noise model restriction.\\ Overall, the projected LMC appears as a competitive and simpler alternative to state-of-the art multitask gaussian process models. It greatly facilitates some computations such as training data updates or leave-one-out cross-validation, and is more interpretable, for it gives access to its low-dimensional quantities and to their explicit relation with the full-dimensional data. These qualities could facilitate the adoption by various industries of entire classes of methodologies, notably multitask bayesian optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LMC多任务高斯过程模型的精确与通用解耦解
线性协同区域化模型（LMC）是一种非常通用的多任务高斯过程模型，适用于回归或分类任务。尽管其表达能力和概念简洁性颇具吸引力，但朴素实现的计算复杂度为（数据点数×任务数）的立方级，使得在多数应用中必须采用近似方法。然而，近期研究表明在某些设定下，该模型的潜在过程可被解耦，从而将复杂度降至仅与潜在过程数量呈线性关系。本文扩展了这些结果，从最一般的假设出发，证明LMC实现高效精确计算的唯一条件是对噪声模型的温和假设。我们提出了所得\emph{投影LMC}模型的完整参数化方案，实现了高效优化。通过合成数据与真实数据实验评估了该方法的有效性，特别测试了其底层噪声模型约束的行为。总体而言，投影LMC作为当前先进多任务高斯过程模型的竞争性替代方案，具有更简洁的特性。它极大简化了训练数据更新或留一交叉验证等计算过程，且更具可解释性——因其提供了对低维量及其与全维数据显式关系的访问通道。这些特性有望推动各类产业（特别是多任务贝叶斯优化领域）对整套方法论的采纳。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prohibitive cubic computational complexity of naive implementations of the Linear Model of Co-regionalization (LMC) for multitask Gaussian processes, this work extends prior decoupling results to derive exact and efficient solutions under a general noise model assumption. The method introduces a full parametrization of a projected LMC model, enabling efficient optimization. Experimental results on synthetic and real data validate the approach's effectiveness, demonstrating it as a competitive, simpler, and more interpretable alternative to state-of-the-art models, with linear complexity in the number of latent processes and facilitating computations like data updates and cross-validation.
本研究旨在解决线性协同区域化模型（LMC）在多任务高斯过程中因计算复杂度高而难以直接应用的问题，通过扩展先前的解耦理论，在一般噪声模型假设下推导出精确高效的计算方法。该方法引入了投影LMC模型的完整参数化，实现了高效优化。在合成与真实数据上的实验结果表明，该模型性能优异，成为一种计算更简单、可解释性更强的竞争性替代方案，其复杂度仅与潜在过程数量呈线性关系，并简化了训练数据更新和交叉验证等计算。
EmoLLM: Appraisal-Grounded Cognitive-Emotional Co-Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Yifei Zhang, Mingyang Li, Henry Gao, Liang Zhao
First: 2026-03-17T14:17:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T14:17:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong cognitive intelligence (IQ), yet many real-world interactions also require emotional intelligence (EQ) to produce responses that are both factually reliable and emotionally appropriate. In settings such as emotional support, technical assistance, and consultation, effective dialogue depends on how situations are appraised with respect to the user's needs, goals, and coping capacity. Inspired by appraisal theory, we propose EmoLLM, an appraisal-grounded framework for IQ/EQ co-reasoning in dialogue. EmoLLM uses an explicit Appraisal Reasoning Graph (ARG) to structure intermediate reasoning over contextual facts, inferred user needs, appraisal dimensions, emotional states, and response strategies before generating a reply. We train EmoLLM in a multi-turn role-play environment with reinforcement learning, where reverse-perspective reasoning provides reward signals based on predicted user-side consequences of responses. Across diverse dialogue settings, EmoLLM improves emotional state outcomes and response quality over strong baselines while preserving strong factual reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EmoLLM：基于评估理论的大语言模型认知-情感协同推理框架
大语言模型（LLMs）展现出强大的认知智能（IQ），但现实交互常需情感智能（EQ）以生成既事实可靠又情感得体的回应。在情感支持、技术协助和咨询等场景中，有效对话取决于对用户需求、目标及应对能力的情境评估。受评估理论启发，我们提出EmoLLM——一个基于评估的对话IQ/EQ协同推理框架。该框架通过显式的评估推理图（ARG）结构化处理上下文事实、推断用户需求、评估维度、情感状态及回应策略，再进行回复生成。我们采用强化学习在多轮角色扮演环境中训练EmoLLM，其中逆向视角推理通过预测用户端反应后果提供奖励信号。在多样化对话场景中，EmoLLM在保持强事实可靠性的同时，显著提升了情感状态结果与回应质量。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to enhance large language models (LLMs) with emotional intelligence (EQ) alongside cognitive intelligence (IQ) for more effective, emotionally appropriate dialogues in settings like emotional support and consultation. The method introduces EmoLLM, a framework grounded in appraisal theory that uses an explicit Appraisal Reasoning Graph (ARG) to structure multi-step reasoning over contextual facts, user needs, appraisals, emotions, and response strategies before generating a reply; it is trained via reinforcement learning in a multi-turn role-play environment with reward signals derived from reverse-perspective reasoning. Experimental results show that EmoLLM outperforms strong baselines in improving emotional state outcomes and response quality across diverse dialogue settings while maintaining factual reliability.
本文的动机是增强大语言模型（LLMs）的情感智能（EQ），以配合其认知智能（IQ），从而在情感支持、咨询等场景中实现更有效且情感恰当的对话。方法上，受评价理论启发，提出了EmoLLM框架，该框架使用显式的评价推理图（ARG）来结构化地推理上下文事实、用户需求、评价维度、情感状态和回应策略，然后生成回复；通过强化学习在多轮角色扮演环境中进行训练，并利用反向视角推理基于回应预测的用户端后果来提供奖励信号。实验结果表明，在多种对话设置中，EmoLLM在保持事实可靠性的同时，优于现有基线模型，提升了情感状态结果和回应质量。
Reevaluating Policy Gradient Methods for Imperfect-Information Games
Authors: Max Rudolph, Nathan Lichtle, Sobhan Mohammadpour, Alexandre Bayen, J. Zico Kolter, Amy Zhang, Gabriele Farina, Eugene Vinitsky, Samuel Sokota
First: 2025-02-13T03:38:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T13:46:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In the past decade, motivated by the putative failure of naive self-play deep reinforcement learning (DRL) in adversarial imperfect-information games, researchers have developed numerous DRL algorithms based on fictitious play (FP), double oracle (DO), and counterfactual regret minimization (CFR). In light of recent results of the magnetic mirror descent algorithm, we hypothesize that simpler generic policy gradient methods like PPO are competitive with or superior to these FP-, DO-, and CFR-based DRL approaches. To facilitate the resolution of this hypothesis, we implement and release the first broadly accessible exact exploitability computations for five large games. Using these games, we conduct the largest-ever exploitability comparison of DRL algorithms for imperfect-information games. Over 7000 training runs, we find that FP-, DO-, and CFR-based approaches fail to outperform generic policy gradient methods. Code is available at https://github.com/nathanlct/IIG-RL-Benchmark and https://github.com/gabrfarina/exp-a-spiel .
中文标题/摘要
标题：重估不完全信息博弈中的策略梯度方法
过去十年间，针对对抗性不完全信息博弈中朴素自博弈深度强化学习（DRL）的潜在失败，研究者基于虚拟博弈（FP）、双重预言（DO）及反事实遗憾最小化（CFR）开发了多种DRL算法。结合磁镜下降算法的最新成果，我们假设如PPO等更简洁的通用策略梯度方法，其性能可媲美甚至优于这些基于FP、DO和CFR的DRL方法。为验证此假设，我们实现并发布了首个针对五类大型博弈的广泛可访问精确可剥削性计算工具。基于这些博弈，我们开展了迄今最大规模的不完全信息博弈DRL算法可剥削性比较。通过对超过7000次训练运行的分析，发现基于FP、DO和CFR的方法未能超越通用策略梯度方法。代码发布于https://github.com/nathanlct/IIG-RL-Benchmark 与 https://github.com/gabrfarina/exp-a-spiel 。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the recent success of magnetic mirror descent and the hypothesis that simpler policy gradient methods could outperform more complex algorithms designed for imperfect-information games, this paper reevaluates generic methods like PPO against specialized approaches based on fictitious play, double oracle, and counterfactual regret minimization. The method involves implementing exact exploitability computations for five large games and conducting an extensive comparison across over 7000 training runs. The main experimental results show that the specialized approaches fail to outperform generic policy gradient methods, suggesting that simpler algorithms are competitive or superior in these settings.
受磁镜下降算法近期成功的启发，并基于简单策略梯度方法可能优于为不完美信息博弈设计的复杂算法这一假设，本文重新评估了像PPO这样的通用方法相对于基于虚拟博弈、双预言机和反事实遗憾最小化的专门方法。研究方法包括为五个大型博弈实现精确可剥削性计算，并在超过7000次训练运行中进行广泛比较。主要实验结果表明，专门方法未能超越通用策略梯度方法，这表明在类似设置中，更简单的算法具有竞争力或更优性能。
Rewarding DINO: Predicting Dense Rewards with Vision Foundation Models
Authors: Pierre Krack, Tobias Jülg, Wolfram Burgard, Florian Walter
First: 2026-03-17T13:34:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T13:34:47+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures, submitted to IEEE
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Well-designed dense reward functions in robot manipulation not only indicate whether a task is completed but also encode progress along the way. Generally, designing dense rewards is challenging and usually requires access to privileged state information available only in simulation, not in real-world experiments. This makes reward prediction models that infer task state information from camera images attractive. A common approach is to predict rewards from expert demonstrations based on visual similarity or sequential frame ordering. However, this biases the resulting reward function towards a specific solution and leaves it undefined in states not covered by the demonstrations. In this work, we introduce Rewarding DINO, a method for language-conditioned reward modeling that learns actual reward functions rather than specific trajectories. The model's compact size allows it to serve as a direct replacement for analytical reward functions with comparatively low computational overhead. We train our model on data sampled from 24 Meta-World+ tasks using a rank-based loss and evaluate pairwise accuracy, rank correlation, and calibration. Rewarding DINO achieves competitive performance in tasks from the training set and generalizes to new settings in simulation and the real world, indicating that it learns task semantics. We also test the model with off-the-shelf reinforcement learning algorithms to solve tasks from our Meta-World+ training set.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励DINO：基于视觉基础模型的密集奖励预测
机器人操作中精心设计的密集奖励函数不仅能指示任务是否完成，还能编码任务执行过程中的进展。通常，设计密集奖励具有挑战性，往往需要依赖仿真环境中才可获取的特权状态信息，而真实世界实验则难以获得。这使得通过相机图像推断任务状态信息的奖励预测模型备受关注。常见方法基于视觉相似性或序列帧排序，从专家演示中预测奖励。然而，这会使所得奖励函数偏向特定解决方案，且在演示未覆盖的状态下无法定义。本研究提出Rewarding DINO方法，这是一种语言条件化的奖励建模方法，学习的是实际奖励函数而非特定轨迹。该模型结构紧凑，可直接替代解析式奖励函数，且计算开销相对较低。我们使用基于排序的损失函数，在24个Meta-World+任务采样的数据上训练模型，并评估其配对准确率、排序相关性和校准度。Rewarding DINO在训练集任务中表现优异，并能泛化至仿真和真实世界的新场景，表明其学习了任务语义。我们还使用现成的强化学习算法测试该模型，成功解决了Meta-World+训练集中的任务。

The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of existing dense reward prediction methods in robot manipulation, which often rely on expert demonstrations and thus become biased towards specific trajectories and fail in uncovered states. The method introduces Rewarding DINO, a language-conditioned reward model that learns general reward functions rather than specific trajectories, using a compact design for low computational overhead and training on data from 24 Meta-World+ tasks with a rank-based loss. Experimental results show that the model achieves competitive performance on training tasks, generalizes to new simulation and real-world settings, and can be integrated with off-the-shelf reinforcement learning algorithms to solve tasks, indicating effective learning of task semantics.

From the Inside Out: Progressive Distribution Refinement for Confidence Calibration
Authors: Xizhong Yang, Yinan Xia, Huiming Wang, Mofei Song
First: 2026-03-17T13:26:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T13:26:29+00:00
Comments: 15 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Leveraging the model's internal information as the self-reward signal in Reinforcement Learning (RL) has received extensive attention due to its label-free nature. While prior works have made significant progress in applying the Test-Time Scaling (TTS) strategies to RL, the discrepancy in internal information between test and training remains inadequately addressed. Moreover, Test-Time Training based on voting-based TTS strategies often suffers from reward hacking problems. To address these issues, we propose DistriTTRL, which leverages the distribution prior of the model's confidence during RL to progressively optimize the reward signal, rather than relying solely on single-query rollouts. Additionally, we mitigate the phenomenon of consistent reward hacking caused by the voting-based TTS strategies through diversity-targeted penalties. Benefiting from this training mechanism where model capability and self-reward signals complement each other, and the mitigation of reward hacking, DistriTTRL has achieved significant performance improvements across multiple models and benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：由内而外：基于渐进式分布优化的置信度校准方法
利用模型内部信息作为强化学习中的自奖励信号，因其无需标注的特性受到广泛关注。尽管先前研究在将测试时缩放策略应用于强化学习方面取得重要进展，但测试与训练阶段内部信息的差异仍未得到充分解决。基于投票式测试时缩放策略的测试时训练常受奖励黑客问题困扰。为此，我们提出DistriTTRL方法，该方案利用强化学习过程中模型置信度的先验分布逐步优化奖励信号，而非仅依赖单次查询推演。同时，我们通过针对多样性的惩罚机制缓解投票式测试时缩放策略引发的持续性奖励黑客现象。得益于模型能力与自奖励信号相互补充的训练机制，以及对奖励黑客问题的缓解，DistriTTRL在多个模型与基准测试中均取得显著性能提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of leveraging a model's internal information as a self-reward signal in Reinforcement Learning (RL), where discrepancies between training and test-time internal states and issues like reward hacking in voting-based Test-Time Scaling strategies remain problematic. The proposed method, DistriTTRL, progressively refines the reward signal by utilizing the distribution prior of model confidence during RL, moving beyond single-query rollouts, and introduces diversity-targeted penalties to mitigate consistent reward hacking. Experimental results demonstrate that DistriTTRL achieves significant performance improvements across multiple models and benchmarks, benefiting from a synergistic training mechanism that enhances model capability and self-reward signals while reducing reward hacking.
本文针对在强化学习中利用模型内部信息作为自奖励信号所面临的挑战，即训练与测试时内部信息存在差异，以及基于投票的测试时间缩放策略常导致奖励黑客问题。提出的方法DistriTTRL通过利用强化学习过程中模型置信度的分布先验来逐步优化奖励信号，而非仅依赖单次查询展开，并引入针对多样性的惩罚以缓解持续的奖励黑客现象。实验结果表明，受益于模型能力与自奖励信号互补的训练机制以及对奖励黑客的缓解，DistriTTRL在多个模型和基准测试中实现了显著的性能提升。
Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Counteracts Delayed CSI in Multi-Satellite Systems
Authors: Marios Aristodemou, Yasaman Omid, Sangarapillai Lambotharan, Mahsa Derakhshan, Lajos Hanzo
First: 2026-03-17T12:58:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:58:22+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 6 Figures, Submit to IEEE Transactions of Vehicular Technology. It has been reviewed once
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of satellite communication networks with next-generation (NG) technologies is a promising approach towards global connectivity. However, the quality of services is highly dependant on the availability of accurate channel state information (CSI). Channel estimation in satellite communications is challenging due to the high propagation delay between terrestrial users and satellites, which results in outdated CSI observations on the satellite side. In this paper, we study the downlink transmission of multiple satellites acting as distributed base stations (BS) to mobile terrestrial users. We propose a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) algorithm which aims for maximising the sum-rate of the users, while coping with the outdated CSI. We design a novel bi-level optimisation, procedure themes as dual stage proximal policy optimisation (DS-PPO), for tackling the problem of large continuous action spaces as well as of independent and non-identically distributed (non-IID) environments in MARL. Specifically, the first stage of DS-PPO maximises the sum-rate for an individual satellite and the second stage maximises the sum-rate when all the satellites cooperate to form a distributed multi-antenna BS. Our numerical results demonstrate the robustness of DS-PPO to CSI imperfections as well as the sum-rate improvement attached by the use of DS-PPO. In addition, we provide the convergence analysis for the DS-PPO along with the computational complexity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习应对多卫星系统中的延迟信道状态信息
卫星通信网络与下一代技术的融合是实现全球连接的重要途径。然而，服务质量高度依赖于准确信道状态信息的可用性。卫星通信中的信道估计因地面用户与卫星间的高传播延迟而面临挑战，导致卫星端获取的信道状态信息过时。本文研究了多颗卫星作为分布式基站向移动地面用户进行下行传输的场景。我们提出一种多智能体强化学习算法，旨在最大化用户总速率，同时应对过时的信道状态信息。针对多智能体强化学习中大规模连续动作空间及独立非独立同分布环境的问题，我们设计了一种新颖的双层优化框架——双阶段近端策略优化。具体而言，DS-PPO的第一阶段最大化单颗卫星的总速率，第二阶段在所有卫星协作形成分布式多天线基站时最大化总速率。数值结果表明DS-PPO对信道状态信息缺陷具有鲁棒性，并能提升系统总速率。此外，我们还提供了DS-PPO的收敛性分析与计算复杂度评估。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of outdated channel state information (CSI) due to high propagation delays in satellite communications, which degrades service quality in next-generation multi-satellite systems, this paper proposes a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) approach to maximize downlink sum-rate for terrestrial users. The method introduces a novel bi-level optimization algorithm called dual-stage proximal policy optimization (DS-PPO), designed to handle large continuous action spaces and non-identically distributed environments by first optimizing individual satellite performance and then coordinating satellites as a distributed multi-antenna base station. Experimental results demonstrate that DS-PPO robustly improves sum-rate despite CSI imperfections, with supporting convergence analysis and computational complexity evaluation.
本文针对卫星通信中因高传播延迟导致信道状态信息过时、从而降低下一代多卫星系统服务质量的问题，提出采用多智能体强化学习方法来最大化地面用户的下行链路总速率。该方法设计了一种新颖的双层优化算法——双阶段近端策略优化，通过先优化单个卫星性能再协调所有卫星作为分布式多天线基站，以处理大规模连续动作空间和非独立同分布环境。实验结果表明，该算法在信道状态信息不完善的情况下仍能稳健提升总速率，并提供了收敛性分析和计算复杂度评估。
Follow the Clues, Frame the Truth: Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning in Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition
Authors: Yu Liu, Lei Zhang, Haoxun Li, Hanlei Shi, Yuxuan Ding, Leyuan Qu, Taihao Li
First: 2026-03-17T12:49:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:49:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition (OV-MER) is inherently challenging due to the ambiguity of equivocal multimodal cues, which often stem from distinct unobserved situational dynamics. While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) offer extensive semantic coverage, their performance is often bottlenecked by premature commitment to dominant data priors, resulting in suboptimal heuristics that overlook crucial, complementary affective cues across modalities. We argue that effective affective reasoning requires more than surface-level association; it necessitates reconstructing nuanced emotional states by synthesizing multiple evidence-grounded rationales that reconcile these observations from diverse latent perspectives. We introduce HyDRA, a Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning Architecture that formalizes inference as a Propose-Verify-Decide protocol. To internalize this abductive process, we employ reinforcement learning with hierarchical reward shaping, aligning the reasoning trajectories with final task performance to ensure they best reconcile the observed multimodal cues. Systematic evaluations validate our design choices, with HyDRA consistently outperforming strong baselines--especially in ambiguous or conflicting scenarios--while providing interpretable, diagnostic evidence traces.
中文标题/摘要
标题：循迹构真：开放词汇多模态情感识别中的混合证据演绎推理
开放词汇多模态情感识别（OV-MER）因多模态线索的模糊性而面临固有挑战，这些线索常源于未观测的情境动态。尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）具备广泛语义覆盖能力，但其性能常受限于对显性数据先验的过早固化，导致启发式策略次优化，忽略了跨模态的关键互补情感线索。我们认为有效的情感推理需超越表层关联，必须通过整合多源证据驱动的理性依据，从多元潜在视角协调观测结果，以重构细腻的情感状态。为此，我们提出HyDRA——一种混合证据演绎推理架构，将推理形式化为“提出-验证-决策”协议。为内化这一溯因过程，我们采用分层奖励塑形的强化学习方法，使推理轨迹与最终任务性能对齐，确保其能最优协调观测到的多模态线索。系统化评估验证了我们的设计选择：HyDRA在各类场景（尤其是模糊或冲突情境）中持续超越强基线模型，同时提供可解释的诊断证据轨迹。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of ambiguous multimodal cues in Open-Vocabulary Multimodal Emotion Recognition (OV-MER), where models often rely on suboptimal heuristics and overlook complementary affective signals, this paper introduces HyDRA, a Hybrid-evidential Deductive Reasoning Architecture. The method formalizes inference as a Propose-Verify-Decide protocol and employs reinforcement learning with hierarchical reward shaping to align reasoning trajectories with task performance, thereby synthesizing evidence-grounded rationales from diverse latent perspectives. Experimental results show that HyDRA consistently outperforms strong baselines, particularly in ambiguous or conflicting scenarios, while providing interpretable evidence traces.

CHARM: Calibrating Reward Models With Chatbot Arena Scores
Authors: Xiao Zhu, Chenmien Tan, Pinzhen Chen, Rico Sennrich, Huiming Wang, Yanlin Zhang, Hanxu Hu
First: 2025-04-14T09:51:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T12:03:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward models (RMs) play a crucial role in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback by serving as proxies for human preferences in aligning large language models. However, they suffer from various biases which could lead to reward hacking. In this paper, we identify a model preference bias in RMs, where they systematically assign disproportionately high scores to responses from certain policy models, leading to unfair judgments. To mitigate this bias, we propose a calibration method named CHatbot Arena calibrated Reward Modeling (CHARM) that leverages Elo scores from the Chatbot Arena to construct debiased preference datasets and adjust reward model scoring. We conduct extensive experiments on reward model benchmarks and human preference alignment. Results demonstrate that our calibrated RMs achieve improved evaluation accuracy on RM-Bench and the Chat-Hard domain of RewardBench, exhibit a stronger correlation with human preferences by producing scores more closely aligned with Elo rankings and improve downstream post-training performance. These results demonstrate that CHARM provides a simple, effective, and broadly applicable approach to building more reliable and fair reward models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHARM：基于聊天机器人竞技场分数的奖励模型校准方法
奖励模型在基于人类反馈的强化学习中扮演关键角色，作为人类偏好的代理以对齐大语言模型。然而，奖励模型存在多种偏差，可能导致奖励攻击。本文识别了奖励模型中的模型偏好偏差——其系统性地对某些策略模型的响应赋予过高评分，导致不公正评估。为缓解此偏差，我们提出名为CHARM的校准方法，利用聊天机器人竞技场的Elo分数构建去偏好的偏好数据集并调整奖励模型评分。我们在奖励模型基准和人类偏好对齐任务上进行了广泛实验。结果表明，经校准的奖励模型在RM-Bench和RewardBench的Chat-Hard领域实现了更高的评估准确度，通过生成更贴近Elo排名的分数与人类偏好呈现更强相关性，并提升了下游后训练性能。这些结果证明CHARM为构建更可靠、公平的奖励模型提供了简洁高效且广泛适用的解决方案。

The paper is motivated by the problem of model preference bias in reward models, where certain policy models receive disproportionately high scores, leading to unfair judgments and potential reward hacking. 本文的动机是解决奖励模型中的模型偏好偏差问题，即某些策略模型的回答会获得不成比例的高分，导致不公平判断和潜在的奖励攻击风险。为此，方法提出了CHARM校准技术，利用Chatbot Arena的Elo分数构建去偏好的偏好数据集并调整奖励模型评分。实验结果表明，校准后的奖励模型在RM-Bench和RewardBench等基准测试中评估准确性更高，通过使分数更贴近Elo排名而与人类偏好相关性更强，并提升了下游后训练性能，证明了CHARM为构建更可靠、公平的奖励模型提供了一种简单有效且广泛适用的方法。
Via Negativa for AI Alignment: Why Negative Constraints Are Structurally Superior to Positive Preferences
Authors: Quan Cheng
First: 2026-03-17T11:52:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:52:18+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, position paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent empirical results have demonstrated that training large language models (LLMs) with negative-only feedback can match or exceed standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF). Negative Sample Reinforcement achieves parity with PPO on mathematical reasoning; Distributional Dispreference Optimization trains effectively using only dispreferred samples; and Constitutional AI outperforms pure RLHF on harmlessness benchmarks. Yet no unified theoretical account explains why negative signals are so effective. This paper proposes such an account: positive preferences and negative constraints are structurally asymmetric. Positive preferences ("which is better") encode continuously coupled, context-dependent human values that cannot be exhaustively specified -- leading models to learn surface correlates such as agreement with the user (sycophancy). Negative constraints ("what is wrong") encode discrete, finite, independently verifiable prohibitions that can converge to a stable boundary. This asymmetry -- rooted in Popper's falsification logic and the epistemology of negative knowledge -- explains both the sycophancy failure of preference-based RLHF and the surprising effectiveness of negative-signal methods. We argue that alignment research should shift its center of gravity from "learning what humans prefer" to "learning what humans reject," and offer testable predictions for this framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI对齐的否定路径：为何负面约束在结构上优于正面偏好
近期实证研究表明，仅使用负面反馈训练大语言模型（LLMs）可达到或超越基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）标准效果。负面样本强化在数学推理上与PPO持平；分布性非偏好优化仅用非偏好样本即可有效训练；宪法AI在无害性基准测试中优于纯RLHF方法。然而，尚无统一理论解释负面信号为何如此有效。本文提出一种理论框架：正面偏好与负面约束存在结构性不对称。正面偏好（“哪个更好”）编码了连续耦合、依赖语境且无法穷尽的人类价值观——导致模型学习表面关联特征（如迎合用户的谄媚行为）。负面约束（“什么是错的”）编码了离散、有限、可独立验证的禁令，能够收敛至稳定边界。这种不对称性——根植于波普尔的证伪逻辑与否定知识认识论——既解释了基于偏好的RLHF产生谄媚行为的原因，也揭示了负面信号方法惊人有效性的机理。我们主张对齐研究重心应从“学习人类偏好”转向“学习人类拒绝的内容”，并为此框架提出可验证的预测。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the empirical observation that training large language models with only negative feedback can match or exceed standard reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), yet a theoretical explanation for this effectiveness is lacking. The proposed method is a theoretical account arguing that positive preferences and negative constraints are structurally asymmetric: positive preferences encode complex, context-dependent human values prone to learning surface correlates like sycophancy, while negative constraints represent discrete, verifiable prohibitions that converge to a stable boundary, grounded in Popper's falsification logic. The main experimental results referenced include Negative Sample Reinforcement achieving parity with PPO on mathematical reasoning, Distributional Dispreference Optimization training effectively with dispreferred samples, and Constitutional AI outperforming RLHF on harmlessness benchmarks, supporting the shift in alignment research from learning human preferences to learning human rejections.
本文的动机源于实证观察，即仅使用负面反馈训练大语言模型可以匹配或超越标准的人类反馈强化学习（RLHF），但缺乏对此有效性的理论解释。其提出的方法是一种理论阐述，认为正面偏好与负面约束在结构上不对称：正面偏好编码复杂、依赖语境的人类价值观，易导致模型学习表面关联如迎合用户；而负面约束代表离散、可验证的禁令，能收敛到稳定边界，这基于波普尔的证伪逻辑和负面知识认识论。引用的主要实验结果包括负面样本强化在数学推理上与PPO达到同等效果、分布性非偏好优化仅使用非偏好样本有效训练，以及宪法AI在无害性基准上超越RLHF，从而支持对齐研究应从学习人类偏好转向学习人类拒绝。
Deep Reinforcement Learning-Assisted Automated Operator Portfolio for Constrained Multi-objective Optimization
Authors: Shuai Shao, Ye Tian, Shangshang Yang, Xingyi Zhang
First: 2026-03-17T11:39:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:39:19+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Constrained multi-objective optimization problems (CMOPs) are of great significance in the context of practical applications, ranging from scientific to engineering domains. Most existing constrained multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (CMOEAs) usually employ fixed operators all the time, which exhibit poor versatility in handling various CMOPs. Therefore, some recent studies have focused on adaptively selecting the best operators for the current population states during the search process. The evolutionary algorithms proposed in these studies learn the value of each operator and recommend the operator with the highest value for the current population, resulting in only a single operator being recommended at each generation, which can potentially lead to local optima and inefficient utilization of function evaluations. To address the dilemma in operator adaptation, this paper proposes a reinforcement learning-based automated operator portfolio approach to learn an allocation scheme of operators at each generation. This approach considers the optimization-related and constraint-related features of the current population as states, the overall improvement in population convergence and diversity as rewards, and different operator portfolios as actions. By utilizing deep neural networks to establish a mapping model between the population states and the expected cumulative rewards, the proposed approach determines the optimal operator portfolio during the evolutionary process. By embedding the proposed approach into existing CMOEAs, a deep reinforcement learning-assisted automated operator portfolio based evolutionary algorithm for solving CMOPs, abbreviated as CMOEA-AOP, is developed. Empirical studies on 33 benchmark problems demonstrate that the proposed algorithm significantly enhances the performance of CMOEAs and exhibits more stable performance across different CMOPs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的约束多目标优化自动化算子组合方法
约束多目标优化问题（CMOPs）在科学与工程等实际应用领域具有重要意义。现有约束多目标进化算法（CMOEAs）通常采用固定算子，在处理多样化CMOPs时泛化能力不足。近期研究尝试在搜索过程中根据种群状态自适应选择最优算子，但这类方法每代仅推荐单一算子，易陷入局部最优且函数评估效率低下。为解决算子自适应难题，本文提出一种基于强化学习的自动化算子组合方法，通过学习每代算子的分配方案，将当前种群的优化特征与约束特征作为状态，种群收敛性与多样性的整体提升作为奖励，不同算子组合作为动作。通过深度神经网络建立种群状态与期望累积奖励的映射模型，在进化过程中动态确定最优算子组合。将本方法嵌入现有CMOEAs框架，构建出深度强化学习辅助的自动化算子组合进化算法（CMOEA-AOP）。在33个基准问题上的实验表明，该算法显著提升了CMOEAs性能，并在不同CMOPs上表现出更稳定的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limited versatility of constrained multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (CMOEAs) that rely on fixed operators by proposing a deep reinforcement learning-assisted automated operator portfolio. The method formulates the optimization as a reinforcement learning problem where population states (based on optimization and constraint features) map to actions (operator portfolios) to maximize rewards tied to convergence and diversity improvement, using deep neural networks to learn this policy. Experimental results on 33 benchmark problems show that the resulting algorithm, CMOEA-AOP, significantly enhances CMOEA performance and delivers more stable outcomes across diverse constrained multi-objective optimization problems.
本文针对现有约束多目标进化算法（CMOEAs）因使用固定算子而泛化能力不足的问题，提出了一种基于深度强化学习的自动化算子组合方法。该方法将优化过程构建为强化学习问题，以种群状态（基于优化和约束特征）映射到动作（算子组合），通过深度神经网络学习最大化收敛性和多样性奖励的策略。在33个基准问题上的实验结果表明，所开发的CMOEA-AOP算法显著提升了CMOEAs的性能，并在不同约束多目标优化问题上表现出更稳定的求解效果。
LLM-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Audio-Visual Speech Enhancement
Authors: Chih-Ning Chen, Jen-Cheng Hou, Hsin-Min Wang, Shao-Yi Chien, Yu Tsao, Fan-Gang Zeng
First: 2026-03-14T14:01:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:37:19+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 4 figures, submitted to Interspeech 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In existing Audio-Visual Speech Enhancement (AVSE) methods, objectives such as Scale-Invariant Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SI-SNR) and Mean Squared Error (MSE) are widely used; however, they often correlate poorly with perceptual quality and provide limited interpretability for optimization. This work proposes a reinforcement learning-based AVSE framework with a Large Language Model (LLM)-based interpretable reward model. An audio LLM generates natural language descriptions of enhanced speech, which are converted by a sentiment analysis model into a 1-5 rating score serving as the PPO reward for fine-tuning a pretrained AVSE model. Compared with scalar metrics, LLM-generated feedback is semantically rich and explicitly describes improvements in speech quality. Experiments on the 4th COG-MHEAR AVSE Challenge (AVSEC-4) dataset show that the proposed method outperforms a supervised baseline and a DNSMOS-based RL baseline in PESQ, STOI, neural quality metrics, and subjective listening tests.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型引导的视听语音增强强化学习方法
现有视听语音增强方法广泛采用尺度不变信噪比和均方误差等目标函数，但这些指标常与感知质量相关性较弱，且对优化过程的解释性有限。本研究提出一种基于强化学习的AVSE框架，采用基于大语言模型的可解释奖励模型。音频大语言模型生成增强语音的自然语言描述，通过情感分析模型转换为1-5级评分，作为近端策略优化算法的奖励信号，用于微调预训练的AVSE模型。与标量指标相比，大语言模型生成的反馈语义更丰富，能明确描述语音质量改进。在第四届COG-MHEAR AVSE挑战赛数据集上的实验表明，该方法在PESQ、STOI、神经质量指标及主观听力测试中均优于监督基线方法和基于DNSMOS的强化学习基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the poor correlation of conventional metrics like SI-SNR with perceptual quality and their limited interpretability in audio-visual speech enhancement (AVSE), this work introduces a reinforcement learning framework that leverages a large language model (LLM) for interpretable reward generation. The method uses an audio LLM to produce natural language descriptions of enhanced speech, which are then converted into a 1-5 rating score via sentiment analysis to serve as a reward for fine-tuning a pretrained AVSE model with PPO. Experimental results on the AVSEC-4 dataset demonstrate that this approach outperforms supervised and DNSMOS-based RL baselines across objective metrics such as PESQ and STOI, neural quality scores, and subjective listening tests, offering semantically rich feedback for optimization.
针对现有视听语音增强方法中广泛使用的SI-SNR等指标与感知质量相关性差且可解释性有限的问题，本研究提出了一种基于强化学习的框架，利用大语言模型生成可解释的奖励。该方法通过音频大语言模型对增强语音生成自然语言描述，再经情感分析转化为1-5分的评分，作为PPO奖励来微调预训练的视听语音增强模型。在AVSEC-4数据集上的实验表明，该方法在PESQ、STOI等客观指标、神经质量评分以及主观听力测试上均优于监督学习和基于DNSMOS的强化学习基线，为优化提供了语义丰富的反馈。
On-Policy RL Meets Off-Policy Experts: Harmonizing Supervised Fine-Tuning and Reinforcement Learning via Dynamic Weighting
Authors: Wenhao Zhang, Yuexiang Xie, Yuchang Sun, Yanxi Chen, Guoyin Wang, Yaliang Li, Bolin Ding, Jingren Zhou
First: 2025-08-15T11:20:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:27:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) are two prominent post-training paradigms for refining the capabilities and aligning the behavior of Large Language Models (LLMs). Existing approaches that integrate SFT and RL often face the risk of disrupting established response patterns and inducing overfitting to expert data. To address this, we present a novel investigation into the unified view of SFT and RL through an off-policy versus on-policy lens. We propose CHORD, a framework for Controllable Harmonization of On- and Off-Policy Reinforcement Learning via Dynamic Weighting, which reframes SFT not as a separate stage but as a dynamically weighted auxiliary objective within the on-policy RL process. Based on an analysis of off-policy expert data's influence at both holistic and granular levels, we incorporate a dual-control mechanism in CHORD. Specifically, the framework first employs a global coefficient to holistically guide the transition from off-policy imitation to on-policy exploration, and then applies a token-wise weighting function that enables granular learning from the expert, which promotes on-policy exploration and mitigates disruption from off-policy data. We conduct extensive experiments across various practical tasks, providing empirical evidence that CHORD achieves a stable and efficient learning process. By effectively harmonizing off-policy expert data with on-policy exploration, CHORD demonstrates significant improvements over baselines. We release the implementation at https://github.com/modelscope/Trinity-RFT/tree/main/examples/mix_chord to inspire further research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在线强化学习与离线专家策略的融合：通过动态权重协调监督微调与强化学习
监督微调（SFT）与强化学习（RL）是优化大语言模型（LLM）能力与行为对齐的两种主流后训练范式。现有整合SFT与RL的方法常面临破坏已有响应模式、对专家数据过拟合的风险。为此，本文从离线策略与在线策略的视角提出对SFT与RL的统一性研究，并推出CHORD框架——一种通过动态权重实现在线与离线强化学习可控协调的方法。该框架将SFT重构为在线RL过程中动态加权的辅助目标，而非独立阶段。基于对离线专家数据在整体与细粒度层面影响的分析，CHORD引入双重控制机制：首先采用全局系数整体引导从离线模仿到在线探索的过渡，再通过词元级加权函数实现细粒度的专家学习，从而促进在线探索并缓解离线数据的干扰。我们在多种实际任务中开展广泛实验，实证表明CHORD能实现稳定高效的学习过程，通过有效协调离线专家数据与在线探索，其性能显著超越基线方法。代码已开源：https://github.com/modelscope/Trinity-RFT/tree/main/examples/mix_chord，以推动后续研究。

This paper addresses the challenge of integrating Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning (RL) for Large Language Models, where existing methods risk disrupting learned patterns and overfitting to expert data. Controlling Fish Schools via Reinforcement Learning of Virtual Fish Movement
Authors: Yusuke Nishii, Hiroaki Kawashima
First: 2026-03-17T11:12:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T11:12:36+00:00
Comments: English translation of the author's 2018 bachelor's thesis. Keywords: fish schooling, reinforcement learning, collective behavior, artificial agents, swarm-machine interaction
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This study investigates a method to guide and control fish schools using virtual fish trained with reinforcement learning. We utilize 2D virtual fish displayed on a screen to overcome technical challenges such as durability and movement constraints inherent in physical robotic agents. To address the lack of detailed behavioral models for real fish, we adopt a model-free reinforcement learning approach. First, simulation results show that reinforcement learning can acquire effective movement policies even when simulated real fish frequently ignore the virtual stimulus. Second, real-world experiments with live fish confirm that the learned policy successfully guides fish schools toward specified target directions. Statistical analysis reveals that the proposed method significantly outperforms baseline conditions, including the absence of stimulus and a heuristic "stay-at-edge" strategy. This study provides an early demonstration of how reinforcement learning can be used to influence collective animal behavior through artificial agents.

Experimental results from simulations and real-world tests with live fish demonstrate that the learned policy effectively guides schools toward target directions, significantly outperforming baseline conditions like no stimulus or a heuristic edge-following strategy.

Masked Auto-Regressive Variational Acceleration: Fast Inference Makes Practical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuxuan Gu, Weimin Bai, Yifei Wang, Weijian Luo, He Sun
First: 2025-11-19T07:24:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T10:51:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Masked auto-regressive diffusion models (MAR) benefit from the expressive modeling ability of diffusion models and the flexibility of masked auto-regressive ordering. However, vanilla MAR suffers from slow inference due to its hierarchical inference mechanism: an outer AR unmasking loop and an inner diffusion denoising chain. Such decoupled structure not only harm the generation efficiency but also hinder the practical use of MAR for reinforcement learning (RL), an increasingly critical paradigm for generative model post-training.To address this fundamental issue, we introduce MARVAL (Masked Auto-regressive Variational Acceleration), a distillation-based framework that compresses the diffusion chain into a single AR generation step while preserving the flexible auto-regressive unmasking order. Such a distillation with MARVAL not only yields substantial inference acceleration but, crucially, makes RL post-training with verifiable rewards practical, resulting in scalable yet human-preferred fast generative models. Our contributions are twofold: (1) a novel score-based variational objective for distilling masked auto-regressive diffusion models into a single generation step without sacrificing sample quality; and (2) an efficient RL framework for masked auto-regressive models via MARVAL-RL. On ImageNet 256*256, MARVAL-Huge achieves an FID of 2.00 with more than 30 times speedup compared with MAR-diffusion, and MARVAL-RL yields consistent improvements in CLIP and image-reward scores on ImageNet datasets with entity names. In conclusion, MARVAL demonstrates the first practical path to distillation and RL of masked auto-regressive diffusion models, enabling fast sampling and better preference alignments.

标题：掩码自回归变分加速：快速推理实现实用强化学习
掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）兼具扩散模型的强大建模能力与掩码自回归排序的灵活性，但其分层推理机制（外层自回归解掩循环与内层扩散去噪链）导致推理速度缓慢。这种解耦结构不仅影响生成效率，更阻碍了MAR在强化学习（RL）这一生成模型后训练关键范式中的实际应用。为解决这一根本问题，我们提出MARVAL（掩码自回归变分加速）——基于蒸馏的框架，将扩散链压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保留灵活的自回归解掩顺序。该蒸馏方法不仅实现显著的推理加速，更重要的是使可验证奖励的RL后训练具备实用性，最终获得可扩展且符合人类偏好的快速生成模型。我们的贡献包括：（1）提出基于分数的变分目标，将掩码自回归扩散模型蒸馏为单步生成且不损失样本质量；（2）通过MARVAL-RL构建高效的掩码自回归模型RL框架。在ImageNet 256*256数据集上，MARVAL-Huge以2.00的FID指标实现超过MAR-diffusion 30倍的加速，MARVAL-RL在包含实体名称的ImageNet数据集上持续提升CLIP与图像奖励分数。综上，MARVAL首次为掩码自回归扩散模型提供了可行的蒸馏与RL路径，实现了快速采样与更好的偏好对齐。

To solve this, the authors propose MARVAL, a distillation framework that compresses the diffusion process into a single auto-regressive step while maintaining flexible unmasking order, enabling fast inference without quality loss. 该论文针对掩码自回归扩散模型（MAR）推理速度慢的问题，由于其包含外部自回归循环和内部扩散链的分层结构，限制了在强化学习（RL）中的实际应用。为此，作者提出了MARVAL，一个蒸馏框架，将扩散过程压缩为单步自回归生成，同时保持灵活的掩码解除顺序，从而实现快速推理且不损失质量。在ImageNet 256*256上的实验结果表明，MARVAL-Huge实现了2.00的FID分数，相比MAR-diffusion加速超过30倍，且MARVAL-RL在CLIP和图像奖励分数上均有提升，证明了其能有效进行RL后训练以生成更符合人类偏好的模型。
A Novel Evolutionary Method for Automated Skull-Face Overlay in Computer-Aided Craniofacial Superimposition
Authors: Práxedes Martínez-Moreno, Andrea Valsecchi, Pablo Mesejo, Pilar Navarro-Ramírez, Valentino Lugli, Sergio Damas
First: 2026-02-26T13:55:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T10:19:20+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 6 figures, 3 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Craniofacial Superimposition is a forensic technique for identifying skeletal remains by comparing a post-mortem skull with ante-mortem facial photographs. A critical step in this process is Skull-Face Overlay (SFO). This stage involves aligning a 3D skull model with a 2D facial image, typically guided by cranial and facial landmarks' correspondence. However, its accuracy is undermined by individual variability in soft-tissue thickness, introducing significant uncertainty into the overlay. This paper introduces Lilium, an automated evolutionary method to enhance the accuracy and robustness of SFO. Lilium explicitly models soft-tissue variability using a 3D cone-based representation whose parameters are optimized via a Differential Evolution algorithm. The method enforces anatomical, morphological, and photographic plausibility through a combination of constraints: landmark matching, camera parameter consistency, head pose alignment, skull containment within facial boundaries, and region parallelism. This emulation of the usual forensic practitioners' approach leads Lilium to outperform the state-of-the-art method in terms of both accuracy and robustness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种用于计算机辅助颅面叠加的自动化颅骨-面部覆盖新进化方法
颅面叠加是一种通过比对死后颅骨与生前面部照片来识别骨骼遗骸的法医技术，其关键步骤是颅骨-面部覆盖。该阶段涉及将三维颅骨模型与二维面部图像对齐，通常依据颅骨与面部标志点的对应关系进行。然而，软组织厚度的个体差异会引入显著不确定性，影响覆盖精度。本文提出一种名为Lilium的自动化进化方法，旨在提升SFO的准确性与鲁棒性。Lilium采用基于三维锥体的表征显式建模软组织变异，并通过差分进化算法优化参数。该方法结合多项约束确保解剖、形态与摄影合理性：标志点匹配、相机参数一致性、头部姿态对齐、颅骨位于面部轮廓内以及区域平行性。通过模拟法医实践者的常规操作，Lilium在精度与鲁棒性上均优于当前最优方法。

DeepStage: Learning Autonomous Defense Policies Against Multi-Stage APT Campaigns
Authors: Trung V. Phan, Tri Gia Nguyen, Thomas Bauschert
First: 2026-03-17T09:46:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T09:46:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper presents DeepStage, a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework for adaptive, stage-aware defense against Advanced Persistent Threats (APTs). The enterprise environment is modeled as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP), where host provenance and network telemetry are fused into unified provenance graphs. Building on our prior work, StageFinder, a graph neural encoder and an LSTM-based stage estimator infer probabilistic attacker stages aligned with the MITRE ATT&CK framework. These stage beliefs, combined with graph embeddings, guide a hierarchical Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) agent that selects defense actions across monitoring, access control, containment, and remediation. Evaluated in a realistic enterprise testbed using CALDERA-driven APT playbooks, DeepStage achieves a stage-weighted F1-score of 0.89, outperforming a risk-aware DRL baseline by 21.9%. The results demonstrate effective stage-aware and cost-efficient autonomous cyber defense.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepStage：针对多阶段APT攻击的自适应防御策略学习
本文提出DeepStage，一种基于深度强化学习（DRL）的自适应、阶段感知防御框架，用于应对高级持续性威胁（APT）。企业环境被建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），其中主机溯源数据与网络遥测数据融合为统一的溯源图。基于先前工作StageFinder，图神经编码器与基于LSTM的阶段估计器推断出与MITRE ATT&CK框架对齐的概率性攻击阶段。这些阶段信念与图嵌入相结合，指导分层近端策略优化（PPO）智能体在监控、访问控制、遏制和修复等维度选择防御动作。通过在使用CALDERA驱动的APT攻击剧本的真实企业测试环境中评估，DeepStage实现了0.89的阶段加权F1分数，较风险感知DRL基线提升21.9%。结果表明该框架能实现高效阶段感知且成本优化的自主网络防御。

ERGO: Efficient High-Resolution Visual Understanding for Vision-Language Models
Authors: Jewon Lee, Wooksu Shin, Seungmin Yang, Ki-Ung Song, DongUk Lim, Jaeyeon Kim, Tae-Ho Kim, Bo-Kyeong Kim
First: 2025-09-26T07:15:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T09:34:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Efficient processing of high-resolution images is crucial for real-world vision-language applications. However, existing Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) incur substantial computational overhead due to the large number of vision tokens. With the advent of "thinking with images" models, reasoning now extends beyond text to the visual domain. This capability motivates our two-stage "coarse-to-fine" reasoning pipeline: first, a downsampled image is analyzed to identify task-relevant regions; then, only these regions are cropped at full resolution and processed in a subsequent reasoning stage. This approach reduces computational cost while preserving fine-grained visual details where necessary. A major challenge lies in inferring which regions are truly relevant to a given query. Recent related methods often fail in the first stage after input-image downsampling, due to perception-driven reasoning, where clear visual information is required for effective reasoning. To address this issue, we propose ERGO (Efficient Reasoning & Guided Observation) that performs reasoning-driven perception-leveraging multimodal context to determine where to focus. Our model can account for perceptual uncertainty, expanding the cropped region to cover visually ambiguous areas for answering questions. To this end, we develop simple yet effective reward components in a reinforcement learning framework for coarse-to-fine perception. Across multiple datasets, our approach delivers higher accuracy than the original model and competitive methods, with greater efficiency. For instance, ERGO surpasses Qwen2.5-VL-7B on the V* benchmark by 4.7 points while using only 23% of the vision tokens, achieving a 3x inference speedup. The code and models can be found at: https://github.com/nota-github/ERGO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ERGO：面向视觉语言模型的高效高分辨率视觉理解
高效处理高分辨率图像对现实世界视觉语言应用至关重要。然而，现有大型视觉语言模型因视觉标记数量庞大而产生巨大计算开销。随着“图像思维”模型的出现，推理能力已从文本延伸至视觉领域。该能力催生了我们两阶段“由粗到精”的推理流程：首先分析降采样图像以定位任务相关区域，随后仅对全分辨率裁剪区域进行后续推理。该方法在保留必要细粒度视觉细节的同时降低了计算成本。核心挑战在于推断哪些区域与给定查询真正相关。现有方法常在降采样后的第一阶段因感知驱动推理而失效——有效推理需要清晰的视觉信息。为此，我们提出ERGO（高效推理与引导观察），通过推理驱动的感知机制利用多模态上下文确定关注区域。该模型能处理感知不确定性，扩展裁剪区域以覆盖视觉模糊区域来回答问题。我们为此在强化学习框架中设计了简洁高效的奖励组件，用于实现由粗到精的感知。在多个数据集上，本方法以更高效率实现了优于原模型及竞争方法的准确率。例如，ERGO在V*基准测试中仅使用23%的视觉标记即超越Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型4.7分，推理速度提升3倍。代码与模型详见：https://github.com/nota-github/ERGO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high computational cost of processing high-resolution images in large vision-language models (LVLMs) by introducing ERGO, a two-stage coarse-to-fine reasoning pipeline. The motivation is to reduce the number of vision tokens needed while preserving fine details, overcoming the limitation of existing methods that often fail at the initial downsampling stage due to perception-driven reasoning. The method employs reasoning-driven perception, using multimodal context to identify and crop only task-relevant regions at full resolution, and incorporates reinforcement learning with reward components to handle perceptual uncertainty by expanding cropped areas when needed. Experimental results show that ERGO achieves higher accuracy than baseline models like Qwen2.5-VL-7B and competitive methods across multiple datasets, with significant efficiency gains, such as a 4.7-point improvement on the V* benchmark while using only 23% of vision tokens and achieving a 3x inference speedup.
本文针对大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）处理高分辨率图像时计算成本高的问题，提出了ERGO，一种两阶段的从粗到细推理流程。其动机是在保留必要细节的同时减少视觉令牌数量，克服现有方法因感知驱动推理而在初始下采样阶段失效的局限。该方法采用推理驱动的感知，利用多模态上下文识别并仅裁剪任务相关区域进行全分辨率处理，并通过强化学习中的奖励组件处理感知不确定性，在需要时扩展裁剪区域以覆盖视觉模糊区域。实验结果表明，ERGO在多个数据集上比基线模型（如Qwen2.5-VL-7B）和竞争方法获得更高准确率，且效率显著提升，例如在V*基准上提升4.7分，仅使用23%的视觉令牌，并实现3倍推理加速。
A Survey of Reinforcement Learning For Economics
Authors: Pranjal Rawat
First: 2026-03-09T21:43:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:31:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This survey (re)introduces reinforcement learning methods to economists. The curse of dimensionality limits how far exact dynamic programming can be effectively applied, forcing us to rely on suitably "small" problems or our ability to convert "big" problems into smaller ones. While this reduction has been sufficient for many classical applications, a growing class of economic models resists such reduction. Reinforcement learning algorithms offer a natural, sample-based extension of dynamic programming, extending tractability to problems with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions. I review the theory connecting classical planning to modern learning algorithms and demonstrate their mechanics through simulated examples in pricing, inventory control, strategic games, and preference elicitation. I also examine the practical vulnerabilities of these algorithms, noting their brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and the absence of global convergence guarantees outside of tabular settings. The successes of reinforcement learning remain strictly bounded by these constraints, as well as a reliance on accurate simulators. When guided by economic structure, reinforcement learning provides a remarkably flexible framework. It stands as an imperfect, but promising, addition to the computational economist's toolkit. A companion survey (Rust and Rawat, 2026b) covers the inverse problem of inferring preferences from observed behavior. All simulation code is publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在经济学中的应用综述
本综述（重新）向经济学家介绍了强化学习方法。维度灾难限制了精确动态规划的有效应用范围，迫使我们依赖适当的“小”问题或将“大”问题转化为较小问题的能力。虽然这种简化对许多经典应用已足够，但越来越多的经济模型难以进行此类简化。强化学习算法作为动态规划的自然样本扩展，将可处理性延伸至高维状态、连续动作和策略交互问题。本文回顾了连接经典规划与现代学习算法的理论，并通过定价、库存控制、策略博弈和偏好诱导的模拟示例展示其机制。同时分析了这些算法的实际脆弱性，包括其脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数的敏感性，以及在非表格化场景中缺乏全局收敛保证。强化学习的成功仍严格受限于这些约束以及对精确模拟器的依赖。当结合经济结构指导时，强化学习提供了一个极具灵活性的框架，虽不完美但前景可期，是计算经济学家工具箱的重要补充。配套综述（Rust与Rawat，2026b）涵盖了从观测行为推断偏好的逆问题。所有模拟代码均已公开。
Summary / 总结
This survey aims to introduce reinforcement learning (RL) to economists as a tool to overcome the curse of dimensionality that limits classical dynamic programming, particularly for economic models with high-dimensional states, continuous actions, and strategic interactions that resist simplification. The method involves reviewing the theoretical connections between classical planning and modern RL algorithms and demonstrating their application through simulated examples in areas like pricing, inventory control, and strategic games. Key experimental insights from these simulations highlight RL's flexibility when guided by economic structure, but also reveal practical vulnerabilities such as brittleness, sample inefficiency, sensitivity to hyperparameters, and a reliance on accurate simulators, which bound its successes outside of tabular settings.
本综述旨在向经济学家介绍强化学习方法，以解决经典动态规划因维度诅咒而受限的问题，特别是对于那些难以简化、具有高维状态、连续动作和策略互动的经济模型。方法包括回顾经典规划与现代强化学习算法的理论联系，并通过定价、库存控制和策略博弈等模拟示例展示其应用机制。这些模拟的主要结果表明，在结合经济结构时，强化学习提供了一个高度灵活的框架，但也暴露出实际弱点，如脆弱性、样本效率低下、对超参数敏感以及依赖精确模拟器，这些因素限制了其在非表格化设置中的成功应用。
Amnesia: Adversarial Semantic Layer Specific Activation Steering in Large Language Models
Authors: Ali Raza, Gurang Gupta, Nikolay Matyunin, Jibesh Patra
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:26:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Warning: This article includes red-teaming experiments, which contain examples of compromised LLM responses that may be offensive or upsetting. Large Language Models (LLMs) have the potential to create harmful content, such as generating sophisticated phishing emails and assisting in writing code of harmful computer viruses. Thus, it is crucial to ensure their safe and responsible response generation. To reduce the risk of generating harmful or irresponsible content, researchers have developed techniques such as reinforcement learning with human feedback to align LLM's outputs with human values and preferences. However, it is still undetermined whether such measures are sufficient to prevent LLMs from generating interesting responses. In this study, we propose Amnesia, a lightweight activation-space adversarial attack that manipulates internal transformer states to bypass existing safety mechanisms in open-weight LLMs. Through experimental analysis on state-of-the-art, open-weight LLMs, we demonstrate that our attack effectively circumvents existing safeguards, enabling the generation of harmful content without the need for any fine-tuning or additional training. Our experiments on benchmark datasets show that the proposed attack can induce various antisocial behaviors in LLMs. These findings highlight the urgent need for more robust security measures in open-weight LLMs and underscore the importance of continued research to prevent their potential misuse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：遗忘症：大语言模型中的对抗性语义层特定激活引导
警告：本文包含红队测试实验，其中包含可能具有冒犯性或令人不安的受损大语言模型响应示例。大语言模型（LLMs）具有生成有害内容的潜力，例如制作复杂的钓鱼邮件和协助编写有害计算机病毒代码。因此，确保其生成安全且负责任的响应至关重要。为降低生成有害或不负责内容的风险，研究人员已开发出如基于人类反馈的强化学习等技术，以使LLM输出与人类价值观和偏好保持一致。然而，此类措施是否足以防止LLM生成有害响应仍不确定。本研究提出“遗忘症”，一种轻量级的激活空间对抗攻击方法，通过操纵内部Transformer状态来绕过开源权重LLMs中的现有安全机制。通过对先进开源权重LLMs的实验分析，我们证明该攻击能有效规避现有防护措施，无需任何微调或额外训练即可生成有害内容。在基准数据集上的实验表明，所提攻击可诱导LLMs产生多种反社会行为。这些发现凸显了开源权重LLMs对更鲁棒安全措施的迫切需求，并强调了持续研究以防止其潜在滥用的重要性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to assess the robustness of safety mechanisms in large language models (LLMs), which are aligned to prevent harmful content generation but may still be vulnerable. The authors propose Amnesia, a method that performs adversarial activation steering within specific transformer layers to manipulate the model's internal states, thereby bypassing existing safeguards without requiring fine-tuning. Experimental results on open-weight LLMs demonstrate that this attack effectively induces antisocial behaviors and generates harmful content, highlighting significant vulnerabilities and underscoring the necessity for more robust security measures.
本文的动机源于评估大型语言模型（LLMs）安全机制的鲁棒性需求，这些机制虽经对齐以阻止有害内容生成，但仍可能存在漏洞。作者提出了Amnesia方法，通过在特定Transformer层中进行对抗性激活引导来操纵模型的内部状态，从而无需微调即可绕过现有安全防护。在开源权重的LLMs上的实验结果表明，该攻击能有效诱导反社会行为并生成有害内容，揭示了显著的安全脆弱性，强调了开发更强大防护措施的紧迫性。
A Survey of Frontiers in LLM Reasoning: Inference Scaling, Learning to Reason, and Agentic Systems
Authors: Zixuan Ke, Fangkai Jiao, Yifei Ming, Xuan-Phi Nguyen, Austin Xu, Do Xuan Long, Minzhi Li, Chengwei Qin, Peifeng Wang, Silvio Savarese, Caiming Xiong, Shafiq Joty
First: 2025-04-12T01:27:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T08:09:31+00:00
Comments: 72 pages, 6 figures. Accepted to TMLR, with Survey Certification award
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reasoning is a fundamental cognitive process that enables logical inference, problem-solving, and decision-making. With the rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs), reasoning has emerged as a key capability that distinguishes advanced AI systems from conventional models that empower chatbots. In this survey, we categorize existing methods along two orthogonal dimensions: (1) Regimes, which define the stage at which reasoning is achieved (either at inference time or through dedicated training); and (2) Architectures, which determine the components involved in the reasoning process, distinguishing between standalone LLMs and agentic compound systems that incorporate external tools, and multi-agent collaborations. Within each dimension, we analyze two key perspectives: (1) Input level, which focuses on techniques that construct high-quality prompts that the LLM condition on; and (2) Output level, which methods that refine multiple sampled candidates to enhance reasoning quality. This categorization provides a systematic understanding of the evolving landscape of LLM reasoning, highlighting emerging trends such as the shift from inference-scaling to learning-to-reason (e.g., DeepSeek-R1), and the transition to agentic workflows (e.g., OpenAI Deep Research, Manus Agent). Additionally, we cover a broad spectrum of learning algorithms, from supervised fine-tuning to reinforcement learning such as PPO and GRPO, and the training of reasoners and verifiers. We also examine key designs of agentic workflows, from established patterns like generator-evaluator and LLM debate to recent innovations. ...
