标题：大语言模型推理前沿综述：推理扩展、学习推理与智能体系统
推理是实现逻辑推断、问题解决与决策制定的基础认知过程。随着大语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展，推理已成为区分先进人工智能系统与赋能聊天机器人的传统模型的关键能力。本综述沿两个正交维度对现有方法进行分类：（1）范式——定义实现推理的阶段（在推理时或通过专门训练）；（2）架构——确定推理过程涉及的组件，区分独立LLM与整合外部工具的智能体复合系统及多智能体协作。在每个维度内，我们分析两个关键视角：（1）输入层面——聚焦于构建高质量提示词的技术；（2）输出层面——通过优化多个采样候选结果以提升推理质量的方法。该分类体系为理解LLM推理的发展格局提供了系统性框架，揭示了从推理扩展向学习推理（如DeepSeek-R1）的转变、向智能体工作流（如OpenAI深度研究、Manus Agent）的过渡等新兴趋势。此外，我们涵盖了从监督微调到强化学习（如PPO、GRPO）的广泛学习算法，以及推理器与验证器的训练。我们还探讨了智能体工作流的关键设计，从生成器-评估器、LLM辩论等成熟模式到近期创新。...
Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the need to systematically categorize and understand the rapidly evolving landscape of reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs), which is a key differentiator for advanced AI. The method involves organizing existing approaches along two orthogonal dimensions: Regimes (reasoning at inference time vs. through dedicated training) and Architectures (standalone LLMs vs. agentic systems with tools or multi-agent collaboration), further analyzed through input-level (prompt construction) and output-level (candidate refinement) perspectives. The main experimental results and analysis highlight emerging trends, such as the shift from inference-scaling techniques to learning-to-reason methods like DeepSeek-R1, and the transition towards agentic workflows exemplified by systems such as OpenAI Deep Research, while also covering a broad spectrum of associated learning algorithms and workflow designs.
本综述论文的动机是，需要对大语言模型（LLM）中快速发展的推理能力进行系统分类和理解，这是高级人工智能的关键区别特征。其方法是将现有方法沿两个正交维度进行组织：范式（在推理时实现推理与通过专门训练实现推理）和架构（独立的大语言模型与包含外部工具或多智能体协作的智能复合系统），并进一步通过输入层（提示构建）和输出层（候选结果精炼）的视角进行分析。主要的实验结果和分析强调了新兴趋势，例如从推理缩放技术向学习推理方法（如DeepSeek-R1）的转变，以及向智能体工作流（如OpenAI Deep Research、Manus Agent所例证）的过渡，同时还涵盖了广泛的相关学习算法和工作流设计。
Dual Consensus: Escaping from Spurious Majority in Unsupervised RLVR via Two-Stage Vote Mechanism
Authors: Kaixuan Du, Meng Cao, Hang Zhang, Yukun Wang, Xiangzhou Huang, Ni Li
First: 2026-03-17T07:57:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:57:23+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current label-free RLVR approaches for large language models (LLMs), such as TTRL and Self-reward, have demonstrated effectiveness in improving the performance of LLMs on complex reasoning tasks. However, these methods rely heavily on accurate pseudo-label estimation and converge on spurious yet popular answers, thereby trapping in a dominant mode and limiting further improvements. Building on this, we propose Dual Consensus Reinforcement Learning (DCRL), a novel self-supervised training method which is capable of generating more reliable learning signals through a two-stage consensus mechanism. The model initially acts as an anchor, producing dominant responses; then it serves as an explorer, generating diverse auxiliary signals via a temporary unlearning process. The final training target is derived from the harmonic mean of these two signal sets. Notably, the process operates entirely without external models or supervision. Across eight benchmarks and diverse domains, DCRL consistently improves Pass@1 over majority vote while yielding more stable training dynamics. These results demonstrate that DCRL establishes a scalable path toward stronger reasoning without labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双重共识：通过两阶段投票机制在无监督RLVR中摆脱伪多数陷阱
当前针对大语言模型的无标签RLVR方法（如TTRL和Self-reward）已证明能有效提升模型在复杂推理任务上的性能。然而，这些方法严重依赖准确的伪标签估计，且易收敛于虚假但流行的答案，从而陷入主导模式并限制进一步改进。基于此，我们提出双重共识强化学习，这是一种新颖的自监督训练方法，通过两阶段共识机制生成更可靠的学习信号。模型首先作为锚点生成主导响应，随后作为探索者通过临时遗忘过程产生多样化的辅助信号。最终训练目标源自这两组信号的调和平均数。值得注意的是，该过程完全无需外部模型或监督。在八个基准测试和多个领域中，DCRL始终在Pass@1指标上优于多数投票法，同时展现出更稳定的训练动态。这些结果表明，DCRL为无需标签的更强推理能力建立了可扩展的路径。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing unsupervised RLVR methods, which often converge on spurious majority answers due to reliance on pseudo-label estimation, thereby limiting further performance gains. The proposed method, Dual Consensus Reinforcement Learning (DCRL), introduces a two-stage consensus mechanism where the model first acts as an anchor to produce dominant responses and then as an explorer to generate diverse auxiliary signals via temporary unlearning, with the final training target derived from the harmonic mean of these signals. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that DCRL consistently improves Pass@1 over majority vote baselines and yields more stable training dynamics, demonstrating its effectiveness in enhancing reasoning without external supervision.
本研究的动机是解决现有无监督RLVR方法的局限性，这些方法因依赖伪标签估计而常收敛于虚假多数答案，从而限制了性能的进一步提升。所提出的方法——双重共识强化学习（DCRL），引入了一个两阶段共识机制：模型首先作为锚点生成主导响应，然后作为探索者通过临时遗忘过程产生多样化的辅助信号，最终训练目标源自这些信号的调和平均值。在八个基准测试上的实验结果表明，DCRL在多数投票基线基础上持续提高了Pass@1指标，并带来了更稳定的训练动态，证明了其在无需外部监督下增强推理能力的有效性。
Offline Exploration-Aware Fine-Tuning for Long-Chain Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Yongyu Mu, Jiali Zeng, Fandong Meng, JingBo Zhu, Tong Xiao
First: 2026-03-17T07:36:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:36:29+00:00
Comments: Working in process
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Through encouraging self-exploration, reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the mathematical reasoning capabilities of large language models. As the starting point for RLVR, the capacity of supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to memorize new chain-of-thought trajectories provides a crucial initialization that shapes the subsequent exploration landscape. However, existing research primarily focuses on facilitating exploration during RLVR training, leaving exploration-aware SFT under-explored. To bridge this gap, we propose Offline eXploration-Aware (OXA) fine-tuning. Specifically, OXA optimizes two objectives: promoting low-confidence verified teacher-distillation data to internalize previously uncaptured reasoning patterns, and suppressing high-confidence incorrect self-distillation data to redistribute probability mass of incorrect patterns toward potentially correct candidates. Experimental results across 6 benchmarks show that OXA consistently improves mathematical reasoning performance, especially achieving an average gain of $+6$ Pass@1 and $+5$ Pass@$k$ points compared to conventional SFT on the Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math. Crucially, OXA elevates initial policy entropy, and performance gains persist throughout extensive RLVR training, demonstrating the long-term value of OXA.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向长链数学推理的离线探索感知微调
通过鼓励自我探索，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大型语言模型的数学推理能力。作为RLVR的起点，监督微调（SFT）记忆新思维链轨迹的能力提供了关键初始化，塑造了后续的探索空间。然而，现有研究主要聚焦于促进RLVR训练期间的探索，对探索感知的SFT研究不足。为填补这一空白，我们提出离线探索感知（OXA）微调。具体而言，OXA优化两个目标：促进低置信度已验证教师蒸馏数据以内化先前未捕获的推理模式，并抑制高置信度错误自蒸馏数据以将错误模式的概率质量重新分配给潜在正确候选。在6个基准测试上的实验结果表明，OXA持续提升数学推理性能，尤其在Qwen2.5-1.5B-Math模型上，相比传统SFT平均获得+6 Pass@1和+5 Pass@k的提升。关键的是，OXA提升了初始策略熵，且性能增益在广泛的RLVR训练中持续存在，证明了OXA的长期价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the under-explored problem of making supervised fine-tuning (SFT) more exploration-aware to better initialize models for subsequent reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) in mathematical reasoning. The proposed method, Offline eXploration-Aware (OXA) fine-tuning, optimizes two objectives: promoting low-confidence verified data to internalize new reasoning patterns and suppressing high-confidence incorrect data to redistribute probability mass toward correct candidates. Experimental results on six benchmarks show that OXA consistently improves performance, notably achieving average gains of +6 Pass@1 and +5 Pass@k points over conventional SFT on a 1.5B parameter model, while also increasing initial policy entropy and providing long-term benefits throughout extended RLVR training.
本文针对数学推理任务中，如何使监督微调（SFT）更具探索意识以更好地为后续可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）初始化模型这一未被充分探索的问题展开研究。提出的方法称为离线探索感知（OXA）微调，它优化两个目标：提升低置信度已验证数据以吸收新的推理模式，并抑制高置信度错误数据以将概率质量重新分配给潜在的正确候选。在六个基准测试上的实验结果表明，OXA持续提升了性能，特别是在一个15亿参数模型上，相比传统SFT平均获得了+6 Pass@1和+5 Pass@k的增益，同时提高了初始策略熵，并在长期的RLVR训练中展现出持久的价值。
SAGE: Multi-Agent Self-Evolution for LLM Reasoning
Authors: Yulin Peng, Xinxin Zhu, Chenxing Wei, Nianbo Zeng, Leilei Wang, Ying Tiffany He, F. Richard Yu
First: 2026-03-16T13:24:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:31:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning in large language models (LLMs), but many methods still rely on large human-labeled datasets. While self-play reduces this dependency, it often lacks explicit planning and strong quality control, limiting stability in long-horizon multi-step reasoning. We present SAGE (Self-evolving Agents for Generalized reasoning Evolution), a closed-loop framework where four agents: Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic, co-evolve from a shared LLM backbone using only a small seed set. The Challenger continuously generates increasingly difficult tasks; the Planner converts each task into a structured multi-step plan; and the Solver follows the plan to produce an answer, whose correctness is determined by external verifiers. The Critic scores and filters both generated questions and plans to prevent curriculum drift and maintain training signal quality, enabling stable self-training. Across mathematics and code-generation benchmarks, SAGE delivers consistent gains across model scales, improving the Qwen-2.5-7B model by 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAGE：面向大语言模型推理的多智能体自进化框架
基于可验证奖励的强化学习能提升大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但现有方法仍依赖大规模人工标注数据集。尽管自博弈机制可降低这种依赖，但其常缺乏显式规划和严格的质量控制，限制了长跨度多步推理的稳定性。本文提出SAGE（面向泛化推理进化的自进化智能体框架），这是一个闭环系统：挑战者、规划者、求解者、评判者四个智能体仅基于少量种子数据，从共享的LLM主干网络协同进化。挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务；规划者将任务转化为结构化多步方案；求解者依据方案生成答案，其正确性由外部验证器判定。评判者对生成的问题和方案进行评分筛选，防止课程漂移并维持训练信号质量，从而实现稳定的自训练。在数学与代码生成基准测试中，SAGE在不同规模模型上均取得稳定提升，将Qwen-2.5-7B模型在LiveCodeBench和OlympiadBench上的性能分别提升8.9%和10.7%。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SAGE, a multi-agent self-evolution framework designed to enhance LLM reasoning without extensive human-labeled data, addressing limitations in self-play methods like insufficient planning and quality control. The method employs four co-evolving agents—Challenger, Planner, Solver, and Critic—derived from a shared LLM backbone, where the Challenger generates progressively harder tasks, the Planner creates structured multi-step plans, the Solver produces answers verified externally, and the Critic filters content to prevent curriculum drift and ensure training stability. Experimental results show consistent improvements across model scales, with the Qwen-2.5-7B model achieving gains of 8.9% on LiveCodeBench and 10.7% on OlympiadBench in mathematics and code-generation benchmarks.
本文提出了SAGE，一种多智能体自进化框架，旨在无需大量人工标注数据的情况下提升大语言模型的推理能力，以解决自对弈方法中规划不足和质量控制有限等问题。该方法采用源自同一大语言模型骨干的四个协同进化智能体——挑战者、规划者、求解者和评判者，其中挑战者持续生成难度递增的任务，规划者将任务转化为结构化多步计划，求解者遵循计划生成答案并由外部验证器检验正确性，评判者则对生成的问题和计划进行评分过滤以防止课程漂移并维持训练信号质量。实验结果表明，该框架在不同模型规模上均带来稳定提升，Qwen-2.5-7B模型在数学和代码生成基准测试中，于LiveCodeBench和OlympiadBench上分别实现了8.9%和10.7%的性能增益。
APEX-Searcher: Augmenting LLMs' Search Capabilities through Agentic Planning and Execution
Authors: Kun Chen, Qingchao Kong, Zhao Feifei, Wenji Mao
First: 2026-03-14T09:17:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T07:07:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), based on large language models (LLMs), serves as a vital approach to retrieving and leveraging external knowledge in various domain applications. When confronted with complex multi-hop questions, single-round retrieval is often insufficient for accurate reasoning and problem solving. To enhance search capabilities for complex tasks, most existing works integrate multi-round iterative retrieval with reasoning processes via end-to-end training. While these approaches significantly improve problem-solving performance, they are still faced with challenges in task reasoning and model training, especially ambiguous retrieval execution paths and sparse rewards in end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) process, leading to inaccurate retrieval results and performance degradation. To address these issues, in this paper, we proposes APEX-Searcher, a novel Agentic Planning and Execution framework to augment LLM search capabilities. Specifically, we introduce a two-stage agentic framework that decouples the retrieval process into planning and execution: It first employs RL with decomposition-specific rewards to optimize strategic planning; Built on the sub-task decomposition, it then applies supervised fine-tuning on high-quality multi-hop trajectories to equip the model with robust iterative sub-task execution capabilities. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our proposed framework achieves significant improvements in both multi-hop RAG and task planning performances across multiple benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：APEX-Searcher：通过智能体规划与执行增强大语言模型的搜索能力
基于大语言模型的检索增强生成技术是各领域应用中获取并利用外部知识的重要方法。面对复杂的多跳问题时，单轮检索往往难以支撑精确推理与问题求解。为提升复杂任务的搜索能力，现有研究多通过端到端训练将多轮迭代检索与推理过程相结合。这些方法虽显著提升了问题解决性能，但在任务推理与模型训练方面仍面临挑战，特别是检索执行路径的模糊性以及端到端强化学习过程中的稀疏奖励问题，导致检索结果不准确与性能下降。为此，本文提出APEX-Searcher——一种增强大语言模型搜索能力的新型智能体规划与执行框架。该框架采用两阶段智能体架构，将检索过程解耦为规划与执行：首先通过配备分解专项奖励的强化学习优化策略规划；基于子任务分解，再对高质量多跳轨迹进行监督微调，使模型具备稳健的迭代子任务执行能力。大量实验表明，所提框架在多个基准测试的多跳检索增强生成与任务规划性能上均取得显著提升。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enhance large language models' (LLMs) search capabilities for complex multi-hop questions, where single-round retrieval in retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) often fails, and existing multi-round approaches suffer from ambiguous retrieval paths and sparse rewards in end-to-end reinforcement learning. The method introduces APEX-Searcher, a novel agentic framework that decouples retrieval into two stages: first, it uses reinforcement learning with decomposition-specific rewards to optimize strategic planning for sub-task decomposition, and second, it applies supervised fine-tuning on high-quality trajectories to equip the model with robust iterative execution capabilities. The main experimental results show that this framework achieves significant improvements in multi-hop RAG and task planning performances across multiple benchmarks.
本研究的动机是增强大语言模型（LLMs）在复杂多跳问题上的搜索能力，因为检索增强生成（RAG）中的单轮检索往往不足，而现有的多轮方法存在检索路径模糊和端到端强化学习中奖励稀疏的问题。方法上提出了APEX-Searcher，一种新颖的智能体规划与执行框架，将检索过程解耦为两个阶段：首先，使用带有分解特定奖励的强化学习来优化子任务分解的战略规划；其次，基于子任务分解，对高质量多跳轨迹进行监督微调，以赋予模型强大的迭代子任务执行能力。主要实验结果表明，该框架在多个基准测试中显著提升了多跳RAG和任务规划的性能。
SQL-ASTRA: Alleviating Sparse Feedback in Agentic SQL via Column-Set Matching and Trajectory Aggregation
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Jiangxuan Long, Peiyang Liu, Weidi Xu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu
First: 2026-03-17T06:26:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:26:36+00:00
Comments: 17 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic Reinforcement Learning (RL) shows promise for complex tasks, but Text-to-SQL remains mostly restricted to single-turn paradigms. A primary bottleneck is the credit assignment problem. In traditional paradigms, rewards are determined solely by the final-turn feedback, which ignores the intermediate process and leads to ambiguous credit evaluation. To address this, we propose Agentic SQL, a framework featuring a universal two-tiered reward mechanism designed to provide effective trajectory-level evaluation and dense step-level signals. First, we introduce Aggregated Trajectory Reward (ATR) to resolve multi-turn credit assignment. Using an asymmetric transition matrix, ATR aggregates process-oriented scores to incentivize continuous improvement. Leveraging Lyapunov stability theory, we prove ATR acts as an energy dissipation operator, guaranteeing a cycle-free policy and monotonic convergence. Second, Column-Set Matching Reward (CSMR) provides immediate step-level rewards to mitigate sparsity. By executing queries at each turn, CSMR converts binary (0/1) feedback into dense [0, 1] signals based on partial correctness. Evaluations on BIRD show a 5% gain over binary-reward GRPO. Notably, our approach outperforms SOTA Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B on BIRD and Spider 2.0 using identical models, propelling Text-to-SQL toward a robust multi-turn agent paradigm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SQL-ASTRA：通过列集匹配与轨迹聚合缓解智能体SQL中的稀疏反馈问题
智能体强化学习在复杂任务中展现出潜力，但文本到SQL领域仍主要局限于单轮范式。核心瓶颈在于信用分配问题：传统范式仅依据最终轮次反馈确定奖励，忽略中间过程并导致信用评估模糊。为此，我们提出智能体SQL框架，采用通用双层奖励机制，提供有效的轨迹级评估与密集的步骤级信号。首先，引入聚合轨迹奖励（ATR）解决多轮信用分配问题，通过非对称转移矩阵聚合过程导向分数以激励持续改进。基于李雅普诺夫稳定性理论，我们证明ATR可作为能量耗散算子，确保无循环策略与单调收敛。其次，列集匹配奖励（CSMR）提供即时步骤级奖励以缓解稀疏性，通过每轮执行查询将二元（0/1）反馈转换为基于部分正确性的密集[0,1]信号。在BIRD数据集上的评估显示，本方法较二元奖励GRPO提升5%。值得注意的是，使用相同模型时，我们的方法在BIRD和Spider 2.0数据集上均优于当前最优的Arctic-Text2SQL-R1-7B模型，推动文本到SQL向鲁棒的多轮智能体范式迈进。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the credit assignment problem in agentic reinforcement learning for multi-turn Text-to-SQL, where sparse binary feedback from final-turn evaluation hampers learning. To alleviate this, the authors propose SQL-ASTRA, a framework with a two-tiered reward mechanism: an Aggregated Trajectory Reward (ATR) that uses an asymmetric transition matrix to provide trajectory-level evaluation and ensure monotonic convergence via Lyapunov stability theory, and a Column-Set Matching Reward (CSMR) that offers dense step-level rewards by assessing partial correctness of queries at each turn. Experimental results on the BIRD benchmark show a 5% improvement over binary-reward GRPO and state-of-the-art performance on BIRD and Spider 2.0, even with identical models, advancing Text-to-SQL toward robust multi-turn agentic paradigms.
本文针对多轮Text-to-SQL中智能体强化学习的信用分配问题，其中仅依赖最终轮次二元反馈的稀疏奖励会阻碍学习。为缓解此问题，作者提出了SQL-ASTRA框架，采用双层奖励机制：聚合轨迹奖励（ATR）利用非对称转移矩阵提供轨迹级评估，并通过李雅普诺夫稳定性理论确保单调收敛；列集匹配奖励（CSMR）则通过每轮查询的部分正确性评估，提供密集的步骤级奖励。在BIRD基准上的实验结果表明，该方法比二元奖励的GRPO提升了5%，并在BIRD和Spider 2.0上取得了最先进的性能，即使使用相同模型，也推动了Text-to-SQL向鲁棒的多轮智能体范式发展。
Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment for GRPO in Code Generation
Authors: Abhijit Kumar, Natalya Kumar, Shikhar Gupta
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-17T06:22:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:22:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted at SPOT ICLR 2026 (https://openreview.net/forum?id=nqkVB5EVXJ)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Critic-free reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves code generation by optimizing unit-test pass rates, but GRPO-style updates suffer from coarse credit assignment: a single outcome signal is spread uniformly across long programs even when failure stems from a localized semantic error. We propose Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment (EGCA), which localizes GRPO updates using execution traces. For programs that satisfy algorithmic constraints but fail tests, EGCA executes the candidate and a canonical reference solution (curated once offline; used for analysis, not supervision) under identical instrumentation, identifies the earliest semantic divergence, and assigns advantage only to the corresponding token span while masking downstream tokens. EGCA is a drop-in modification requiring no critic, auxiliary loss, or learned verifier, yielding 82.1% pass@1 on HumanEval (+3.1 over GRPO) and 68.9% on MBPP (+1.5) with 18% wall-clock overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向代码生成中GRPO的执行溯源信用分配方法
基于可验证奖励的无评论家强化学习通过优化单元测试通过率改进代码生成，但GRPO式更新存在信用分配粗糙的问题：即使失败源于局部语义错误，单一结果信号仍被均匀分配至长程序中。我们提出执行溯源信用分配方法，利用执行轨迹定位GRPO更新。对于满足算法约束但测试失败的程序，EGCA在相同插桩环境下执行候选程序与规范参考解（离线一次性构建，仅用于分析而非监督），识别最早的语义分歧点，仅对相应词元区间分配优势值并掩码后续词元。EGCA作为即插即用改进方案，无需评论家网络、辅助损失或学习型验证器，在HumanEval上实现82.1%的pass@1（较GRPO提升3.1），在MBPP上达68.9%（提升1.5），仅产生18%的额外计算开销。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the coarse credit assignment problem in critic-free reinforcement learning for code generation, where uniform reward distribution across long programs fails to localize semantic errors. The proposed Execution-Grounded Credit Assignment (EGCA) method improves GRPO-style updates by using execution traces: it compares a candidate program with a canonical reference solution under identical instrumentation to identify the earliest semantic divergence and assigns advantage only to the relevant token span, masking downstream tokens. Experimental results show that EGCA, as a drop-in modification without additional critics or losses, achieves 82.1% pass@1 on HumanEval (a 3.1% improvement over GRPO) and 68.9% on MBPP (a 1.5% improvement) with only 18% wall-clock overhead.
本文针对代码生成中无评论者强化学习的粗粒度信用分配问题提出改进，传统方法将奖励均匀分配给长程序而无法定位语义错误。提出的执行基础信用分配方法通过执行轨迹优化GRPO更新：在相同工具下比较候选程序与规范参考解决方案，识别最早的语义分歧，仅将优势分配给对应词元片段并屏蔽后续词元。实验结果表明，该方法作为无需额外评论者或损失的即插即用修改，在HumanEval上达到82.1%的pass@1（较GRPO提升3.1%），在MBPP上达到68.9%（提升1.5%），仅增加18%的时钟开销。
DyJR: Preserving Diversity in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards via Dynamic Jensen-Shannon Replay
Authors: Long Li, Zhijian Zhou, Tianyi Wang, Weidi Xu, Zuming Huang, Wei Chu, Zhe Wang, Shirui Pan, Chao Qu, Yuan Qi
First: 2026-03-17T06:20:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:20:56+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning (RL) enhances Large Language Model reasoning, on-policy algorithms like GRPO are sample-inefficient as they discard past rollouts. Existing experience replay methods address this by reusing accurate samples for direct policy updates, but this often incurs high computational costs and causes mode collapse via overfitting. We argue that historical data should prioritize sustaining diversity rather than simply reinforcing accuracy. To this end, we propose Dynamic Jensen-Shannon Replay (DyJR), a simple yet effective regularization framework using a dynamic reference distribution from recent trajectories. DyJR introduces two innovations: (1) A Time-Sensitive Dynamic Buffer that uses FIFO and adaptive sizing to retain only temporally proximal samples, synchronizing with model evolution; and (2) Jensen-Shannon Divergence Regularization, which replaces direct gradient updates with a distributional constraint to prevent diversity collapse. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and Text-to-SQL benchmarks demonstrate that DyJR significantly outperforms GRPO as well as baselines such as RLEP and Ex-GRPO, while maintaining training efficiency comparable to the original GRPO. Furthermore, from the perspective of Rank-$k$ token probability evolution, we show that DyJR enhances diversity and mitigates over-reliance on Rank-1 tokens, elucidating how specific sub-modules of DyJR influence the training dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DyJR：通过动态Jensen-Shannon回放实现可验证奖励的强化学习多样性保持
尽管强化学习（RL）能增强大语言模型的推理能力，但如GRPO等在线策略算法因丢弃历史轨迹而样本效率低下。现有经验回放方法通过重用精确样本直接更新策略来解决此问题，但这通常带来高计算成本，并因过拟合导致模式崩溃。我们认为历史数据应优先维持多样性而非单纯强化精确性。为此，我们提出动态Jensen-Shannon回放（DyJR），这是一个简单而有效的正则化框架，利用近期轨迹的动态参考分布。DyJR引入两项创新：（1）时间敏感动态缓冲区，采用FIFO和自适应大小机制，仅保留时间邻近样本，与模型演化同步；（2）Jensen-Shannon散度正则化，用分布约束替代直接梯度更新，防止多样性崩溃。在数学推理和Text-to-SQL基准测试上的实验表明，DyJR显著优于GRPO及RLEP、Ex-GRPO等基线方法，同时保持与原始GRPO相当的训练效率。此外，从Rank-$k$词元概率演化的视角，我们证明DyJR能增强多样性并缓解对Rank-1词元的过度依赖，阐明了DyJR特定子模块如何影响训练动态。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the sample inefficiency of on-policy reinforcement learning for language models, where discarding past rollouts wastes data and existing replay methods risk computational cost and mode collapse from overfitting on accurate samples. The proposed method, Dynamic Jensen-Shannon Replay (DyJR), introduces a regularization framework using a dynamic reference distribution from recent trajectories, featuring a time-sensitive dynamic buffer for temporally proximal samples and Jensen-Shannon divergence regularization to impose distributional constraints instead of direct gradient updates. HIPO: Instruction Hierarchy via Constrained Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Keru Chen, Jun Luo, Sen Lin, Yingbin Liang, Alvaro Velasquez, Nathaniel Bastian, Shaofeng Zou
First: 2026-03-17T06:12:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T06:12:41+00:00
Comments: 9 pages + appendix. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical Instruction Following (HIF) refers to the problem of prompting large language models with a priority-ordered stack of instructions. Standard methods like RLHF and DPO typically fail in this problem since they mainly optimize for a single objective, failing to explicitly enforce system prompt compliance. Meanwhile, supervised fine-tuning relies on mimicking filtered, compliant data, which fails to establish the priority asymmetry at the algorithmic level. In this paper, we introduce \textsc{HIPO}, a novel alignment framework that formulates HIF as a Constrained Markov Decision Process. \textsc{HIPO} elevates system prompts from mere input context to strict algorithmic boundaries. Using a primal-dual safe reinforcement learning approach, the algorithm dynamically enforces system prompt compliance as an explicit constraint, maximizing user utility strictly within this feasible region. Extensive evaluations across diverse model architectures (e.g., Qwen, Phi, Llama) demonstrate that \textsc{HIPO} significantly improves both system compliance and user utility. Furthermore, mechanistic analysis reveals that this constrained optimization autonomously drives the model to shift its attention toward long-range system tokens, providing a principled foundation for reliable LLM deployment in complex workflows.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HIPO：基于约束强化学习的指令层次化方法
层次化指令跟随（HIF）指通过优先级排序的指令栈来提示大语言模型的问题。RLHF和DPO等标准方法通常在此问题上失效，因其主要优化单一目标，未能显式强制系统提示的遵从性。同时，监督微调依赖模仿经过筛选的合规数据，无法在算法层面建立优先级不对称性。本文提出HIPO，一种将HIF建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程的新型对齐框架。HIPO将系统提示从单纯的输入上下文提升为严格的算法边界。通过原对偶安全强化学习方法，该算法将系统提示遵从性作为显式约束动态执行，严格在可行域内最大化用户效用。跨多种模型架构（如Qwen、Phi、Llama）的广泛评估表明，HIPO显著提升了系统遵从性与用户效用。机制分析进一步揭示，这种约束优化能自主驱动模型将注意力转向长程系统标记，为复杂工作流中可靠部署大语言模型提供了原理性基础。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces HIPO, a novel alignment framework motivated by the challenge of Hierarchical Instruction Following (HIF), where large language models must prioritize a stack of instructions. Standard methods like RLHF and DPO often fail to enforce system prompt compliance or establish priority asymmetry. HIPO formulates HIF as a Constrained Markov Decision Process, using a primal-dual safe reinforcement learning approach to dynamically enforce system prompts as strict constraints while maximizing user utility within that region. Experimental results across models such as Qwen, Phi, and Llama show that HIPO significantly improves both system compliance and user utility, with mechanistic analysis indicating it shifts model attention toward long-range system tokens for more reliable deployment.
本文提出了HIPO这一新颖的对齐框架，其动机是解决分层指令跟随问题，即大语言模型需要优先处理一组有序指令。传统方法如RLHF和DPO通常无法强制系统提示的遵从性或建立优先级不对称性。HIPO将分层指令跟随建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程，采用原始-对偶安全强化学习方法，动态地将系统提示作为严格约束强制执行，同时在该可行区域内最大化用户效用。在Qwen、Phi、Llama等多种模型上的广泛评估表明，HIPO显著提升了系统遵从性和用户效用；机制分析进一步揭示，这种约束优化能自主驱动模型将注意力转向长距离系统标记，为复杂工作流中的可靠部署提供了原理性基础。
Communication-Aware Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Decentralized Cooperative UAV Deployment
Authors: Enguang Fan, Yifan Chen, Zihan Shan, Matthew Caesar, Jae Kim
First: 2026-03-17T05:48:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:48:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Autonomous Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) swarms are increasingly used as rapidly deployable aerial relays and sensing platforms, yet practical deployments must operate under partial observability and intermittent peer-to-peer links. We present a graph-based multi-agent reinforcement learning framework trained under centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE): a centralized critic and global state are available only during training, while each UAV executes a shared policy using local observations and messages from nearby neighbors. Our architecture encodes local agent state and nearby entities with an agent-entity attention module, and aggregates inter-UAV messages with neighbor self-attention over a distance-limited communication graph. We evaluate primarily on a cooperative relay deployment task (DroneConnect) and secondarily on an adversarial engagement task (DroneCombat). In DroneConnect, the proposed method achieves high coverage under restricted communication and partial observation (e.g. 74% coverage with M = 5 UAVs and N = 10 nodes) while remaining competitive with a mixed-integer linear programming (MILP) optimization-based offline upper bound, and it generalizes to unseen team sizes without fine-tuning. In the adversarial setting, the same framework transfers without architectural changes and improves win rate over non-communicating baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向分散式协同无人机部署的通信感知多智能体强化学习
自主无人机集群正日益被用作快速部署的空中中继与感知平台，但实际部署需在部分可观测性与间歇性点对点链路条件下运行。本文提出一种基于图结构的多智能体强化学习框架，采用集中训练分散执行模式：训练时使用集中式评价器与全局状态，而每架无人机仅基于局部观测与邻近邻居消息执行共享策略。该架构通过智能体-实体注意力模块编码本地状态与邻近实体，并在距离受限的通信图上通过邻居自注意力聚合无人机间消息。主要评估任务为协同中继部署，次要任务为对抗性交战。在中继部署任务中，所提方法在受限通信与部分观测条件下实现高覆盖率，且与基于混合整数线性规划的离线优化上界性能相当，并能泛化至未经微调的新团队规模。在对抗性任务中，相同框架无需结构调整即可迁移，并较无通信基线提升胜率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for autonomous UAV swarms to operate effectively under partial observability and intermittent communication links, this paper proposes a graph-based multi-agent reinforcement learning framework using centralized training with decentralized execution. The method employs an agent-entity attention module to encode local states and nearby entities, along with neighbor self-attention to aggregate messages over a distance-limited communication graph. Experimental results on a cooperative relay deployment task (DroneConnect) show the approach achieves high coverage, such as 74% with 5 UAVs and 10 nodes, remains competitive with an offline MILP upper bound, and generalizes to unseen team sizes without fine-tuning; it also transfers effectively to an adversarial engagement task (DroneCombat), improving win rates over non-communicating baselines.
本文针对无人机集群在部分可观测和间歇性通信链路下的自主部署需求，提出了一种基于图的多智能体强化学习框架，采用集中训练与分散执行的训练范式。该方法通过智能体-实体注意力模块编码局部状态和附近实体，并利用邻居自注意力在距离受限的通信图上聚合消息。在协作中继部署任务（DroneConnect）中的实验结果表明，该方法实现了高覆盖率（例如5架无人机和10个节点时达到74%），与离线混合整数线性规划上界性能相当，且无需微调即可泛化到未见过的团队规模；在对抗性任务（DroneCombat）中，同一框架无需架构修改即可迁移，并相比无通信基线提高了胜率。
Noisy Data is Destructive to Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Yuxuan Zhu, Daniel Kang
First: 2026-03-17T05:48:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:48:32+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has driven recent capability advances of large language models across various domains. Recent studies suggest that improved RLVR algorithms allow models to learn effectively from incorrect annotations, achieving performance comparable to learning from clean data. In this work, we show that these findings are invalid because the claimed 100% noisy training data is "contaminated" with clean data. After rectifying the dataset with a rigorous re-verification pipeline, we demonstrate that noise is destructive to RLVR. We show that existing RLVR algorithm improvements fail to mitigate the impact of noise, achieving similar performance to that of the basic GRPO. Furthermore, we find that the model trained on truly incorrect annotations performs 8-10% worse than the model trained on clean data across mathematical reasoning benchmarks. Finally, we show that these findings hold for real-world noise in Text2SQL tasks, where training on real-world, human annotation errors cause 5-12% lower accuracy than clean data. Our results show that current RLVR methods cannot yet compensate for poor data quality. High-quality data remains essential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：噪声数据对可验证奖励强化学习具有破坏性
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型语言模型在各领域的能力进展。近期研究表明，改进的RLVR算法使模型能从错误标注中有效学习，达到与干净数据相当的性能。本工作指出这些结论无效，因为其所称的100%噪声训练数据实际“掺杂”了干净数据。通过严格的重新验证流程修正数据集后，我们证明噪声对RLVR具有破坏性：现有RLVR算法改进未能缓解噪声影响，其性能与基础GRPO相当；在数学推理基准测试中，使用真实错误标注训练的模型比干净数据训练的模型性能低8-10%；在Text2SQL任务中，使用现实世界人工标注错误训练的数据比干净数据准确率低5-12%。结果表明当前RLVR方法尚无法弥补数据质量缺陷，高质量数据仍至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges prior claims that reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) can effectively learn from noisy data, arguing that earlier studies used datasets inadvertently contaminated with clean examples. The authors introduce a rigorous re-verification pipeline to create truly noisy datasets and demonstrate that noise is highly detrimental to RLVR performance. Their experiments show that existing RLVR algorithm improvements fail to mitigate this effect, performing similarly to basic methods like GRPO, with models trained on verified noisy data underperforming by 8-10% on mathematical reasoning tasks and by 5-12% on real-world Text2SQL tasks compared to clean data. The findings underscore that high-quality data remains essential, as current RLVR methods cannot compensate for poor data quality.
本文质疑了先前关于可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）能从噪声数据中有效学习的观点，指出早期研究使用的数据集无意中混杂了干净样本。作者引入了一个严格的重验证流程来创建真正的噪声数据集，并证明噪声对RLVR性能具有破坏性影响。实验表明，现有的RLVR算法改进无法缓解这种影响，其表现与GRPO等基础方法相似；在数学推理基准测试中，使用验证过的噪声数据训练的模型比使用干净数据的模型性能低8-10%，而在真实世界的Text2SQL任务中，基于人工标注错误训练导致准确率下降5-12%。这些结果强调高质量数据仍然至关重要，因为当前的RLVR方法尚无法弥补数据质量的不足。
SWE-QA-Pro: A Representative Benchmark and Scalable Training Recipe for Repository-Level Code Understanding
Authors: Songcheng Cai, Zhiheng Lyu, Yuansheng Ni, Xiangchao Chen, Baichuan Zhou, Shenzhe Zhu, Yi Lu, Haozhe Wang, Chi Ruan, Benjamin Schneider, Weixu Zhang, Xiang Li, Andy Zheng, Yuyu Zhang, Ping Nie, Wenhu Chen
First: 2026-03-17T05:12:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T05:12:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic repository-level code understanding is essential for automating complex software engineering tasks, yet the field lacks reliable benchmarks. Existing evaluations often overlook the long tail topics and rely on popular repositories where Large Language Models (LLMs) can cheat via memorized knowledge. To address this, we introduce SWE-QA-Pro, a benchmark constructed from diverse, long-tail repositories with executable environments. We enforce topical balance via issue-driven clustering to cover under-represented task types and apply a rigorous difficulty calibration process: questions solvable by direct-answer baselines are filtered out. This results in a dataset where agentic workflows significantly outperform direct answering (e.g., a ~13-point gap for Claude Sonnet 4.5), confirming the necessity of agentic codebase exploration. Furthermore, to tackle the scarcity of training data for such complex behaviors, we propose a scalable synthetic data pipeline that powers a two-stage training recipe: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) followed by Reinforcement Learning from AI Feedback (RLAIF). This approach allows small open models to learn efficient tool usage and reasoning. Empirically, a Qwen3-8B model trained with our recipe surpasses GPT-4o by 2.3 points on SWE-QA-Pro and substantially narrows the gap to state-of-the-art proprietary models, demonstrating both the validity of our evaluation and the effectiveness of our agentic training workflow.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SWE-QA-Pro：面向仓库级代码理解的代表性基准与可扩展训练方案
智能体驱动的仓库级代码理解对自动化复杂软件工程任务至关重要，但该领域缺乏可靠基准。现有评估常忽略长尾主题，并依赖大型语言模型可通过记忆知识作弊的热门仓库。为此，我们推出SWE-QA-Pro——一个基于多样化长尾仓库与可执行环境构建的基准。我们通过议题驱动的聚类确保主题均衡性以覆盖低代表性任务类型，并采用严格的难度校准流程：过滤可直接通过基线模型回答的问题。由此产生的数据集中，智能体工作流显著优于直接回答（如Claude Sonnet 4.5存在约13分差距），证实了智能化代码库探索的必要性。此外，针对此类复杂行为训练数据稀缺的问题，我们提出可扩展的合成数据流水线，支持两阶段训练方案：监督微调后接基于AI反馈的强化学习。该方法使小型开源模型能学习高效工具使用与推理。实证表明，采用本方案训练的Qwen3-8B模型在SWE-QA-Pro上超越GPT-4o达2.3分，并大幅缩小与顶尖专有模型的差距，同时验证了评估体系的有效性与智能体训练流程的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the lack of reliable benchmarks for agentic repository-level code understanding, as existing evaluations often overlook long-tail topics and are vulnerable to LLM memorization. The method introduces SWE-QA-Pro, a benchmark built from diverse, long-tail repositories with executable environments, using issue-driven clustering for topical balance and a difficulty calibration to filter out questions solvable by direct-answer baselines. The main experimental results show that agentic workflows significantly outperform direct answering on this benchmark (e.g., a ~13-point gap for Claude Sonnet 4.5), and a Qwen3-8B model trained with the proposed scalable synthetic data pipeline and two-stage training recipe surpasses GPT-4o by 2.3 points, narrowing the gap to state-of-the-art proprietary models.
本研究的动机在于，面向智能体（agentic）的仓库级代码理解领域缺乏可靠的基准测试，现有评估常忽略长尾主题且易受大语言模型记忆知识的影响。方法上，提出了SWE-QA-Pro基准，该基准构建自多样化的长尾仓库并配备可执行环境，通过问题驱动的聚类确保主题平衡，并采用严格的难度校准过程以过滤可直接回答的问题。主要实验结果表明，在该基准上，智能体工作流显著优于直接回答（例如Claude Sonnet 4.5有约13分的差距），且使用所提出的可扩展合成数据管道和两阶段训练方法（监督微调后接基于AI反馈的强化学习）训练的Qwen3-8B模型，其表现超过GPT-4o达2.3分，大幅缩小了与顶尖专有模型的差距。
Urban Socio-Semantic Segmentation with Vision-Language Reasoning
Authors: Yu Wang, Yi Wang, Rui Dai, Yujie Wang, Kaikui Liu, Xiangxiang Chu, Yansheng Li
First: 2026-01-15T15:00:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T04:11:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As hubs of human activity, urban surfaces consist of a wealth of semantic entities. Segmenting these various entities from satellite imagery is crucial for a range of downstream applications. Current advanced segmentation models can reliably segment entities defined by physical attributes (e.g., buildings, water bodies) but still struggle with socially defined categories (e.g., schools, parks). In this work, we achieve socio-semantic segmentation by vision-language model reasoning. To facilitate this, we introduce the Urban Socio-Semantic Segmentation dataset named SocioSeg, a new resource comprising satellite imagery, digital maps, and pixel-level labels of social semantic entities organized in a hierarchical structure. Additionally, we propose a novel vision-language reasoning framework called SocioReasoner that simulates the human process of identifying and annotating social semantic entities via cross-modal recognition and multi-stage reasoning. We employ reinforcement learning to optimize this non-differentiable process and elicit the reasoning capabilities of the vision-language model. Experiments demonstrate our approach's gains over state-of-the-art models and strong zero-shot generalization. The dataset and code are open-sourced under the Apache License 2.0 at https://github.com/AMAP-ML/SocioReasoner.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于视觉语言推理的城市社会语义分割
作为人类活动的枢纽，城市地表包含丰富的语义实体。从卫星图像中分割这些多样实体对一系列下游应用至关重要。当前先进的语义分割模型能可靠分割由物理属性定义的实体（如建筑、水体），但在处理社会定义类别（如学校、公园）时仍面临挑战。本研究通过视觉语言模型推理实现了社会语义分割。为此，我们构建了名为SocioSeg的城市社会语义分割数据集，该资源包含卫星影像、数字地图及按层级结构组织的社会语义实体像素级标注。同时，我们提出名为SocioReasoner的新型视觉语言推理框架，通过跨模态识别与多阶段推理模拟人类识别标注社会语义实体的认知过程。采用强化学习优化这一不可微分流程，以激发视觉语言模型的推理能力。实验表明，该方法优于当前最优模型，并展现出强大的零样本泛化性能。数据集与代码已在Apache 2.0协议下开源：https://github.com/AMAP-ML/SocioReasoner。

This paper addresses the challenge of segmenting socially defined urban entities, such as schools and parks, from satellite imagery, which existing models struggle with despite being proficient at segmenting physical entities like buildings. The authors introduce a new dataset, SocioSeg, containing satellite images, maps, and hierarchical pixel-level labels for social semantics, and propose a vision-language reasoning framework called SocioReasoner that mimics human annotation through cross-modal recognition and multi-stage reasoning, optimized via reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that this approach outperforms state-of-the-art models and exhibits strong zero-shot generalization capabilities.
本文针对从卫星图像中分割社会定义的城市场景实体（如学校、公园）的挑战，现有模型虽能可靠分割物理实体（如建筑、水体），但仍难以处理此类社会类别。作者引入了包含卫星图像、数字地图和分层像素级标签的新数据集SocioSeg，并提出了一种名为SocioReasoner的视觉语言推理框架，通过跨模态识别和多阶段推理模拟人类标注过程，并使用强化学习优化这一不可微分流程。实验结果表明，该方法优于现有先进模型，并展现出强大的零样本泛化能力。
DRL-Based Beam Positioning for LEO Satellite Constellations with Weighted Least Squares
Authors: Po-Heng Chou, Chiapin Wang, Kuan-Hao Chen, Wei-Chen Hsiao
First: 2025-11-12T00:14:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T04:06:51+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 3 figures, 1 table, accepted by 2026 IEEE ICC Workshops
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates a lightweight deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-assisted weighting framework for CSI-free multi-satellite positioning in LEO constellations, where each visible satellite provides one serving beam (one pilot response) per epoch. A discrete-action Deep Q-Network (DQN) learns satellite weights directly from received pilot measurements and geometric features, while an augmented weighted least squares (WLS) estimator provides physics-consistent localization and jointly estimates the receiver clock bias. The proposed hybrid design targets an accuracy-runtime trade-off rather than absolute supervised optimality. In a representative 2-D setting with 10 visible satellites, the proposed approach achieves sub-meter accuracy (0.395m RMSE) with low computational overhead, supporting practical deployment for resource-constrained LEO payloads.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的加权最小二乘低轨卫星星座波束定位方法
本文研究了一种轻量级深度强化学习辅助的加权框架，用于低轨星座中无需信道状态信息的多卫星定位。每个可见卫星每周期提供一个服务波束（一个导频响应）。离散动作深度Q网络直接从接收的导频测量值和几何特征中学习卫星权重，而增强的加权最小二乘估计器提供物理一致的定位并联合估计接收机时钟偏差。所提出的混合设计旨在权衡精度与运行时间，而非追求绝对监督最优性。在具有10颗可见卫星的代表性二维场景中，该方法以较低计算开销实现了亚米级精度（0.395米均方根误差），支持资源受限低轨载荷的实际部署。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need for efficient and accurate beam positioning in LEO satellite constellations, particularly for resource-constrained payloads. The method proposes a hybrid framework combining a Deep Q-Network (DQN) with a weighted least squares (WLS) estimator; the DQN learns to assign weights to satellites from pilot measurements and geometric features, while the WLS provides physics-consistent localization and clock bias estimation. Experimental results in a 2-D scenario with 10 visible satellites demonstrate that the approach achieves sub-meter accuracy (0.395m RMSE) with low computational overhead, effectively balancing accuracy and runtime for practical deployment.
本文旨在为资源受限的低地球轨道卫星星座提供高效、精确的波束定位方案。所提出的方法采用了一种混合框架，将深度Q网络与加权最小二乘估计器相结合：深度Q网络直接从接收的导频测量和几何特征中学习卫星权重，而加权最小二乘估计器则提供符合物理规律的定位并联合估计接收机时钟偏差。在具有10颗可见卫星的代表性二维场景中，实验结果表明该方法实现了亚米级精度（均方根误差0.395米）且计算开销低，有效权衡了精度与运行时间，支持实际部署。
Large Reward Models: Generalizable Online Robot Reward Generation with Vision-Language Models
Authors: Yanru Wu, Weiduo Yuan, Ang Qi, Vitor Guizilini, Jiageng Mao, Yue Wang
First: 2026-03-17T02:22:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T02:22:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has shown great potential in refining robotic manipulation policies, yet its efficacy remains strongly bottlenecked by the difficulty of designing generalizable reward functions. In this paper, we propose a framework for online policy refinement by adapting foundation VLMs into online reward generators. We develop a robust, scalable reward model based on a state-of-the-art VLM, trained on a large-scale, multi-source dataset encompassing real-world robot trajectories, human-object interactions, and diverse simulated environments. Unlike prior approaches that evaluate entire trajectories post-hoc, our method leverages the VLM to formulate a multifaceted reward signal comprising process, completion, and temporal contrastive rewards based on current visual observations. Initializing with a base policy trained via Imitation Learning (IL), we employ these VLM rewards to guide the model to correct sub-optimal behaviors in a closed-loop manner. We evaluate our framework on challenging long-horizon manipulation benchmarks requiring sequential execution and precise control. Crucially, our reward model operates in a purely zero-shot manner within these test environments. Experimental results demonstrate that our method significantly improves the success rate of the initial IL policy within just 30 RL iterations, demonstrating remarkable sample efficiency. This empirical evidence highlights that VLM-generated signals can provide reliable feedback to resolve execution errors, effectively eliminating the need for manual reward engineering and facilitating efficient online refinement for robot learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型奖励模型：基于视觉语言模型的可泛化在线机器人奖励生成
强化学习（RL）在优化机器人操作策略方面展现出巨大潜力，但其效果仍受限于设计可泛化奖励函数的困难。本文提出一种在线策略优化框架，将基础视觉语言模型（VLM）适配为在线奖励生成器。我们基于先进VLM构建了鲁棒、可扩展的奖励模型，该模型通过大规模多源数据集训练，涵盖真实世界机器人轨迹、人机交互及多样化仿真环境。与先前事后评估完整轨迹的方法不同，我们的方法利用VLM基于当前视觉观测构建多维奖励信号，包含过程奖励、完成奖励与时间对比奖励。通过从模仿学习（IL）训练的基础策略初始化，我们运用这些VLM奖励以闭环方式引导模型修正次优行为。我们在需要顺序执行与精确控制的复杂长程操作基准测试中评估本框架。关键的是，我们的奖励模型在这些测试环境中完全以零样本方式运行。实验结果表明，仅需30次RL迭代，我们的方法就能显著提升初始IL策略的成功率，展现出卓越的样本效率。这一实证证据表明，VLM生成的信号能提供可靠反馈以解决执行误差，有效避免了人工奖励工程的需求，为机器人学习实现了高效的在线优化。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the bottleneck of designing generalizable reward functions for robotic reinforcement learning (RL) by leveraging vision-language models (VLMs). The method involves adapting a foundation VLM into an online reward generator, trained on a large-scale, multi-source dataset, to produce multifaceted reward signals (process, completion, and temporal contrastive) from current visual observations for refining an imitation-learned base policy. The main experimental results on challenging long-horizon manipulation benchmarks show that the framework, operating in a zero-shot manner, significantly improves the initial policy's success rate within just 30 RL iterations, demonstrating high sample efficiency and eliminating the need for manual reward engineering.
本研究的动机是利用视觉语言模型（VLM）来克服机器人强化学习中设计通用奖励函数的瓶颈。方法是将基础VLM适配为在线奖励生成器，通过在包含真实机器人轨迹、人机交互和模拟环境的大规模多源数据集上进行训练，从当前视觉观察中生成多方面的奖励信号（过程、完成和时间对比奖励），用于优化模仿学习得到的基础策略。在需要顺序执行和精确控制的复杂长程操作基准上的主要实验结果表明，该框架以零样本方式运行，仅在30次强化学习迭代内就显著提升了初始策略的成功率，展现了出色的样本效率，并无需人工设计奖励函数。
ARISE: Agent Reasoning with Intrinsic Skill Evolution in Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yu Li, Rui Miao, Zhengling Qi, Tian Lan
First: 2026-03-17T02:03:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-17T02:03:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The dominant paradigm for improving mathematical reasoning in language models relies on Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards. Yet existing methods treat each problem instance in isolation without leveraging the reusable strategies that emerge and accumulate during training. To this end, we introduce ARISE (Agent Reasoning via Intrinsic Skill Evolution), a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework, in which a shared policy operates both to manage skills at high-level and to generate responses at low-level (denoted as a Skills Manager and a Worker, respectively). The Manager maintains a tiered skill library through a dedicated skill generation rollout that performs structured summarization of successful solution traces (after execution), while employing a policy-driven selection mechanism to retrieve relevant skills to condition future rollouts (before execution). A hierarchical reward design guides the co-evolution of reasoning ability and library quality. Experiments on two base models and seven benchmarks spanning both competition mathematics and Omni-MATH show that ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, with particularly notable gains on out-of-distribution tasks. Ablation studies confirm that each component contributes to the observed improvements and that library quality and reasoning performance improve in tandem throughout training. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARISE：分层强化学习中基于内在技能演化的智能体推理
当前提升语言模型数学推理能力的主流范式依赖于可验证奖励的强化学习，但现有方法孤立处理每个问题实例，未能充分利用训练过程中涌现和积累的可复用策略。为此，我们提出ARISE（基于内在技能演化的智能体推理），一种分层强化学习框架。该框架通过共享策略同时实现高层技能管理与低层响应生成（分别称为技能管理器与执行器）。管理器通过专用技能生成推演维护分层技能库：在执行后对成功解题轨迹进行结构化总结，并在执行前通过策略驱动的选择机制检索相关技能以指导后续推演。分层奖励设计引导推理能力与技能库质量的协同演化。在两个基础模型和涵盖竞赛数学与Omni-MATH的七个基准测试中，ARISE持续优于GRPO系列算法及记忆增强基线方法，在分布外任务上提升尤为显著。消融实验证实各组件均对性能提升有贡献，且技能库质量与推理能力在训练过程中同步增强。代码发布于\href{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}{https://github.com/Skylanding/ARISE}。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to move beyond treating each mathematical reasoning problem in isolation and to leverage reusable strategies that accumulate during training, this paper introduces ARISE, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework where a shared policy acts as both a high-level Skills Manager and a low-level Worker. The method involves the Manager maintaining a tiered skill library by summarizing successful solution traces and selecting relevant skills to condition future responses, guided by a hierarchical reward design that co-evolves reasoning ability and library quality. Experimental results on seven benchmarks with two base models show that ARISE consistently outperforms GRPO-family algorithms and memory-augmented baselines, especially on out-of-distribution tasks, with ablations confirming each component's contribution and the tandem improvement of library quality and reasoning performance.
本文的动机是超越对每个数学推理问题孤立处理的方式，以利用训练中积累的可重用策略，为此提出了ARISE这一分层强化学习框架，其中共享策略同时充当高层技能管理器和低层工作者。该方法通过管理器对成功解题轨迹进行结构化总结以维护分层技能库，并采用策略驱动的选择机制来检索相关技能以指导后续生成，同时通过分层奖励设计共同演化推理能力和库质量。在七个基准测试和两个基础模型上的实验结果表明，ARISE持续优于GRPO系列算法和记忆增强基线，尤其在分布外任务上提升显著，消融研究证实了各组件均贡献于性能提升，且库质量与推理性能在训练中协同提高。
